\begin{document}

\title{\textbf{Additional Online Appendix for \textquotedblleft Jackknife
Estimation of a Cluster-Sample IV Regression Model with Many Weak
Instruments"\thanks{%
Corresponding author: John C. Chao, Department of Economics, 7343 Preinkert
Drive, University of Maryland, chao@econ.umd.edu. Norman R. Swanson,
Department of Economics, 9500 Hamilton Street, Rutgers University,
nswanson@econ.rutgers.edu. Tiemen Woutersen, Department of Economics, 1130 E
Helen Street, University of Arizona, woutersen@arizona.edu. The authors
would like to thank the Editor, Xiaohong Chen, an Associate Editor, and an
anonymous referee for very helpful comments and suggestions. The authors
also owe special thanks to Jerry Hausman and Whitney Newey for many
discussions on the topic of this paper over a number of years. In addition,
thanks are owed to all of the particpants of the 2019 MIT Conference
Honoring Whitney Newey for comments on and advice given about the topic of
this paper. Finally, the authors wish to thank Miriam Arden for excellent
research assistance. Chao thanks the University of Maryland for research
support, and Woutersen's work was supported by an Eller College of
Management Research Grant.}}}
\author{John C. Chao, Norman R. Swanson, and Tiemen Woutersen}
\date{\textit{First Draft}: September 5, 2020 \ \ \textit{This Version}:
December 20, 2022}
\maketitle

\begin{abstract}
This online appendix is comprised of four sections. Section 1 contains
proofs for the key lemmas used to show the main theorems of the paper
\textquotedblleft Jackknife Estimation of a Cluster-Sample IV Regression
with Many Weak Instruments." More specifically, in section 1, we provide
proofs for Lemmas S2-1 to S2-18 which are stated without proof in the
Supplemental Appendix of the aforementioned paper. In section 2, we provide
a proof of Lemma 1 of the main paper. Section 3 of this online appendix
provides proofs of some additional lemmas which give further supporting
arguments for the proofs presented in section 1. Finally, section 4 gives
some additional Monte Carlo results which complement those reported in the
main paper.
\end{abstract}

\noindent \noindent \setcounter{page}{1}

\section*{Section 1: Proof of Lemmas S2-1 to S2-18}

In this section of the online appendix, we provide proof of Lemmas S2-1 to
S2-18, which have been stated without proof in the Appendix S2 of the
Supplemental Appendix to our paper.

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma S2-1: }Let $A=P^{\perp }-M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{%
\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }$. Then, under Assumptions 2-6,
the following statements hold as $K_{2,n}$, $n\rightarrow \infty $.

\begin{enumerate}
\item[(a)] 
\begin{equation*}
\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left(
i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2}=O_{a.s.}\left( K_{2,n}\right) \text{.}
\end{equation*}

\item[(b)] 
\begin{equation*}
\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left(
i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{4}=O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{3}}{n^{2}}\right) \text{.}
\end{equation*}

\item[(c)] 
\begin{equation*}
\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right)  \\ \left( k,\upsilon \right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}=O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right)
\end{equation*}

\item[(d)] 
\begin{equation*}
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left( \dsum\nolimits_{\left(
j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\right)
=O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{n}\right)
\end{equation*}

\item[(e)] 
\begin{eqnarray*}
\dsum\limits_{i_{1},i_{2}=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ j=1  \\ j\neq
i_{1},i_{2}}}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\dsum%
\limits_{t_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\dsum\limits_{s_{1},s_{2}=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left(
i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left( j,s_{1}\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i_{2},t_{2}\right)
,\left( j,s_{2}\right) }^{2} &=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right) 
\text{,} \\
\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ j_{1}=1  \\ j_{1}\neq i}}%
^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ j_{2}=1  \\ j_{2}\neq i}}^{n}\dsum%
\limits_{t_{1},t_{2}=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s_{1}=1}^{T_{j_{1}}}\dsum%
\limits_{s_{2}=1}^{T_{j_{2}}}A_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) ,\left(
j_{1},s_{1}\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i,t_{2}\right) ,\left( j_{2},s_{2}\right)
}^{2} &=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right) \text{.}
\end{eqnarray*}

\item[(f)] 
\begin{equation*}
\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum%
\limits_{s=1}^{T_{i}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,s\right)
}^{2}=O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right) \text{.}
\end{equation*}

\item[(g)] 
\begin{equation*}
\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ s_{1},t_{1}=1  \\ s_{1}\neq
t_{1}}}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ s_{2},t_{2}=1  \\ s_{2}\neq t_{2}}}%
^{T_{i}}A_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) ,\left( i,s_{1}\right) }^{2}A_{\left(
i,t_{2}\right) ,\left( i,s_{2}\right) }^{2}=O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{4}%
}{n^{3}}\right) \text{.}
\end{equation*}
\end{enumerate}

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma S2-1:}

To show part (a), note first that, by Lemma OA-1 given in section 3 of this
online appendix, we have%
\begin{equation*}
tr\left\{ D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}^{2}\right\} =O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{%
K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right) ,
\end{equation*}%
\textbf{\ }where $D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}=diag\left( \widehat{\vartheta }%
_{1},...,\widehat{\vartheta }_{m_{n}}\right) $. Now, by straightforward
calculations and by making use of the inequality 
\begin{equation}
\left\vert \dsum\nolimits_{i=1}^{G}a_{i}\right\vert ^{r}\leq
G^{r-1}\dsum\nolimits_{i=1}^{G}\left\vert a_{i}\right\vert ^{r},
\label{cr type ineq}
\end{equation}
we get%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left(
i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2} &=&\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}\left(
P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{\perp }-e_{\left( i,t\right)
}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,s\right) }\right) ^{2} \\
&\leq &2\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{\perp }\right) ^{2}+2\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right)
\neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}\left( e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}e_{\left( j,s\right) }\right) ^{2} \\
&\leq &2\left[ K_{2,n}+\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}e_{\left(
i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }%
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}e_{\left( i,t\right) }\right] \\
&\leq &2\left[ K_{2,n}+tr\left\{ M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta 
}}^{2}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\right\} \right] =2\left[ K_{2,n}+tr\left\{ D_{%
\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}\right\} %
\right] \\
&\leq &2\left[ K_{2,n}+tr\left\{ D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}^{2}\right\} \right]
=O_{a.s.}\left( K_{2,n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right)
=O_{a.s.}\left( K_{2,n}\right) \text{.}
\end{eqnarray*}

Next, to show part (b), note that, by applying the inequality in expression (%
\ref{cr type ineq}) as well as the CS inequality and using the fact that $%
\lambda _{\max }\left( M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\right) =1$, we obtain%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{4} \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{\perp }-e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}e_{\left( j,s\right) }\right) ^{4} \\
&\leq &2^{3}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1 
\\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}\left\{ \left(
P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{\perp }\right) ^{4}+\left(
e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }%
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,s\right) }\right) ^{4}\right\} \\
&\leq &8\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left(
P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{\perp }\right) ^{4} \\
&&+\text{\ }8\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left\{ \left( e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}^{2}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left(
i,t\right) }\right) \left( e_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,s\right) }\right) \right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \times e_{\left(
i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }%
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,s\right) }e_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}e_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\} \\
&\leq &8\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left(
P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{\perp }\right) ^{4}+8\max_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert \widehat{\vartheta }_{\left(
i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{%
\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,t\right) } \\
&\leq &8\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp }\right) ^{2}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{\perp }\right) ^{2} \\
&&+8\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert \widehat{%
\vartheta }_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\right) tr\left\{ D_{%
\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}e_{\left( i,t\right) }e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}\right\} \\
&\leq &8\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp }\right) ^{2}K_{2,n}+8\left( \max_{1\leq \left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert \widehat{\vartheta }_{\left( i,t\right)
}\right\vert ^{2}\right) tr\left\{ D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}\right\} \\
&\leq &8\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp }\right) ^{2}K_{2,n}+8\left( \max_{1\leq \left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert \widehat{\vartheta }_{\left( i,t\right)
}\right\vert ^{2}\right) tr\left\{ D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}^{2}\right\} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{3}}{n^{2}}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{%
K_{2,n}^{4}}{n^{3}}\right) \text{ \ (by parts (a) and (b) of Lemma OA-1)} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{3}}{n^{2}}\right) \text{.}
\end{eqnarray*}

To show part (c), note that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2} \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ %
\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq
\left( j,s\right)  \\ \left( k,\upsilon \right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{\perp }-e_{\left(
i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }%
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,s\right) }\right) ^{2}\left( P_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{\perp }-e_{\left( j,s\right)
}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\right) ^{2} \\
&\leq &\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left(
P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{\perp }-e_{\left( i,t\right)
}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,s\right) }\right) ^{2} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{\perp }-e_{\left( j,s\right)
}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\right) ^{2} \\
&\leq &4\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left[
\left( P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{\perp }\right) ^{2}+\left(
e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }%
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,s\right) }\right) ^{2}\right] \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left[ \left(
P_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{\perp }\right)
^{2}+\left( e_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{%
\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}\right) ^{2}\right] \text{ } \\
&&\left( \text{by the inequality in expression (\ref{cr type ineq})}\right)
\\
&=&4\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left\{ 
\left[ \left( P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{\perp }\right)
^{2}+\left( e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{%
\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,s\right) }\right) ^{2}%
\right] \right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \times \left[ P_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{\perp }+e_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{%
\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,s\right) }\right]
\right\} \\
&\leq &4\left( \max_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{\perp }\right) \dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left[ \left( P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{\perp }\right) ^{2}+\left( e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left(
j,s\right) }\right) ^{2}\right] \\
&&+4\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left[
\left( P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{\perp }\right) ^{2}+\left(
e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }%
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,s\right) }\right) ^{2}\right] e_{\left(
j,s\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }%
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}e_{\left( j,s\right) } \\
&\leq &4\left( \max_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{\perp }\right) \dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left[ P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp
}+e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{%
\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,t\right) }\right] \\
&&+4\left( \max_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert \widehat{%
\vartheta }_{\left( j,s\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\right) \dsum\limits_{\left(
i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left[ P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right)
}^{\perp }+e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{%
\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,t\right) }\right] \\
&\leq &4\left[ \left( \max_{\left( j,s\right) \in \Lambda _{2}}P_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{\perp }\right) +\left( \max_{1\leq \left(
j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert \widehat{\vartheta }_{\left( j,s\right)
}\right\vert ^{2}\right) \right] \left[ K_{2,n}+tr\left\{ D_{\widehat{%
\vartheta }}^{2}\right\} \right] \\
&=&\left[ O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{%
K_{2,n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) \right] \left[ O_{a.s.}\left( K_{2,n}\right)
+O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right) \right] \text{ (using Lemma
OA-1)} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right) \text{. }
\end{eqnarray*}%
\ 

Finally, to show part (d), note that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2} &=&\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left(
P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{\perp }-e_{\left( i,t\right)
}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,s\right) }\right) ^{2} \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{\perp }\right) ^{2}-2e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}e_{\left( j,s\right) }e_{\left(
j,s\right) }^{\prime }P^{\perp }e_{\left( i,t\right) } \\
&&+e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{%
\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}e_{\left( j,s\right) }e_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left(
i,t\right) } \\
&=&P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp }+e_{\left( i,t\right)
}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left(
i,t\right) } \\
&\leq &P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp }+e_{\left(
i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }%
}^{2}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,t\right) } \\
&\leq &P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp }+e_{\left(
i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,t\right) }\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert \widehat{\vartheta }%
_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\right) \text{ } \\
&\leq &P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp }+\left( \max_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert \widehat{\vartheta }_{\left(
i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\right) \text{ (since }e_{\left( i,t\right)
}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,t\right) }\leq 1\text{)}
\end{eqnarray*}%
It follows that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left( \dsum\limits_{\left(
j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\right)
&\leq &\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp }\right) +\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right)
\leq m_{n}}\left\vert \widehat{\vartheta }_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert
^{2}\right) \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}%
}{n^{2}}\right) \text{ } \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{n}\right) \text{. }
\end{eqnarray*}

To show part (e), we apply the inequality (\ref{cr type ineq}), Assumption
6, and parts (a) and (b) of Lemma OA-1 to obtain%
\begin{eqnarray}
&&\dsum\limits_{i_{1},i_{2}=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ j=1  \\ j\neq
i_{1},i_{2}}}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\dsum%
\limits_{t_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\dsum\limits_{s_{1},s_{2}=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left(
i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left( j,s_{1}\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i_{2},t_{2}\right)
,\left( j,s_{2}\right) }^{2}  \notag \\
&\leq
&\dsum\limits_{i_{1}=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{j=1}^{n}\dsum%
\limits_{t_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\dsum\limits_{s_{1}=1}^{T_{j}}\left( P_{\left(
i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left( j,s_{1}\right) }^{\perp }-e_{\left(
i_{1},t_{1}\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }%
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,s_{1}\right) }\right) ^{2}  \notag \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times
\dsum\limits_{i_{2}=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\dsum%
\limits_{s_{2}=1}^{T_{j}}\left( P_{\left( i_{2},t_{2}\right) ,\left(
j,s_{2}\right) }^{\perp }-e_{\left( i_{2},t_{2}\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left(
j,s_{2}\right) }\right) ^{2}  \notag \\
&\leq
&4\dsum\limits_{i_{1}=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{j=1}^{n}\dsum%
\limits_{t_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\dsum\limits_{s_{1}=1}^{T_{j}}\left[ \left(
P_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left( j,s_{1}\right) }^{\perp }\right)
^{2}+\left( e_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{%
\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,s_{1}\right) }\right)
^{2}\right]  \notag \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times
\dsum\limits_{s_{2}=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{i_{2}=1}^{n}\dsum%
\limits_{t_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\left[ \left( P_{\left( i_{2},t_{2}\right)
,\left( j,s_{2}\right) }^{\perp }\right) ^{2}+\left( e_{\left(
i_{2},t_{2}\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }%
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,s_{2}\right) }\right) ^{2}\right]  \notag
\\
&=&4\dsum\limits_{i_{1}=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{j=1}^{n}\dsum%
\limits_{t_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\dsum\limits_{s_{1}=1}^{T_{j}}\left[ \left(
P_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left( j,s_{1}\right) }^{\perp }\right)
^{2}+\left( e_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{%
\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,s_{1}\right) }\right)
^{2}\right]  \notag \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{s_{2}=1}^{T_{j}}\left[ P_{\left( j,s_{2}\right)
,\left( j,s_{2}\right) }^{\perp }+e_{\left( j,s_{2}\right) }^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{%
\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,s_{2}\right) }\right]
\notag \\
&\leq &4\overline{T}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp }\right)
\dsum\limits_{i_{1}=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{j=1}^{n}\dsum%
\limits_{t_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\dsum\limits_{s_{1}=1}^{T_{j}}\left[ \left(
P_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left( j,s_{1}\right) }^{\perp }\right)
^{2}+\left( e_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{%
\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,s_{1}\right) }\right)
^{2}\right]  \notag \\
&&+4\overline{T}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert 
\widehat{\vartheta }_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\right)
\dsum\limits_{i_{1}=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{j=1}^{n}\dsum%
\limits_{t_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\dsum\limits_{s_{1}=1}^{T_{j}}\left[ \left(
P_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left( j,s_{1}\right) }^{\perp }\right)
^{2}+\left( e_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{%
\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,s_{1}\right) }\right)
^{2}\right]  \notag \\
&\leq &4\overline{T}\left[ \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp }\right) +\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert \widehat{\vartheta }%
_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\right) \right] \left[
K_{2,n}+tr\left\{ D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}^{2}\right\} \right]  \notag \\
&=&\left[ O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{%
K_{2,n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) \right] \left[ O_{a.s.}\left( K_{2,n}\right)
+O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right) \right] \text{ (using Lemma
OA-1)}  \notag \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right)  \label{part e 1st result}
\end{eqnarray}%
Next, note that, since $A$ is a symmetric matrix, we have $A_{\left(
i,t_{1}\right) ,\left( j_{1},s_{1}\right) }^{2}=A_{\left( j_{1},s_{1}\right)
,\left( i,t_{1}\right) }^{2}$ and $A_{\left( i,t_{2}\right) ,\left(
j_{2},s_{2}\right) }^{2}=A_{\left( j_{2},s_{2}\right) ,\left( i,t_{2}\right)
}^{2}$. It follows, by switching the indices $\left( i,t_{1}\right)
\rightarrow \left( j,s_{1}\right) $, $\left( i,t_{2}\right) \rightarrow
\left( j,s_{2}\right) $, $\left( j_{1},s_{1}\right) \rightarrow \left(
i_{1},t_{1}\right) $, and $\left( j_{2},s_{2}\right) \rightarrow \left(
i_{2},t_{2}\right) $, and applying the result given in expression (\ref{part
e 1st result}) above, we have 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ j_{1}=1  \\ j_{1}\neq i}}%
^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ j_{2}=1  \\ j_{2}\neq i}}^{n}\dsum%
\limits_{t_{1},t_{2}=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s_{1}=1}^{T_{j_{1}}}\dsum%
\limits_{s_{2}=1}^{T_{j_{2}}}A_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) ,\left(
j_{1},s_{1}\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i,t_{2}\right) ,\left( j_{2},s_{2}\right)
}^{2} \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ j_{1}=1  \\ j_{1}\neq i}}%
^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ j_{2}=1  \\ j_{2}\neq i}}^{n}\dsum%
\limits_{t_{1},t_{2}=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s_{1}=1}^{T_{j_{1}}}\dsum%
\limits_{s_{2}=1}^{T_{j_{2}}}A_{\left( j_{1},s_{1}\right) ,\left(
i,t_{1}\right) }^{2}A_{\left( j_{2},s_{2}\right) ,\left( i,t_{2}\right) }^{2}
\\
&=&\dsum\limits_{j=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i_{1}=1  \\ i_{1}\neq j}}%
^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i_{2}=1  \\ i_{2}\neq j}}^{n}\dsum%
\limits_{s_{1},s_{2}=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{t_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\dsum%
\limits_{t_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}A_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left(
j,s_{1}\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i_{2},t_{2}\right) ,\left( j,s_{2}\right) }^{2}
\\
&=&\dsum\limits_{i_{1},i_{2}=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ j=1  \\ j\neq
i_{1},i_{2}}}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\dsum%
\limits_{t_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\dsum\limits_{s_{1},s_{2}=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left(
i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left( j,s_{1}\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i_{2},t_{2}\right)
,\left( j,s_{2}\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right) \text{.}
\end{eqnarray*}

Turning our attention to part (f), note that, by applying the inequality (%
\ref{cr type ineq}) and making use of Assumption 6(ii), we have 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum%
\limits_{s=1}^{T_{i}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,s\right) }^{2} \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum%
\limits_{s=1}^{T_{i}}\left( P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,s\right) }^{\perp
}-e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{%
\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,s\right) }\right) ^{2} \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum%
\limits_{s=1}^{T_{i}}\left\{ \left( P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,s\right)
}^{\perp }\right) ^{2}-2P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,s\right) }^{\perp
}e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta 
}}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,s\right) }\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. +\left[ e_{\left(
i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }%
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,s\right) }\right] ^{2}\right\} \\
&\leq
&2\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{i}}%
\left\{ \left( P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,s\right) }^{\perp }\right)
^{2}+\left[ e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{%
\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,s\right) }\right]
^{2}\right\} \\
&\leq
&2\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{i}}%
\left\{ P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp }P_{\left(
i,s\right) ,\left( i,s\right) }^{\perp }+\left( e_{\left( i,t\right)
}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}^{2}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,t\right) }\right) \left( e_{\left( i,s\right)
}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,s\right) }\right) \right\} \\
&=&2\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}P_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp }\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{i}}P_{\left( i,s\right)
,\left( i,s\right) }^{\perp } \\
&&+2\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\left( e_{\left(
i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }%
}^{2}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,t\right) }\right)
\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{i}}e_{\left( i,s\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,s\right) } \\
&\leq &2\overline{T}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp }\right)
\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,t\right) }^{\perp }+2\overline{T}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}\left\vert \widehat{\vartheta }_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert
^{2}\right) \dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left( e_{\left(
i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,t\right) }\right) \\
&\leq &2\overline{T}\left[ \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp }\right)
K_{2,n}+\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert \widehat{%
\vartheta }_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\right) \left(
m_{n}-K_{n}-n\right) \right] \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{%
K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right) \text{ \ (by part (b) of Lemma OA-1)} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right) \text{. }
\end{eqnarray*}

To show part (g), note that, by making use of Assumption 6(ii), we have%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ s_{1},t_{1}=1  \\ s_{1}\neq
t_{1}}}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ s_{2},t_{2}=1  \\ s_{2}\neq t_{2}}}%
^{T_{i}}A_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) ,\left( i,s_{1}\right) }^{2}A_{\left(
i,t_{2}\right) ,\left( i,s_{2}\right) }^{2} \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ s_{1},t_{1}=1  \\ %
s_{1}\neq t_{1}}}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ s_{2},t_{2}=1  \\ %
s_{2}\neq t_{2}}}^{T_{i}}\left\{ \left( P_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) ,\left(
i,s_{1}\right) }^{\perp }-e_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left(
i,s_{1}\right) }\right) ^{2}\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \text{\ }\times
\left( P_{\left( i,t_{2}\right) ,\left( i,s_{2}\right) }^{\perp }-e_{\left(
i,t_{2}\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }%
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,s_{2}\right) }\right) ^{2}\right\} \\
&\leq &4\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ s_{1},t_{1}=1  \\ %
s_{1}\neq t_{1}}}^{T_{i}}\left[ \left( P_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) ,\left(
i,s_{1}\right) }^{\perp }\right) ^{2}+\left( e_{\left( i,t_{1}\right)
}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,s_{1}\right) }\right) ^{2}\right] \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{\substack{ s_{2},t_{2}=1  \\ s_{2}\neq t_{2}}}^{T_{i}}%
\left[ \left( P_{\left( i,t_{2}\right) ,\left( i,s_{2}\right) }^{\perp
}\right) ^{2}+\left( e_{\left( i,t_{2}\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left(
i,s_{2}\right) }\right) ^{2}\right] \text{ \ (using inequality (\ref{cr type
ineq}))} \\
&\leq &4\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{1}=1}^{T_{i}}\left[ \left(
P_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) ,\left( i,t_{1}\right) }^{\perp }\right)
\dsum\limits_{s_{1}=1}^{T_{i}}\left( P_{\left( i,s_{1}\right) ,\left(
i,s_{1}\right) }^{\perp }\right) \right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }+\left( e_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) }^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}^{2}M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}e_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) }\right) \dsum\limits_{s_{1}=1}^{T_{i}}\left(
e_{\left( i,s_{1}\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left(
i,s_{1}\right) }\right) \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{\substack{ s_{2},t_{2}=1  \\ s_{2}\neq t_{2}}}^{T_{i}}%
\left[ \left( P_{\left( i,t_{2}\right) ,\left( i,t_{2}\right) }^{\perp
}\right) \left( P_{\left( i,s_{1}\right) ,\left( i,s_{1}\right) }^{\perp
}\right) +\left( e_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}^{2}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,t_{1}\right)
}\right) \left( e_{\left( i,s_{1}\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}e_{\left( i,s_{1}\right) }\right) \right] \\
&\leq &4\overline{T}^{3}\left[ \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp }\right) ^{2}+\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert \widehat{\vartheta }%
_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\right) \right] \\
&&\times \left[ \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp }\right) \dsum\limits_{\left(
i,t_{1}\right) =1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) ,\left( i,t_{1}\right)
}^{\perp }+\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert 
\widehat{\vartheta }_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\right)
\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) =1}^{m_{n}}e_{\left( i,t_{1}\right)
}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) }\right] \\
&\leq &4\overline{T}^{3}\left[ \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp }\right) ^{2}+\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert \widehat{\vartheta }%
_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\right) \right] \\
&&\times \left[ \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp }\right) K_{2,n}+\left( \max_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert \widehat{\vartheta }_{\left(
i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\right) \left( m_{n}-K_{n}-n\right) \right] \\
&=&\left[ O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( 
\frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) \right] \left[ O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{%
K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right) \right] 
\text{ (using Lemma OA-1(b))} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{4}}{n^{3}}\right) \text{. }\square
\end{eqnarray*}

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma S2-2: }Let Assumptions 1-6 be satisfied. Then, the
following statements are true: (a) $D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }XD_{\mu }^{-1}=O_{p}\left( n\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right)
^{-2}\right) $; (b) $D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }AXD_{\mu
}^{-1}=H_{n}+o_{p}\left( 1\right) $, where $H_{n}=\Upsilon ^{\prime
}Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }Z_{2}\Upsilon /n=O_{p}\left(
1\right) $.

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma S2-2:}

To show part (a), note first that $D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }XD_{\mu }^{-1}$

\noindent $\leq 2\left[ \Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }Z_{2}\Upsilon /n+D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }UD_{\mu }^{-1}\right] $, where we take $A\leq B$ for two
square matrices $A$ and $B$ to mean that $A-B$ is negative semi-definite,
or, alternatively, $B-A$ is positive semidefinite. Now, for $a,b\in \mathbb{R%
}^{d}$ such that $\left\Vert a\right\Vert _{2}=\left\Vert b\right\Vert
_{2}=1 $, we can apply the CS inequality and Assumption 3(iii) to obtain $%
\left\vert a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }Z_{2}\Upsilon b/n\right\vert \leq \sqrt{a^{\prime }\Upsilon
^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }Z_{2}\Upsilon a/n}\sqrt{%
b^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}Z_{2}\Upsilon b/n}\leq \sqrt{a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime
}Z_{2}\Upsilon a/n}\sqrt{b^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime
}Z_{2}\Upsilon b/n}=O_{a.s.}\left( 1\right) $. Since the above argument
holds for all $a$, $b\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$ such that $\left\Vert a\right\Vert
_{2}=\left\Vert b\right\Vert _{2}=1$, we further deduce that $\Upsilon
^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }Z_{2}\Upsilon
/n=O_{p}\left( 1\right) $.

Next, note that, by the CS inequality, $\left\vert a^{\prime }D_{\mu
}^{-1}U^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }UD_{\mu }^{-1}b\right\vert $

\noindent $\leq \sqrt{a^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }UD_{\mu }^{-1}a}\sqrt{b^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }UD_{\mu }^{-1}b}$. Now, by Assumptions 2(i),
3(ii), and 6(ii), 
\begin{eqnarray*}
E\left[ a^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }UD_{\mu
}^{-1}a|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] &\leq &a^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}E\left[
U^{\prime }U|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] D_{\mu }^{-1}a \\
&\leq &\frac{\overline{T}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E%
\left[ \left\Vert U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) n}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}%
=O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{n}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}\right) \text{,}
\end{eqnarray*}%
where $\overline{T}=\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}T_{i}$. Hence,
by Theorem 16.1 of Billingsley (1995), there exists a constant $\overline{C}%
<\infty $ such that for all $n$ sufficiently large $E\left[ \left( \left(
\mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}/n\right) a^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }UD_{\mu }^{-1}a\right] =E_{Z}\left( \left( \left(
\mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}/n\right) E\left[ \frac{a^{\prime }U^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }Ua}{n}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \leq 
\overline{C}$. It follows from the Markov's inequality that

\noindent $a^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}UD_{\mu }^{-1}a=O_{p}\left( n\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{-2}\right) $.
In the same way, we also have

\noindent $b^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}UD_{\mu }^{-1}b=O_{p}\left( n/\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}\right) $,
so that $\left\vert a^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }UD_{\mu }^{-1}b\right\vert \leq $

\noindent $\sqrt{a^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}UD_{\mu }^{-1}a}\sqrt{b^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }UD_{\mu }^{-1}b}=O_{p}\left( n\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right)
^{-2}\right) $. Since this result holds for all $a$, $b\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$
such that $\left\Vert a\right\Vert _{2}=\left\Vert b\right\Vert _{2}=1$, we
further deduce that $D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}UD_{\mu }^{-1}=O_{p}\left( n\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{-2}\right) $.
Putting these results together, it follows that $D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }XD_{\mu }^{-1}=O_{p}\left( 1\right) +O_{p}\left(
n\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{-2}\right) =O_{p}\left( n\left( \mu
_{n}^{\min }\right) ^{-2}\right) $, as required to show part (a).

To show part (b), note that, by applying parts (a)-(c) of Lemma OA-12, we
obtain%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }AXD_{\mu }^{-1} \\
&=&D_{\mu }^{-1}\left( \frac{D_{\kappa }\Theta ^{\prime }Z_{1}^{\prime }}{%
\sqrt{n}}+\frac{D_{\mu }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }}{\sqrt{n}}+\Xi
^{\prime }Q^{\prime }+U^{\prime }\right) A\left( \frac{Z_{1}\Theta D_{\kappa
}}{\sqrt{n}}+\frac{Z_{2}\Upsilon D_{\mu }}{\sqrt{n}}+Q\Xi +U\right) D_{\mu
}^{-1} \\
&=&D_{\mu }^{-1}\left( \frac{D_{\mu }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }}{%
\sqrt{n}}+U\right) ^{\prime }A\left( \frac{Z_{2}\Upsilon D_{\mu }}{\sqrt{n}}%
+U\right) D_{\mu }^{-1}\text{ }\left( \text{since }AZ_{1}=0\text{ and }%
AQ=0\right) \\
&=&\frac{D_{\mu }^{-1}D_{\mu }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime
}AZ_{2}\Upsilon D_{\mu }D_{\mu }^{-1}}{n}+D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }AUD_{\mu
}^{-1}+\frac{D_{\mu }^{-1}D_{\mu }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }AUD_{\mu
}^{-1}}{\sqrt{n}} \\
&&+\frac{D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }AZ_{2}\Upsilon D_{\mu }D_{\mu }^{-1}}{\sqrt{%
n}} \\
&=&\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }AZ_{2}\Upsilon }{n}+D_{\mu
}^{-1}U^{\prime }AUD_{\mu }^{-1}+\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime
}AUD_{\mu }^{-1}}{\sqrt{n}}+\frac{D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }AZ_{2}\Upsilon }{%
\sqrt{n}} \\
&=&\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}Z_{2}\Upsilon }{n}+o_{p}\left( 1\right) .\text{ \textit{\ }}
\end{eqnarray*}%
Moreover, $\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}Z_{2}\Upsilon /n=O_{p}\left( 1\right) $, as shown in the proof of part (a)
above. This shows part (b). $\square $

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma S2-3: }Let $\underline{U}=U-\varepsilon \rho
^{\prime }$ and $\underline{U}_{\left( i,t\right) }=U_{\left( i,t\right)
}-\rho \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }$ and let $VC\left( X|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) $ denote the conditional covariance matrix of the random
vector $X$ given $\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}$. Under Assumptions 1-2, 5-6, and 8;
there exists positive constants $0<\underline{C}\leq \overline{C}<\infty $
such that the following statements are true.

\noindent (a) $\lambda _{\max }\left[ VC\left( \Upsilon ^{\prime
}Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon /\sqrt{n}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) \right] \leq \overline{C}$ \ \ $a.s.$ and $\lambda _{\min }%
\left[ VC\left( \Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\varepsilon /\sqrt{n}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \right] \geq \underline{C}$
\ $a.s.$ for all $n$ sufficiently large.

\noindent (b) $VC\left( \underline{U}^{\prime }A\varepsilon /\sqrt{K_{2,n}}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \geq \underline{C}I_{d}>\underset{d\times d}{0}$
\ $a.s.$, for all $n$ sufficiently large.

\noindent (c) $\lambda _{\max }\left( VC\left[ \underline{U}^{\prime
}A\varepsilon /\sqrt{K_{2,n}}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \leq 
\overline{C}$ \ $a.s.$, $\lambda _{\max }\left( VC\left[ \underline{U}%
^{\prime }A\varepsilon /\sqrt{K_{2,n}}\right] \right) \leq \overline{C}$,

\noindent $\lambda _{\max }\left( VC\left[ U^{\prime }A\varepsilon /\sqrt{%
K_{2,n}}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \leq \overline{C}$ \ $a.s.$, and 
$\lambda _{\max }\left( VC\left[ U^{\prime }A\varepsilon /\sqrt{K_{2,n}}%
\right] \right) \leq \overline{C}$, for all $n$ sufficiently large.

\noindent (d) For any $a\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$ with $\left\Vert a\right\Vert
_{2}=1$ and for all $n$ sufficiently large, $\lambda _{\min }\left( \Sigma
_{n}\right) \geq \underline{C}>0$ $a.s.$ and $a^{\prime }\Sigma
_{n}^{-1}a\leq \overline{C}<\infty $ \ $a.s.$, where $\Sigma _{n}=VC\left( 
\mathcal{Y}_{n}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) =\Sigma _{1,n}+\Sigma _{2,n}$, as
defined in section 4 of the main paper, and where $\mathcal{Y}_{n}=\Upsilon
^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon /\sqrt{n}%
+D_{\mu }^{-1}\underline{U}^{\prime }A\varepsilon $.

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma S2-3:}

For part (a), note that, by Assumptions 1, 2, and 3(iii); there exists a
pair of constants $0<\underline{C}$ $\leq \overline{C}<\infty $ such that,
for any $b\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$ such that $\left\Vert b\right\Vert =1$ and for
all $n$ sufficiently large, $b^{\prime }VC\left( \Upsilon ^{\prime
}Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon /\sqrt{n}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) b=b^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }E\left[ \varepsilon \varepsilon ^{\prime }|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }Z_{2}\Upsilon b/n$

\noindent $\leq \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[
\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right)
\lambda _{\max }\left( \Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }Z_{2}\Upsilon
/n\right) \leq \overline{C}$ $a.s.$ and $b^{\prime }VC\left( \Upsilon
^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon /\sqrt{n}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) b\geq \left( \min_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \right) b^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }Z_{2}\Upsilon b/n\geq \underline{C}$ $a.s.$ Since the above
bounds hold for any $b\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$ such that $\left\Vert b\right\Vert
_{2}=1$, it follows that, almost surely, $\lambda _{\max }\left[ VC\left(
\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon /%
\sqrt{n}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \right] =\max_{\left\Vert b\right\Vert
=1}b^{\prime }VC\left( \Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon /\sqrt{n}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) b\leq 
\overline{C}<\infty $ and $\lambda _{\min }\left[ VC\left( \Upsilon ^{\prime
}Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon /\sqrt{n}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) \right] $

\noindent $=\min_{\left\Vert b\right\Vert =1}b^{\prime }VC\left( \Upsilon
^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon /\sqrt{n}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) b\geq \underline{C}>0$ for all $n$ sufficiently
large, which establishes the required result.

To show part (b), let $a\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$ such that $\left\Vert
a\right\Vert _{2}=1$, and we define $\underline{U}_{\left( i,t\right)
}=U_{\left( i,t\right) }-\rho \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }$, $%
\underline{u}_{a,\left( i,t\right) }=a^{\prime }\underline{U}_{\left(
i,t\right) }$, $\sigma _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}=E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] $, $\widetilde{\omega }%
_{a,\left( i,t\right) }^{2}=E\left[ \underline{u}_{a,\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] $, $\widetilde{\psi }_{a,\left( i,t\right) }=E%
\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }\underline{u}_{a,\left( i,t\right) }|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] $, and $\varrho _{a,\left( i,t\right) }=%
\widetilde{\psi }_{a,\left( i,t\right) }/\left( \sigma _{\left( i,t\right) }%
\widetilde{\omega }_{a,\left( i,t\right) }\right) $; for $\left( i,t\right)
=1,..,m_{n}$, where we have suppressed the dependence of $\sigma _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}$, $\widetilde{\omega }_{a,\left( i,t\right) }^{2}$, $%
\widetilde{\psi }_{a,\left( i,t\right) }$, and $\varrho _{a,\left(
i,t\right) }$ on $\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}=\sigma \left( Z\right) $ for
notational convenience. Note also that we can write $a^{\prime }VC\left( 
\underline{U}^{\prime }A\varepsilon /\sqrt{K_{2,n}}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) a=$

\noindent $K_{2,n}^{-1}\dsum\nolimits_{\left( i,t\right)
=2}^{m_{n}}\dsum\nolimits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{\left( i,t\right)
-1}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}E\left[ \left( \varepsilon
_{\left( j,s\right) }\underline{u}_{a,\left( i,t\right) }+\varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }\underline{u}_{a,\left( j,s\right) }\right) ^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] $, since, by construction, $A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( i,t\right) }=0$ for $\left( i,t\right) =1,...,m_{n}$. Moreover,
define $\delta _{a,\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }=\left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
\sigma _{\left( j,s\right) }\widetilde{\omega }_{a,\left( i,t\right) } & 
\sigma _{\left( i,t\right) }\widetilde{\omega }_{a,\left( j,s\right) }%
\end{array}%
\right) ^{\prime }$ and 
\begin{equation*}
\Delta _{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{a}=\left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
1 & \varrho _{a,\left( i,t\right) }\varrho _{a,\left( j,s\right) } \\ 
\varrho _{a,\left( i,t\right) }\varrho _{a,\left( j,s\right) } & 1%
\end{array}%
\right)
\end{equation*}%
and note that, given that $\left( j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) $, we have $E%
\left[ \left( \varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) }\underline{u}_{a,\left(
i,t\right) }+\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }\underline{u}_{a,\left(
j,s\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] $

\noindent $=\delta _{a,\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime
}\Delta _{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{a}\delta _{a,\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }$. Now, by the quadratic formula, the
smallest eigenvalue of $\Delta _{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{a}$
is given by $\lambda _{\min }\left( \Delta _{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{a}\right) =1-\left\vert \varrho _{a,\left( i,t\right)
}\right\vert \left\vert \varrho _{a,\left( j,s\right) }\right\vert $. In
addition, write%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\widetilde{\Omega }_{\left( i,t\right) } &=&\left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] & E 
\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }\underline{U}_{\left( i,t\right)
}^{\prime }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\ 
E\left[ \underline{U}_{\left( i,t\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] & E\left[ \underline{U}_{\left( i,t\right) }%
\underline{U}_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]%
\end{array}%
\right) \\
&=&\left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
1 & 0 \\ 
-\rho & I_{d}%
\end{array}%
\right) \left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] & E 
\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }U_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\ 
E\left[ U_{\left( i,t\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] & E\left[ U_{\left( i,t\right) }U_{\left( i,t\right)
}^{\prime }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]%
\end{array}%
\right) \left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
1 & -\rho ^{\prime } \\ 
0 & I_{d}%
\end{array}%
\right) \\
&=&L_{\rho }\Omega _{\left( i,t\right) }L_{\rho }^{\prime }\text{, where }%
L_{\rho }\text{ }\mathbb{=}\left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
1 & 0 \\ 
-\rho & I_{d}%
\end{array}%
\right) \text{. }
\end{eqnarray*}%
Note that $L_{\rho }$ is nonsingular, so that $L_{\rho }L_{\rho }^{\prime }$
is positive definite. Hence, by Assumption 2 part (ii) and by the fact that $%
L_{\rho }L_{\rho }^{\prime }$ is a fixed, finite-dimensional positive
definite matrix, there exists some constant $C_{1}>1$ such that 
\begin{equation}
\min_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\lambda _{\min }\left( \widetilde{%
\Omega }_{\left( i,t\right) }\right) \geq \min_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}\lambda _{\min }\left( \Omega _{\left( i,t\right) }\right) \lambda
_{\min }\left( L_{\rho }L_{\rho }^{\prime }\right) \geq 1/C_{1}>0\text{ }%
a.s.n.  \label{Omegtilde lower bd}
\end{equation}

Next, let%
\begin{equation*}
\underset{\left( d+1\right) \times 2}{D_{a}}=\left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
1 & 0 \\ 
0 & a%
\end{array}%
\right) \text{, }D_{SD,\left( i,t\right) }=\left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
\sigma _{\left( i,t\right) } & 0 \\ 
0 & \widetilde{\omega }_{a,\left( i,t\right) }%
\end{array}%
\right) \text{, and }D_{\varrho ,\left( i,t\right) }=\left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
1 & \varrho _{a,\left( i,t\right) } \\ 
\varrho _{a,\left( i,t\right) } & 1%
\end{array}%
\right)
\end{equation*}%
and note that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
D_{a}^{\prime }\widetilde{\Omega }_{\left( i,t\right) }D_{a} &=&\left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
1 & 0 \\ 
0 & a^{\prime }%
\end{array}%
\right) \left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] & E 
\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }\underline{U}_{\left( i,t\right)
}^{\prime }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\ 
E\left[ \underline{U}_{\left( i,t\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] & E\left[ \underline{U}_{\left( i,t\right) }%
\underline{U}_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]%
\end{array}%
\right) \left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
1 & 0 \\ 
0 & a%
\end{array}%
\right) \\
&=&\left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
\sigma _{\left( i,t\right) } & 0 \\ 
0 & \widetilde{\omega }_{a,\left( i,t\right) }%
\end{array}%
\right) \left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
1 & \varrho _{a,\left( i,t\right) } \\ 
\varrho _{a,\left( i,t\right) } & 1%
\end{array}%
\right) \left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
\sigma _{\left( i,t\right) } & 0 \\ 
0 & \widetilde{\omega }_{a,\left( i,t\right) }%
\end{array}%
\right) =D_{SD,\left( i,t\right) }D_{\varrho ,\left( i,t\right)
}D_{SD,\left( i,t\right) }\text{,}
\end{eqnarray*}%
Now, as can be seen from expression (\ref{Omegtilde lower bd}) above, an
implication of Assumption 2(ii) is that%
\begin{eqnarray}
\min_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\sigma _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}
&=&e_{1,d+1}^{\prime }\widetilde{\Omega }_{\left( i,t\right) }e_{1,d+1}\geq
1/C_{1}>0\text{ }a.s.n.  \label{sigma2 lower bd} \\
\min_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\widetilde{\omega }_{a,\left(
i,t\right) }^{2} &=&\underline{a}^{\prime }\widetilde{\Omega }_{\left(
i,t\right) }\underline{a}\geq 1/C_{1}>0\text{ }a.s.n.
\label{omega2 lower bd}
\end{eqnarray}%
where $\underset{\left( d+1\right) \times 1}{e_{1,d+1}}=\left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
1 & 0^{\prime }%
\end{array}%
\right) ^{\prime }$ and $\underset{\left( d+1\right) \times 1}{\underline{a}}%
=\left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
0 & a^{\prime }%
\end{array}%
\right) ^{\prime }$, from which we deduce that $D_{SD,\left( i,t\right) }$
is invertible almost surely for each $\left( i,t\right) \in \left\{
1,...,m_{n}\right\} $ and for all $n$ sufficiently large. The invertibility
of $D_{SD,\left( i,t\right) }$ then allows us to write $D_{\varrho ,\left(
i,t\right) }=D_{SD,\left( i,t\right) }^{-1}D_{a}^{\prime }\widetilde{\Omega }%
_{\left( i,t\right) }D_{a}D_{SD,\left( i,t\right) }^{-1}$. On the other
hand, Assumption 2(i) implies that there exists some constant $C_{2}>1$ such
that%
\begin{equation}
\min_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\lambda _{\min }\left( D_{SD,\left(
i,t\right) }^{-1}\right) =\frac{1}{\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}\lambda _{\max }\left( D_{SD,\left( i,t\right) }\right) }\geq \frac{1}{%
C_{2}}>0\text{ \ }a.s.  \label{DSD lower bd}
\end{equation}%
It follows from the fact that $\lambda _{\min }\left( D_{a}^{\prime
}D_{a}\right) =\lambda _{\min }\left( I_{2}\right) =1$ and from making use
of Assumptions 2(i) and (ii) and the lower bounds given in (\ref{Omegtilde
lower bd}) and (\ref{DSD lower bd}) that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\min_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\lambda _{\min }\left( D_{\varrho
,\left( i,t\right) }\right) &\geq &\min_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}\lambda _{\min }\left( \widetilde{\Omega }_{\left( i,t\right) }\right)
\lambda _{\min }\left( D_{a}^{\prime }D_{a}\right) \lambda _{\min }\left(
D_{SD,\left( i,t\right) }^{-2}\right) \\
&\geq &\frac{\min_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\lambda _{\min }\left( 
\widetilde{\Omega }_{\left( i,t\right) }\right) }{\max_{1\leq \left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left( \lambda _{\max }\left( D_{SD,\left( i,t\right)
}\right) \right) ^{2}}\geq \frac{1}{C^{3}}>0\text{ \ }a.s.n.,
\end{eqnarray*}%
where $C=\max \left\{ C_{1},C_{2}\right\} $. Moreover, by solving the
characteristic equation of $D_{\varrho ,\left( i,t\right) }$, we see that
the smallest eigenvalue of $D_{\varrho ,\left( i,t\right) }$ is given by $%
\lambda _{\min }\left( D_{\varrho ,\left( i,t\right) }\right) =1-\left\vert
\varrho _{a,\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert $, so that $\min_{1\leq \left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\lambda _{\min }\left( D_{\varrho ,\left( i,t\right)
}\right) =1-\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert \rho
_{a,\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert \geq 1/C^{3}>0$ \ $a.s.n.$, from which we
further deduce that $\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert
\varrho _{a,\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert \leq 1-\left( 1/C^{3}\right) <1$
\ $a.s.n.$ Applying this upper bound along with the lower bounds given by (%
\ref{sigma2 lower bd}) and (\ref{omega2 lower bd}) as well as the fact that $%
\lambda _{\min }\left( \Delta _{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{a}\right) =1-\left\vert \varrho _{a,\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert
\left\vert \varrho _{a,\left( j,s\right) }\right\vert $, as derived earlier,
we have%
\begin{eqnarray*}
E\left[ \left( \varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) }\underline{u}_{a,\left(
i,t\right) }+\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }\underline{u}_{a,\left(
j,s\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] &=&\delta _{a,\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime }\Delta _{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{a}\delta _{a,\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) } \\
&\geq &\left[ 1-\left\vert \varrho _{a,\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert
\left\vert \varrho _{a,\left( j,s\right) }\right\vert \right] \left[ \sigma
_{\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\widetilde{\omega }_{a,\left( i,t\right)
}^{2}+\sigma _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}\widetilde{\omega }_{a,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2}\right] \\
&\geq &\left( \frac{2}{C^{3}}-\frac{1}{C^{6}}\right) \left[ \frac{1}{C^{2}}+%
\frac{1}{C^{2}}\right] \geq \frac{2}{C^{5}}>0\text{ \ \ \ }a.s.n.
\end{eqnarray*}%
Summing over $1\leq \left( j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}$, we
obtain

\noindent $K_{2,n}^{-1}\dsum\nolimits_{\left( i,t\right)
=2}^{m_{n}}\dsum\nolimits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{\left( i,t\right)
-1}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}E\left[ \left( \varepsilon
_{\left( j,s\right) }\underline{u}_{a,\left( i,t\right) }+\varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }\underline{u}_{a,\left( j,s\right) }\right) ^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] $

\noindent $\geq \left( 2/C^{5}\right) K_{2,n}^{-1}\dsum\nolimits_{\left(
i,t\right) =2}^{m_{n}}\dsum\nolimits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{\left(
i,t\right) -1}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}=\left(
1/C^{5}\right) K_{2,n}^{-1}\dsum\nolimits_{\left( i,t\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\nolimits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}$, where the last equality follows from the symmetry
of $A$ and by the fact that $A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }=0$
for $\left( i,t\right) =1,...,m_{n}$. Furthermore, by straightforward
calculation, we obtain%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} &=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left[ e_{\left(
i,t\right) }^{\prime }P^{\perp }e_{\left( j,s\right) }-e_{\left( i,t\right)
}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,s\right) }\right] ^{2} \\
&=&1+\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}e_{\left(
i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }%
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}e_{\left( i,t\right) }\geq 1
\end{eqnarray*}%
Putting everything together, we have

\noindent $K_{2,n}^{-1}\dsum\nolimits_{\left( i,t\right)
=2}^{m_{n}}\dsum\nolimits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{\left( i,t\right)
-1}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}E\left[ \left( \varepsilon
_{\left( j,s\right) }\underline{u}_{a,\left( i,t\right) }+\varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }\underline{u}_{a,\left( j,s\right) }\right) ^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \geq $

\noindent $\left( 1/C^{5}\right) K_{2,n}^{-1}\dsum\nolimits_{\left(
i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\nolimits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\geq 1/C^{5}\geq \underline{C}>0$, by
choosing $\underline{C}$ such that $0<\underline{C}\leq 1/C^{5}$. Since the
above argument holds for any $a\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$ such that $\left\Vert
a\right\Vert =1$, it further follows that $VC\left( \underline{U}^{\prime
}A\varepsilon /\sqrt{K_{2,n}}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \geq \underline{C}%
I_{d}>0$ \ $a.s.$, as required.

To show part (c), note first that, given Assumption 2(i), there exists a
positive constant $C$ such that%
\begin{eqnarray}
&&\max_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\lambda _{\max }\left( E\left[ 
\underline{U}_{\left( j,s\right) }\underline{U}_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime
}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right)  \notag \\
&\leq &\max_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}tr\left\{ E\left[ \underline{%
U}_{\left( j,s\right) }\underline{U}_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime }|\mathcal{%
F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right\}  \notag \\
&\leq &\max_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\{ E\left[ \left\Vert
U_{\left( j,s\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] +2E%
\left[ \left\vert U_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime }\rho \varepsilon _{\left(
j,s\right) }\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] +\rho ^{\prime }\rho E%
\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\right\} \text{ }  \notag \\
&\leq &\max_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\{ E\left[ \left\Vert
U_{\left( j,s\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
+2\left\Vert \rho \right\Vert _{2}\sqrt{E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
j,s\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] }\sqrt{E\left[ \left\Vert
U_{\left( j,s\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] }%
\right.  \notag \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. +\left\Vert \rho \right\Vert
_{2}^{2}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \right\}  \notag \\
&\leq &2\left\{ \left( \max_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[
\left\Vert U_{\left( j,s\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \right) +\left\Vert \rho \right\Vert _{2}^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq
\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) }^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \right\}  \notag \\
&\leq &C<\infty \text{ \ }a.s.  \label{max eig EUU}
\end{eqnarray}

\noindent where the third inequality above follows from applying the CS
inequality while the fourth inequality stems in part from applying the
inequality $\left\vert XY\right\vert \leq \left( 1/2\right) X^{2}+\left(
1/2\right) Y^{2}$. Now, for any $a\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$ such that $\left\Vert
a\right\Vert _{2}=1$; we obtain by applying the triangle and CS
inequalities, expression (\ref{max eig EUU}), as well as part (a) of Lemma
S2-1 and Assumptions 2(i) and 8%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&a^{\prime }VC\left( \underline{U}^{\prime }A\varepsilon /\sqrt{K_{2,n}}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) a \\
&\leq &\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left( E\left[
\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] a^{\prime }E%
\left[ \underline{U}_{\left( j,s\right) }\underline{U}_{\left( j,s\right)
}^{\prime }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] a\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. +\sqrt{a^{\prime }E\left[ \underline{U}%
_{\left( i,t\right) }\underline{U}_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] a}\sqrt{E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] }\sqrt{a^{\prime }E\left[ \underline{U}_{\left(
j,s\right) }\underline{U}_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] a}\sqrt{E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] }\right) \\
&\leq &\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{ E\left[
\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \lambda
_{\max }\left( E\left[ \underline{U}_{\left( j,s\right) }\underline{U}%
_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \right. \\
&&\text{ }\left. +\sqrt{\lambda _{\max }\left( E\left[ \underline{U}_{\left(
j,s\right) }\underline{U}_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \right) }\sqrt{E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] }\sqrt{\lambda _{\max }\left( E\left[ \underline{U%
}_{\left( j,s\right) }\underline{U}_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime }|\mathcal{F%
}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) }\sqrt{E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] }\right\} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( 1\right) \text{.}
\end{eqnarray*}%
From this, we deduce that $\lambda _{\max }\left[ VC\left( \underline{U}%
^{\prime }A\varepsilon /\sqrt{K_{2,n}}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \right]
=\max_{\left\Vert a\right\Vert =1}a^{\prime }VC\left( \underline{U}^{\prime
}A\varepsilon /\sqrt{K_{2,n}}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) a$

\noindent $\leq \overline{C}$ \ $a.s.n.$ Moreover, by applying the law of
iterated expectations and part (i) of Theorem 16.1 of Billingsley (1995)
that there exists a constant $\overline{C}>0$ such that $a^{\prime }VC\left( 
\underline{U}^{\prime }A\varepsilon /\sqrt{K_{2,n}}\right) a=E_{Z}\left\{ E%
\left[ \left( a^{\prime }\underline{U}^{\prime }A\varepsilon \right)
^{2}/K_{2,n}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right\} \leq \overline{C}$, for all 
$a\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$ such that $\left\Vert a\right\Vert =1$, from which we
further deduce the unconditional version of this inequality, i.e., $\lambda
_{\max }\left( VC\left[ \underline{U}^{\prime }A\varepsilon /\sqrt{K_{2,n}}%
\right] \right) $

\noindent $=\max_{\left\Vert a\right\Vert =1}a^{\prime }VC\left( \underline{U%
}^{\prime }A\varepsilon /\sqrt{K_{2,n}}\right) a\leq \overline{C}<\infty $,
where $\underline{U}=U-\varepsilon \rho ^{\prime }$ and $\underline{U}%
_{\left( i,t\right) }=U_{\left( i,t\right) }-\rho \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }$.

Furthermore, since $\underline{U}=U-\varepsilon \rho ^{\prime }$, we see
that, by setting $\rho =0$ in the argument given above, we can also show
that there exists a constant $\overline{C}$ such that $\lambda _{\max
}\left( VC\left[ U^{\prime }A\varepsilon /\sqrt{K_{2,n}}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \right) \leq \overline{C}<\infty $ \ $a.s.n.$ and $\lambda _{\max
}\left( VC\left[ U^{\prime }A\varepsilon /\sqrt{K_{2,n}}\right] \right) \leq 
\overline{C}<\infty $ for all $n$ sufficiently large.

Finally, to show part (d), note first that, by straightforward calculations,
we get $\Sigma _{n}=VC\left( \mathcal{Y}_{n}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right)
=VC\left( \Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\varepsilon /\sqrt{n}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) +VC\left( D_{\mu }^{-1}%
\underline{U}^{\prime }A\varepsilon |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) =\Sigma
_{1,n}+\Sigma _{2,n}$. It follows by part (a) of this lemma that there
exists a positive constant $\underline{C}$ such that $\lambda _{\min }\left(
\Sigma _{n}\right) \geq \lambda _{\min }\left[ VC\left( \Upsilon ^{\prime
}Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon /\sqrt{n}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) \right] +\lambda _{\min }\left[ VC\left( D_{\mu }^{-1}%
\underline{U}^{\prime }A\varepsilon |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \right] \geq
\lambda _{\min }\left[ VC\left( \Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon /\sqrt{n}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \right] $

\noindent $\geq \underline{C}>0$ \ $a.s.n.$, so that $\Sigma _{n}$ is
positive definite $a.s.n$. Moreover, again by part (a) of this lemma, for
any $a\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$ such that $\left\Vert a\right\Vert =1$, 
\begin{eqnarray*}
a^{\prime }\Sigma _{n}^{-1}a &\leq &\frac{1}{\lambda _{\min }\left\{
VC\left( \Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\varepsilon /\sqrt{n}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) +VC\left( D_{\mu }^{-1}%
\underline{U}^{\prime }A\varepsilon |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \right\} } \\
&\leq &\frac{1}{\lambda _{\min }\left[ VC\left( \Upsilon ^{\prime
}Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon /\sqrt{n}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) \right] }\leq \frac{1}{\underline{C}}\leq \overline{C}%
<\infty \text{ }a.s.n.
\end{eqnarray*}%
where $\overline{C}$ can be taken to be any finite, positive constant such
that $\overline{C}\geq 1/\underline{C}$. $\square $

\bigskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma S2-4: }Under Assumptions 1-6, $D_{\mu
}^{-1}X^{\prime }A\varepsilon =\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon /\sqrt{n}+D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }A\varepsilon $

\noindent $=O_{p}\left( \max \left\{ 1,\sqrt{K_{2,n}}/\left( \mu _{n}^{\min
}\right) \right\} \right) $

\noindent \medskip

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma S2-4:}

To proceed, since%
\begin{eqnarray*}
A &=&P^{\perp }-M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) } \\
&=&P^{\left( Z,Q\right) }-P^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }-M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) } \\
&=&M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }-\left[ M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }+M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\right] \text{,}
\end{eqnarray*}
we can write%
\begin{eqnarray}
&&D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }A\varepsilon  \notag \\
&=&D_{\mu }^{-1}\left( \frac{D_{\kappa }}{\sqrt{n}}\Theta ^{\prime
}Z_{1}^{\prime }+\frac{D_{\mu }}{\sqrt{n}}\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime
}+\Xi ^{\prime }Q^{\prime }+U^{\prime }\right) \left( M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }-\left[ M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }+M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{%
\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\right] \right) \varepsilon 
\notag \\
&=&\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }A\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}+D_{\mu
}^{-1}U^{\prime }A\varepsilon  \label{DXAe}
\end{eqnarray}%
Moreover, by straightfoward calculations, it can be easily shown that%
\begin{eqnarray}
\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }A\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}} &=&\frac{%
\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon }{%
\sqrt{n}}-\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}-\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\varepsilon }{%
\sqrt{n}}  \notag \\
&=&\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}  \notag \\
&=&O_{p}\left( 1\right)  \label{GammaZ2e}
\end{eqnarray}

\noindent Now, let $b\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$ such that $\left\Vert b\right\Vert
_{2}=1$, and, by straightforward calculations, we obtain%
\begin{eqnarray*}
E\left( \left[ b^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }A\varepsilon \right] ^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) &=&K_{2,n}b^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}E\left( \frac{%
U^{\prime }A\varepsilon \varepsilon ^{\prime }AU}{K_{2,n}}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) D_{\mu }^{-1}b \\
&=&K_{2,n}b^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}VC\left( U^{\prime }A\varepsilon /\sqrt{%
K_{2,n}}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) D_{\mu }^{-1}b \\
&\leq &\lambda _{\max }\left[ VC\left( U^{\prime }A\varepsilon /\sqrt{K_{2,n}%
}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \right] \frac{K_{2,n}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min
}\right) ^{2}} \\
&\leq &\overline{C}\frac{K_{2,n}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}\text{ 
}a.s.
\end{eqnarray*}%
for some positive constant $\overline{C}<\infty $. Hence, for all $n$
sufficiently large%
\begin{equation*}
E\left( \frac{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}{K_{2,n}}\left[ b^{\prime
}D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }A\varepsilon \right] ^{2}\right) =E_{Z}\left\{ 
\frac{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}{K_{2,n}}E\left( \left[ b^{\prime
}D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }A\varepsilon \right] ^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) \right\} \leq \overline{C}\text{.}
\end{equation*}%
It follows from Markov's inequality, for any $\epsilon >0$, we can set $%
C_{\epsilon }=\sqrt{\overline{C}/\epsilon }$ so that for all $n$
sufficiently large%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\Pr \left( \left\vert \frac{\mu _{n}^{\min }}{\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}b^{\prime
}D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }A\varepsilon \right\vert \geq C_{\epsilon }\right)
&=&\Pr \left( \left\vert \frac{\mu _{n}^{\min }}{\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}b^{\prime
}D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }A\varepsilon \right\vert ^{2}\geq C_{\epsilon
}^{2}\right) \\
&\leq &\frac{1}{C_{\epsilon }^{2}}E\left( \frac{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min
}\right) ^{2}}{K_{2,n}}\left[ b^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime
}A\varepsilon \right] ^{2}\right) \\
&\leq &\frac{\overline{C}}{\overline{C}/\epsilon }=\epsilon
\end{eqnarray*}%
which shows that%
\begin{equation*}
b^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }A\varepsilon =O_{p}\left( \frac{\sqrt{%
K_{2,n}}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) }\right) .
\end{equation*}%
Since the above result holds for all $b\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$ such that $%
\left\Vert b\right\Vert _{2}=1$, we further deduce that 
\begin{equation}
D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }A\varepsilon =O_{p}\left( \frac{\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{%
\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) }\right) .  \label{OAe}
\end{equation}

Expressions (\ref{DXAe})-(\ref{OAe}) together imply that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\frac{D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }A\varepsilon }{\mu _{n}^{\min }} &=&\frac{%
\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }A\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}+D_{\mu
}^{-1}U^{\prime }A\varepsilon \\
&=&\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}+D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }A\varepsilon \\
&=&O_{p}\left( \max \left\{ 1,\frac{\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min
}\right) }\right\} \right) \text{. }\square
\end{eqnarray*}

\bigskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma S2-5: }Under Assumptions 1-6, $D_{\mu
}^{-1}X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon =O_{p}\left( n/\mu
_{n}^{\min }\right) $.

\noindent

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma S2-5: }

To proceed, let $b\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$ such that $\left\Vert b\right\Vert
_{2}=1$ and let $u_{b}=UD_{\mu }^{-1}b$ and $u_{b,\left( i,t\right)
}=U_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}b$. Now, write%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&b^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon \\
&=&b^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}\left( \frac{D_{\kappa }}{\sqrt{n}}\Theta
^{\prime }Z_{1}^{\prime }+\frac{D_{\mu }}{\sqrt{n}}\Upsilon ^{\prime
}Z_{2}^{\prime }+\Xi ^{\prime }Q^{\prime }+U^{\prime }\right) M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon \\
&=&\frac{b^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}+u_{b}^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon \text{. }
\end{eqnarray*}%
By straightforward calculations and by applying Assumptions 1, 2(i), 3, 4,
5(i), and 5(iii) as well as the CS and Markov's inequalities, we can show
that $b^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\varepsilon /\sqrt{n}=O_{p}\left( 1\right) $. From the CS inequality, we
also obtain $E\left[ \left\vert u_{b}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\varepsilon \right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] $

\noindent $\leq \sqrt{E\left[ u_{b}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }u_{b}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] }\sqrt{E\left[ \varepsilon ^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] }$. Next, note that,
by applying Assumptions 2(i) and 6(ii), we have $E\left[ \varepsilon
^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\leq E\left[ \varepsilon ^{\prime }\varepsilon |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\leq n\overline{T}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[
\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right)
=O_{a.s.}\left( n\right) $. Similarly, by applying Assumptions 2(i), 3(ii),
and 6(ii); we obtain $E\left[ u_{b}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }u_{b}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] $

\noindent $=E\left[ b^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }UD_{\mu }^{-1}b|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \leq \overline{T}%
\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert U_{\left(
i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \left[
n/\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}\right] $

\noindent $=O_{a.s.}\left( n\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{-2}\right) $.
It follows from these results that $E\left[ \left\vert u_{b}^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon \right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] =O_{a.s.}\left( n\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{-1}\right) $.
Hence, by the law of iterated expectations and Theorem 16.1 of Billingsley
(1995), there exists a constant $\overline{C}<\infty $ such that for all $n$
sufficiently large $E\left[ \left( \left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) /n\right)
\left\vert u_{b}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon \right\vert %
\right] $

\noindent $=E_{Z}\left( \left( \left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) /n\right) E%
\left[ \left\vert u_{b}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon
\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \leq \overline{C}$. By
applying Markov's inequality, we further obtain 
\begin{equation}
b^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon
=O_{p}\left( n\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{-1}\right) .  \label{UMZ1Qe}
\end{equation}%
Putting everything together, we have%
\begin{eqnarray*}
b^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon &=&%
\frac{b^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}+b^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon \\
&=&O_{p}\left( 1\right) +O_{p}\left( \frac{n}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) 
}\right) =O_{p}\left( \frac{n}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) }\right)
\end{eqnarray*}

\noindent Since the above argument holds for all $b\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$ such
that $\left\Vert b\right\Vert _{2}=1$, we further deduce that $D_{\mu
}^{-1}X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon =O_{p}\left( n\left(
\mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{-1}\right) $. $\square $

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma S2-6: }If Assumptions 2 and 8 are satisfied; then,
for $1\leq p\leq 8$ and for all $n$, there exists a positive constant $C$
such that $\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert 
\underline{U}_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{p}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \leq C<\infty \ a.s.$, where $\underline{U}_{\left( i,t\right)
}=U_{\left( i,t\right) }-\rho \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }$.

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma S2-6: }Note that, for $1\leq p\leq 8$ and
for any $\left( i,t\right) \in \left\{ 1,....,m_{n}\right\} $, there exists
a positive constant $C$ such that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
E\left[ \left\Vert \underline{U}_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{p}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] &=&E\left[ \left( \left\Vert U_{\left( i,t\right)
}-\rho \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}\right) ^{p}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &2^{p-1}\left\{ \left( E\left[ \left\Vert U_{\left( i,t\right)
}\right\Vert _{2}^{8}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{p/8}+\left\Vert
\rho \right\Vert _{2}^{p}\left( E\left[ \left\vert \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{8}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right)
^{p/8}\right\} \\
&\leq &C<\infty \text{ \ }a.s.\text{,}
\end{eqnarray*}%
where the first inequality follows by applying the triangle inequality, Lo%
\`{e}ve's $c_{r}$ inequality, and Liapunov's inequality in sequence and
where the second inequality follows from applying Assumption 2(i) and from
the fact that $\rho \in \mathcal{S}_{\rho }$, some compact subset of $%
\mathbb{R}^{d}$ as stated in Assumption 8. Since the upper bound above holds
for all $\left( i,t\right) \in \left\{ 1,....,m_{n}\right\} $, for all $\rho
\in \mathcal{S}_{\rho }$, and for all $n$, it further follows that $%
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert \underline{U}%
_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{p}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \leq
C<\infty $ \ $a.s.$, as required. $\square $

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma S2-7: }Under Assumptions 1-6, the following results
hold: (a) $\widehat{\ell }_{L,n}=o_{p}\left( \left[ \mu _{n}^{\min }\right]
^{2}/n\right) $; (b) $\widehat{\ell }_{F,n}=o_{p}\left( \left[ \mu
_{n}^{\min }\right] ^{2}/n\right) $.

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma S2-7: }To proceed, first define%
\begin{equation*}
\overline{D}_{n}=\left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
\mu _{n}^{\min } & 0 \\ 
0 & D_{\mu }%
\end{array}%
\right) \text{ and }L_{\delta }=\left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
1 & 0 \\ 
\delta _{0} & I_{d}%
\end{array}%
\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
and note that%
\begin{equation*}
L_{\delta }^{-1}=\left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
1 & 0 \\ 
-\delta _{0} & I_{d}%
\end{array}%
\right)
\end{equation*}%
Now, for any $\beta \in \mathbb{R}^{d+1}$ such that $\left\Vert \beta
\right\Vert _{2}=1$ and for $\overline{X}=\left[ 
\begin{array}{cc}
