y & X%
\end{array}%
\right] $, we can write $\beta ^{\prime }\overline{X}^{\prime }A\overline{X}%
\beta =$

\noindent $\beta ^{\prime }L_{\delta }^{\prime }\overline{D}_{n}\left( 
\overline{D}_{n}^{-1}L_{\delta }^{\prime -1}\overline{X}^{\prime }A\overline{%
X}L_{\delta }^{-1}\overline{D}_{n}^{-1}\right) \overline{D}_{n}L_{\delta
}\beta $. Moreover, by direct multiplication,%
\begin{equation*}
\overline{D}_{n}^{-1}L_{\delta }^{\prime -1}\overline{X}^{\prime }A\overline{%
X}L_{\delta }^{-1}\overline{D}_{n}^{-1}=\left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) ^{\prime }A\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) /\left(
\mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2} & \left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) ^{\prime
}AXD_{\mu }^{-1}/\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) \\ 
D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }A\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) /\left( \mu _{n}^{\min
}\right) & D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }AXD_{\mu }^{-1}%
\end{array}%
\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
Now, by straightforward but tedious calculations and by applying Assumptions
1, 2(i), 3(ii)-(iii), 4, 5, and 6(i), as well as Lemmas S2-3(c) and S2-1(a);
we can show that, under the rate condition $\sqrt{K_{2}}/\left( \mu
_{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}\rightarrow 0$,%
\begin{equation*}
\overline{D}_{n}^{-1}L_{\delta }^{\prime -1}\overline{X}^{\prime }A\overline{%
X}L_{\delta }^{-1}\overline{D}_{n}^{-1}=\left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
0 & 0 \\ 
0 & \Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}Z_{2}\Upsilon /n%
\end{array}%
\right) +o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{\footnote{%
Details of the calculations leading to this result can be obtained from the
authors upon request.},}
\end{equation*}%
where, in light of Assumption 3(iii), $\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }Z_{2}\Upsilon /n=O_{p}\left( 1\right) $ and $%
\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }Z_{2}\Upsilon /n$
is positive definite for all $n$ large sufficiently large. It follows that $%
\overline{D}_{n}^{-1}L_{\delta }^{\prime -1}\overline{X}^{\prime }A\overline{%
X}L_{\delta }^{-1}\overline{D}_{n}^{-1}$ is positive semidefinite w.p.a.1,
so that

\noindent $\beta ^{\prime }\overline{X}^{\prime }A\overline{X}\beta =\beta
^{\prime }L_{\delta }^{\prime }\overline{D}_{n}\left( \overline{D}%
_{n}^{-1}L_{\delta }^{\prime -1}\overline{X}^{\prime }A\overline{X}L_{\delta
}^{-1}\overline{D}_{n}^{-1}\right) \overline{D}_{n}L_{\delta }\beta \geq 0$
\ w.p.a.1 for all $\beta \in \mathbb{R}^{d+1}$ such that $\left\Vert \beta
\right\Vert _{2}=1$. Moreover, by straightforward calculations, we can show
that%
\begin{equation*}
\frac{\beta ^{\prime }\overline{X}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }%
\overline{X}\beta }{n}=\frac{\beta ^{\prime }L_{\delta ,2}^{\prime }D_{\mu
}\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }Z_{2}\Upsilon
D_{\mu }L_{\delta ,2}\beta }{n^{2}}+\beta ^{\prime }L_{\delta }^{\prime }E%
\left[ \frac{V^{\prime }M^{Q}V}{n}\right] L_{\delta }\beta +o_{p}\left(
1\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where $V=\left[ 
\begin{array}{cc}
\varepsilon & U%
\end{array}%
\right] $ and $L_{\delta ,2}=\left[ 
\begin{array}{cc}
\delta _{0} & I_{d}%
\end{array}%
\right] $ and where $E\left[ V^{\prime }M^{Q}V/n\right] $ is positive
definite for all $n$ sufficiently large in light of Assumptions 2(ii) and
6(i). Since $L_{\delta }\beta \neq 0$ for all $\beta \in \mathbb{R}^{d+1}$
such that $\left\Vert \beta \right\Vert _{2}=1$, it follows that $\beta
^{\prime }\overline{X}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\overline{X}\beta
/n>0$ \ w.p.a.1 for all $\beta \in \mathbb{R}^{d+1}$ such that $\left\Vert
\beta \right\Vert _{2}=1$. Hence, with probability approaching one as $%
n\rightarrow \infty $,%
\begin{equation*}
R\left( \beta \right) =\frac{\beta ^{\prime }\overline{X}^{\prime }A%
\overline{X}\beta }{\beta ^{\prime }\overline{X}^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\overline{X}\beta }
\end{equation*}%
is a continuous function of $\beta $ for all values of $\beta $ such that $%
\left\Vert \beta \right\Vert _{2}=1$. The Weierstrass extreme value theorem
then implies that there exists some $\widetilde{\beta }$ such that $%
\widetilde{\beta }=\arg \min_{\left\Vert \beta \right\Vert _{2}=1}R\left(
\beta \right) $ w.p.a.1. Next, note that $\widehat{\ell }_{L,n}$ is the
smallest root of the determinantal equation

\noindent $\det \left\{ \overline{X}^{\prime }A\overline{X}-\ell \overline{X}%
^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\overline{X}\right\} =0$; and, thus, $%
\widehat{\ell }_{L,n}$ has the representation 
\begin{equation*}
\widehat{\ell }_{L,n}=R\left( \widetilde{\beta }\right) =\frac{\widetilde{%
\beta }^{\prime }\overline{X}^{\prime }A\overline{X}\widetilde{\beta }}{%
\widetilde{\beta }^{\prime }\overline{X}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }%
\overline{X}\widetilde{\beta }}=\min_{\left\Vert \beta \right\Vert
_{2}=1}\left( \frac{\beta ^{\prime }\overline{X}^{\prime }A\overline{X}\beta 
}{\beta ^{\prime }\overline{X}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\overline{X%
}\beta }\right) .
\end{equation*}%
Now, let $\delta _{\ast }=\left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
1 & -\delta _{0}^{\prime }%
\end{array}%
\right) ^{\prime }/\left\Vert \left( 
\begin{array}{cc}
1 & -\delta _{0}^{\prime }%
\end{array}%
\right) ^{\prime }\right\Vert _{2}$; and we have, with probability
approaching one as $n\rightarrow \infty $, 
\begin{eqnarray*}
0 &\leq &\widehat{\ell }_{L,n}=\min_{\left\Vert \beta \right\Vert
_{2}=1}\left( \frac{\beta ^{\prime }\overline{X}^{\prime }A\overline{X}\beta 
}{\beta ^{\prime }\overline{X}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\overline{X%
}\beta }\right) \\
&\leq &\frac{\delta _{\ast }^{\prime }\overline{X}^{\prime }A\overline{X}%
\delta _{\ast }}{\delta _{\ast }^{\prime }\overline{X}^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\overline{X}\delta _{\ast }} \\
&=&\frac{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}{n}\left\{ \frac{\left(
y-X\delta _{0}\right) ^{\prime }A\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) /\sqrt{K_{2,n}}%
}{\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta
_{0}\right) /n}\right\} \frac{\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right)
^{2}} \\
&=&O\left( \frac{\left[ \mu _{n}^{\min }\right] ^{2}}{n}\right) O_{p}\left(
1\right) O_{p}\left( \frac{\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right)
^{2}}\right) =o_{p}\left( \frac{\left[ \mu _{n}^{\min }\right] ^{2}}{n}%
\right) \text{,}
\end{eqnarray*}%
given the rate condition $\sqrt{K_{2}}/\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right)
^{2}\rightarrow 0$. This shows part (a).

For part (b), we use the result in part (a) above and the fact that $%
m_{n}/n\sim 1$ by Assumption 5(i) to obtain%
\begin{equation}
\widehat{\ell }_{F,n}=\frac{\widehat{\ell }_{L,n}-\left( 1-\widehat{\ell }%
_{L,n}\right) C/m_{n}}{1-\left( 1-\widehat{\ell }_{L,n}\right) C/m_{n}}=%
\left[ \widehat{\ell }_{L,n}+O_{p}\left( \frac{1}{n}\right) \right] \left[
1+O_{p}\left( \frac{1}{n}\right) \right] =o_{p}\left( \frac{\left[ \mu
_{n}^{\min }\right] ^{2}}{n}\right) \text{. }\square \text{\textit{\ }}
\label{asy equiv of F and L}
\end{equation}

\bigskip

We introduce some notations before proceeding to the next lemma. Let

\noindent $\left( u_{\left( 1,1\right) ,n},\varepsilon _{\left( 1,1\right)
,n}\right) ,...,\left( u_{\left( 1,T_{1}\right) ,n},\varepsilon _{\left(
1,T_{1}\right) ,n}\right) ,\left( u_{\left( 2,1\right) ,n},\varepsilon
_{\left( 2,1\right) ,n}\right) ,...,\left( u_{\left( 2,T_{2}\right)
,n},\varepsilon _{\left( 2,T_{2}\right) ,n}\right) ,...,$

\noindent $\left( u_{\left( n,1\right) ,n},\varepsilon _{\left( n,1\right)
,n}\right) ....,\left( u_{\left( n,T_{n}\right) ,n},\varepsilon _{\left(
n,T_{n}\right) ,n}\right) $ denote a triangular array of (bivariate) random
vectors{\small . }Also, let $\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}=\phi _{\left(
i,t\right) ,n}\left( Z\right) ,\left( i,t\right) =1,...,m_{n}$, denote a
triangular array of measurable functions. In applications of the lemma given
below, we will take $\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}$ to be either a
conditional variance or a conditional covariance given $\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}=\sigma \left( Z\right) $, the $\sigma $-algebra generated by $Z$.
In addition, we let $\sigma _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}=E[\varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}],\;\overline{\omega }%
_{\left( i,t\right) .n}^{2}=E[u_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}],$and{\small \ }$\overline{\psi }_{\left( i,t\right)
,n}=E[\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}u_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}]$. In order to simplify notation, we suppress the dependence of $%
\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}$, $\sigma _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}$, $%
\overline{\omega }_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}$,\ and $\overline{\psi }%
_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}$\ on $Z$.

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma S2-8: }Let $A$ be as defined above. Assume that%
{\small \ }i){\small \ }$\left( u_{\left( 1,1\right) ,n},\varepsilon
_{\left( 1,1\right) }\right) ,...,\left( u_{\left( 1,T_{1}\right)
,n},\varepsilon _{\left( 1,T_{1}\right) }\right) ,$

\noindent $\left( u_{\left( 2,1\right) ,n},\varepsilon _{\left( 2,1\right)
,n}\right) ,...,\left( u_{\left( 2,T_{2}\right) ,n},\varepsilon _{\left(
2,T_{2}\right) ,n}\right) ,...,\left( u_{\left( n,1\right) ,n},\varepsilon
_{\left( n,1\right) ,n}\right) ....,\left( u_{\left( n,T_{n}\right)
,n},\varepsilon _{\left( n,T_{n}\right) ,n}\right) ${\small \ }are
independent conditional on $\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}=\sigma \left( Z\right) $;
ii)\ there exists a constant $C$\ such that, almost surely for all $n$
sufficiently large, $\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left(
u_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \leq C$, $%
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left( \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) ,n}^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \leq C$, and $\max_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert \phi _{\left( i,t\right)
,n}\right\vert \leq C$. In addition, define $\overline{\psi }_{\left(
j,s\right) ,n}=E\left[ u_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}\varepsilon _{\left(
j,s\right) ,n}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] $ for $\left( j,s\right)
=1,...,m_{n}$. Then, under Assumptions 5 and 6, the following statements are
true:

\noindent (a) $K_{2,n}^{-1}\dsum\nolimits_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) <\left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\phi
_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}\left\{ u_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}\varepsilon _{\left(
j,s\right) ,n}-\overline{\psi }_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}\right\} \overset{p}{%
\rightarrow }0$;

\noindent (b) $K_{2,n}^{-1}\dsum\nolimits_{1\leq \text{ }\left( k,\upsilon
\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq \text{ }m_{n}}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}\left\{ u_{\left( j,s\right)
,n}\varepsilon _{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,n}+\varepsilon _{\left(
j,s\right) ,n}u_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,n}\right\} \overset{p}{%
\rightarrow }0$;

\noindent (c) $K_{2,n}^{-1}\dsum\nolimits_{1\leq \text{ }\left( k,\upsilon
\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq \text{ }m_{n}}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}\varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right)
,n}\varepsilon _{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,n}\overset{p}{\rightarrow }0$;

\noindent (d) $K_{2,n}^{-1}\dsum\nolimits_{1\leq \text{ }\left( k,\upsilon
\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq \text{ }m_{n}}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}u_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}u_{\left(
k,\upsilon \right) ,n}\overset{p}{\rightarrow }0$.

{\small \noindent }\noindent \noindent

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma S2-8: }To show part (a), note that{\small \ 
}%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \left( \frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\nolimits_{1\leq \left( j,s\right)
<\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}\left\{ u_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}\varepsilon
_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}-\overline{\psi }_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}\right\}
\right) ^{2}\text{ }|\text{ }\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\nolimits_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) <\left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{4}\phi
_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}\left\{ E\left( \varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right)
,n}^{2}u_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) -\overline{%
\psi }_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}^{2}\right\} \\
&&+\frac{2}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\nolimits_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( k,\upsilon
\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\phi _{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,n}\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}\left\{
E\left( u_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}^{2}\varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) ,n}^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) -\overline{\psi }_{\left( j,s\right)
,n}^{2}\right\} \\
&\leq &\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\nolimits_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) <\left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\{ A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{4}\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}\right. \\
&&\left. \times \left[ \sqrt{E\left( u_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}^{4}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) E\left( \varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) ,n}^{4}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) }+E\left( u_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) E\left( \varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) ,n}^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) \right] \right\} \\
&&+\frac{2}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\nolimits_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( k,\upsilon
\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\left\vert \phi _{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,n}\right\vert \left\vert
\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}\right\vert \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \left\{ \sqrt{E\left( u_{\left(
j,s\right) ,n}^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) E\left( \varepsilon _{\left(
j,s\right) ,n}^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) }+E\left( u_{\left( j,s\right)
,n}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) E\left( \varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right)
,n}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \right\} \\
&\leq &C\left\{ \frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\nolimits_{1\leq \left( j,s\right)
<\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{4}+%
\frac{2}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\nolimits_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( k,\upsilon
\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\right\} \\
&\leq &C\left\{ \frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{4}+\frac{2}{%
K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) =1  \\ \left(
i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\right\} \\
&=&o_{a.s.}\left( 1\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
where the first inequality is the result of applying T and a conditional
version of CS, the second inequality follows by hypothesis, and the
convergence to zero almost surely follows from parts (b) and (c) of Lemma
S2-1 and the symmetry of $A$. It follows by the conditional version of the
Markov's inequality that for any $\epsilon >0$ 
\begin{equation*}
\Pr \left( \left\vert \frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\nolimits_{1\leq \left(
j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2}\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}\left\{ \varepsilon _{\left(
j,s\right) }u_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}-\overline{\psi }_{\left( j,s\right)
,n}\right\} \right\vert \geq \epsilon \text{ }|\text{ }\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) \rightarrow 0\text{ \ }a.s.
\end{equation*}%
Note further that%
\begin{equation*}
\sup_{n}E\left[ \left\vert \Pr \left( \left\vert \dsum\limits_{1\leq \left(
j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\frac{A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2}\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}\left\{ \varepsilon _{\left(
j,s\right) }u_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}-\overline{\psi }_{\left( j,s\right)
,n}\right\} }{K_{2,n}}\right\vert \geq \epsilon \text{ }|\text{ }\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) \right\vert ^{2}\right] <\infty
\end{equation*}%
Hence, by a version of the dominated convergence theorem, as given by
Theorem 25.12 of Billingsley (1986), we have, as $n\rightarrow \infty $,%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\Pr \left( \left\vert \frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\nolimits_{1\leq \left(
j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2}\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}\left\{ \varepsilon _{\left(
j,s\right) ,n}u_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}-\overline{\psi }_{\left( j,s\right)
,n}\right\} \right\vert \geq \epsilon \right) \\
&=&E\left[ \Pr \left( \left\vert \frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left(
j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2}\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}\left\{ \varepsilon _{\left(
j,s\right) ,n}u_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}-\overline{\psi }_{\left( j,s\right)
,n}\right\} \right\vert \geq \epsilon \text{ }|\text{ }\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) \right] \rightarrow 0,
\end{eqnarray*}%
as required for part (a).

To show part (b), first let $L$ be the lower triangular matrix such that $%
L_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }$

\noindent $=A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }\mathbb{I}\left\{
\left( i,t\right) >\left( j,s\right) \right\} $, and define $D_{\overline{%
\psi }}=diag\left( \overline{\psi }_{\left( 1,1\right) ,n},...,\overline{%
\psi }_{\left( n,T_{n}\right) ,n}\right) =diag\left( \overline{\psi }%
_{1},...,\overline{\psi }_{m_{n}}\right) $, $D_{\phi }=diag\left( \phi
_{\left( 1,1\right) },...,\phi _{\left( n,T_{n}\right) }\right) =diag\left(
\phi _{1},...,\phi _{m_{n}}\right) $, $\ u=\left( u_{\left( 1,1\right)
},...,u_{\left( n,T_{n}\right) }\right) ^{\prime }=\left(
u_{1},...,u_{m_{n}}\right) ^{\prime },$\ and $\varepsilon =\left(
\varepsilon _{\left( 1,1\right) },...,\varepsilon _{\left( n,T_{n}\right)
}\right) ^{\prime }=\left( \varepsilon _{1},...,\varepsilon _{m_{n}}\right)
^{\prime }$. \ It then follows by direct multiplication that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\varepsilon ^{\prime }L^{\prime }D_{\phi }Lu-tr\left\{ L^{\prime }D_{\phi
}LD_{\overline{\psi }}\right\} \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\phi _{\left( i,t\right)
,n}\left\{ u_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}\varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) ,n}-%
\overline{\psi }_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}\right\} \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{1\leq \text{ }\left( k,\upsilon \right) <\left( j,s\right)
<\left( i,t\right) \leq \text{ }m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\phi _{\left(
i,t\right) ,n}\left\{ u_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}\varepsilon _{\left(
k,\upsilon \right) ,n}+\varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) ,n}u_{\left(
k,\upsilon \right) ,n}\right\}
\end{eqnarray*}%
so that by making use of Lo\`{e}ve's $c_{r}$\ inequality, we have that%
\begin{eqnarray}
&&E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{\substack{ 1\leq \text{ }\left( k,\upsilon
\right) <\left( j,s\right)  \\ <\left( i,t\right) \leq \text{ }m_{n}}}\frac{%
A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) }\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}\left\{ u_{\left( j,s\right)
,n}\varepsilon _{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,n}+\varepsilon _{\left(
j,s\right) ,n}u_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,n}\right\} }{K_{2,n}^{2}}\right)
^{2}|\text{ }\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]  \notag \\
&\leq &2\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}E\left[ \left( u^{\prime }L^{\prime }D_{\phi
}L\varepsilon -tr\left\{ L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{\psi }}\right\}
\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]  \notag \\
&&+2\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{1\leq \left(
j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2}\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}\left\{ u_{\left( j,s\right)
,n}\varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) ,n}-\overline{\psi }_{\left( j,s\right)
,n}\right\} \right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]  \label{MS Calculation}
\end{eqnarray}%
From the proof of part (a), we already have%
\begin{equation*}
\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}E\left[ \left( \dsum\nolimits_{1\leq \left( j,s\right)
<\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}\left\{ u_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}\varepsilon
_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}-\overline{\psi }_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}\right\}
\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] =o_{a.s.}\left( 1\right) \text{.}
\end{equation*}

\noindent To show that{\small \ }%
\begin{equation*}
\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}E\left[ \left( u^{\prime }L^{\prime }D_{\phi
}L\varepsilon -tr\left\{ L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{\psi }}\right\}
\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] =o_{a.s.}\left( 1\right) ,
\end{equation*}

\noindent note first that%
\begin{eqnarray}
&&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}E\left[ \left( u^{\prime }L^{\prime }D_{\phi
}L\varepsilon -tr\left\{ L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LDD_{\overline{\psi }}\right\}
\right) ^{2}\text{ }|\text{ }\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]  \notag \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}E\left[ \left( u^{\prime }L^{\prime }D_{\phi
}L\varepsilon \right) ^{2}|\text{ }\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] -\frac{1}{%
K_{2,n}^{2}}\left[ tr\left\{ L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{\psi }%
}\right\} \right] ^{2}  \notag \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}E\left[ u^{\prime }L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\varepsilon
\otimes u^{\prime }L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\varepsilon \text{ }|\text{ }%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] -\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\left[ tr\left\{ L^{\prime
}D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{\psi }}\right\} \right] ^{2}  \notag \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}E\left[ tr\left\{ \left( u^{\prime }\otimes
u^{\prime }\right) \left( L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\otimes L^{\prime }D_{\phi
}L\right) \left( \varepsilon \otimes \varepsilon \right) \right\} |\text{ }%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]  \notag \\
&&-\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\left[ tr\left\{ L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{%
\psi }}\right\} \right] ^{2}  \notag \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ \left( L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\otimes
L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\right) E\left[ \varepsilon u^{\prime }\otimes
\varepsilon u^{\prime }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right\} -\frac{1}{%
K_{2,n}^{2}}\left[ tr\left\{ L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{\psi }%
}\right\} \right] ^{2}.  \label{MS calculation 1}
\end{eqnarray}%
Next, by straightforward calculations, we obtain%
\begin{eqnarray}
&&E\left[ \varepsilon u^{\prime }\otimes \varepsilon u^{\prime }|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right]  \notag \\
&=&\left( 
\begin{array}{ccc}
\sigma _{\left( 1,1\right) ,n}^{2}\overline{\omega }_{\left( 1,1\right)
,n}^{2}e_{\left( 1,1\right) }e_{\left( 1,1\right) }^{\prime } & \cdots & 
\sigma _{\left( 1,1\right) ,n}^{2}\overline{\omega }_{\left( n,T_{n}\right)
,n}^{2}e_{\left( 1,1\right) }e_{\left( n,T_{n}\right) }^{\prime } \\ 
\vdots &  & \vdots \\ 
\sigma _{\left( 1,T_{1}\right) ,n}^{2}\overline{\omega }_{\left( 1,1\right)
,n}^{2}e_{\left( 1,T_{1}\right) }e_{\left( 1,1\right) }^{\prime } & \cdots & 
\sigma _{\left( 1,T_{1}\right) ,n}^{2}\overline{\omega }_{\left(
n,T_{n}\right) ,n}^{2}e_{\left( 1,T_{1}\right) }e_{\left( n,T_{n}\right)
}^{\prime } \\ 
\vdots &  & \vdots \\ 
\sigma _{\left( n,1\right) ,n}^{2}\overline{\omega }_{\left( 1,1\right)
,n}^{2}e_{\left( n,1\right) }e_{\left( 1,1\right) }^{\prime } & \cdots & 
\sigma _{\left( n,1\right) ,n}^{2}\overline{\omega }_{\left( n,T_{n}\right)
,n}^{2}e_{\left( n,1\right) }e_{\left( n,T_{n}\right) }^{\prime } \\ 
\vdots &  & \vdots \\ 
\sigma _{\left( n,T_{n}\right) ,n}^{2}\overline{\omega }_{\left( 1,1\right)
,n}^{2}e_{\left( n,T_{n}\right) }e_{\left( 1,1\right) }^{\prime } & \cdots & 
\sigma _{\left( n,T_{n}\right) ,n}^{2}\overline{\omega }_{\left(
n,T_{n}\right) ,n}^{2}e_{\left( n,T_{n}\right) }e_{\left( n,T_{n}\right)
}^{\prime }%
\end{array}%
\right)  \notag \\
&&+\left( 
\begin{array}{ccc}
\overline{\psi }_{\left( 1,1\right) ,n}^{2}e_{\left( 1,1\right) }e_{\left(
1,1\right) }^{\prime } & \cdots & \overline{\psi }_{\left( 1,1\right) ,n}%
\overline{\psi }_{\left( n,T_{n}\right) ,n}e_{\left( n,T_{n}\right)
}e_{\left( 1,1\right) }^{\prime } \\ 
\vdots &  & \vdots \\ 
\overline{\psi }_{\left( 1,T_{1}\right) ,n}\overline{\psi }_{\left(
1,1\right) ,n}e_{\left( 1,1\right) }e_{\left( 1,T_{1}\right) }^{\prime } & 
\cdots & \overline{\psi }_{\left( 1,T_{1}\right) ,n}\overline{\psi }_{\left(
n,T_{n}\right) ,n}e_{\left( n,T_{n}\right) }e_{\left( 1,T_{1}\right)
}^{\prime } \\ 
\vdots &  & \vdots \\ 
\overline{\psi }_{\left( n,1\right) ,n}\overline{\psi }_{\left( 1,1\right)
,n}e_{\left( 1,1\right) }e_{\left( n,1\right) }^{\prime } & \cdots & 
\overline{\psi }_{\left( n,1\right) ,n}\overline{\psi }_{\left(
n,T_{n}\right) ,n}e_{\left( n,T_{n}\right) }e_{\left( n,1\right) }^{\prime }
\\ 
\vdots &  & \vdots \\ 
\overline{\psi }_{\left( n,T_{n}\right) ,n}\overline{\psi }_{\left(
1,1\right) ,n}e_{\left( 1,1\right) }e_{\left( n,T_{n}\right) }^{\prime } & 
\cdots & \overline{\psi }_{\left( n,T_{n}\right) ,n}\overline{\psi }_{\left(
n,T_{n}\right) ,n}e_{\left( n,T_{n}\right) }e_{\left( n,T_{n}\right)
}^{\prime }%
\end{array}%
\right)  \notag \\
&&+\left( 
\begin{array}{ccccc}
\overline{\varkappa }_{\left( 1,1\right) ,n}e_{\left( 1,1\right) }e_{\left(
1,1\right) }^{\prime } & \underset{m_{n}\times m_{n}}{0} & \cdots & \cdots & 
\underset{m_{n}\times m_{n}}{0} \\ 
\underset{m_{n}\times m_{n}}{0} & \ddots & \ddots &  & \vdots \\ 
\vdots & \ddots & \overline{\varkappa }_{\left( 1,T_{1}\right) ,n}e_{\left(
1,T_{1}\right) }e_{\left( 1,T_{1}\right) }^{\prime } & \ddots & \vdots \\ 
\vdots &  & \ddots & \ddots & \underset{m_{n}\times m_{n}}{0} \\ 
\underset{m_{n}\times m_{n}}{0} & \underset{m_{n}\times m_{n}}{0} & \cdots & 
\underset{m_{n}\times m_{n}}{0} & \overline{\varkappa }_{\left(
n,T_{n}\right) ,n}e_{\left( n,T_{n}\right) }e_{\left( n,T_{n}\right)
}^{\prime }%
\end{array}%
\right)  \notag \\
&&+\left( 
\begin{array}{ccccc}
\overline{\psi }_{\left( 1,1\right) ,n}\otimes D_{\overline{\psi }} & 
\underset{m_{n}\times m_{n}}{0} & \cdots & \cdots & \underset{m_{n}\times
m_{n}}{0} \\ 
\underset{m_{n}\times m_{n}}{0} & \ddots & \ddots &  & \vdots \\ 
\vdots & \ddots & \overline{\psi }_{\left( 1,T_{1}\right) ,n}\otimes D_{%
\overline{\psi }} & \ddots & \vdots \\ 
\vdots &  & \ddots & \ddots & \underset{m_{n}\times m_{n}}{0} \\ 
\underset{m_{n}\times m_{n}}{0} & \underset{m_{n}\times m_{n}}{0} & \cdots & 
\underset{m_{n}\times m_{n}}{0} & \overline{\psi }_{\left( n,T_{n}\right)
,n}\otimes D_{\overline{\psi }}%
\end{array}%
\right)  \notag \\
&=&\left( D_{\sigma }\otimes I_{m_{n}}\right) vec\left( I_{m_{n}}\right)
vec\left( I_{m_{n}}\right) \left( D_{\overline{\omega }}\otimes
I_{m_{n}}\right)  \notag \\
&&+\left( D_{\psi }\otimes I_{m_{n}}\right) \underline{K}_{m_{n}m_{n}}\left(
D_{\psi }\otimes I_{m_{n}}\right) +\underline{E}^{\prime }D_{\overline{%
\varkappa }}\underline{E}+\left( D_{\overline{\psi }}\otimes D_{\overline{%
\psi }}\right) ,  \label{MS Cal 2}
\end{eqnarray}%
where $\underline{K}_{m_{n}m_{n}}$\ is an $m_{n}^{2}\times m_{n}^{2}$\
commutation matrix such that for any $m_{n}\times m_{n}$\ matrix $A$, $%
\underline{K}_{m_{n}m_{n}}vec\left( A\right) =vec\left( A^{\prime }\right) $%
. Also, here, $D_{\overline{\psi }}=diag\left( \overline{\psi }_{1},....,%
\overline{\psi }_{m_{n}}\right) $, $D_{\sigma }=diag\left( \sigma
_{1}^{2},....,\sigma _{m_{n}}^{2}\right) $, $D_{\overline{\omega }%
}=diag\left( \overline{\omega }_{1}^{2},....,\overline{\omega }%
_{m_{n}}^{2}\right) $, $D_{\overline{\varkappa }}=diag\left( \overline{%
\varkappa }_{1},...,\overline{\varkappa }_{m_{n}}\right) $\ with $\overline{%
\varkappa }_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}=E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right)
,n}^{2}u_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] -\sigma
_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}\overline{\omega }_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}-2%
\overline{\psi }_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}\ \ $for $\left( i,t\right)
=1,....,m_{n}$. Also, let

\noindent $\underline{E}=\left( e_{1,m_{n}}\otimes e_{1,m_{n}},\cdot \cdot
\cdot ,e_{m_{n},m_{n}}\otimes e_{m_{n},m_{n}}\right) ^{\prime }$; and $%
e_{i,m_{n}}$\ is the $i^{th}$\ column of an $m_{n}\times m_{n}$\ identity
matrix . It follows from {\small (}\ref{MS calculation 1}{\small )} and (\ref%
{MS Cal 2}) that%
\begin{eqnarray}
&&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}E\left[ \left( u^{\prime }L^{\prime }D_{\phi
}L\varepsilon -tr\left\{ L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{\psi }}\right\}
\right) ^{2}\text{ }|\text{ }\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]  \notag \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ \left( L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\otimes
L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\right) E\left[ \varepsilon u^{\prime }\otimes
\varepsilon u^{\prime }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right\} -\frac{1}{%
K_{2,n}^{2}}\left[ tr\left\{ L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{\psi }%
}\right\} \right] ^{2}  \notag \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ \left( L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\otimes
L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\right) \left( D_{\sigma }\otimes I_{m_{n}}\right)
vec\left( I_{m_{n}}\right) vec\left( I_{m_{n}}\right) ^{\prime }\left( D_{%
\overline{\omega }}\otimes I_{m_{n}}\right) \right\}  \notag \\
&&+\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ \left( L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\otimes
L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\right) \left( D_{\psi }\otimes I_{m_{n}}\right) 
\underline{K}_{m_{n}m_{n}}\left( D_{\overline{\psi }}\otimes
I_{m_{n}}\right) \right\}  \notag \\
&&+\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ \left( L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\otimes
L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\right) \underline{E}^{\prime }D_{\overline{\varkappa }}%
\underline{E}\right\} +\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ \left( L^{\prime
}D_{\phi }L\otimes L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\right) \left( D_{\overline{\psi }%
}\otimes D_{\overline{\psi }}\right) \right\}  \notag \\
&&-\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\left[ tr\left\{ L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{%
\psi }}\right\} \right] ^{2}  \notag \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}vec\left( I_{m_{n}}\right) ^{\prime }\left( D_{%
\overline{\omega }}L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\sigma }\otimes L^{\prime
}D_{\phi }L\right) vec\left( I_{m_{n}}\right)  \notag \\
&&+\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ \left( D_{\psi }L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{%
\overline{\psi }}\otimes L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\right) \underline{K}%
_{m_{n}m_{n}}\right\} +\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ \left( L^{\prime
}D_{\phi }L\otimes L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\right) \underline{E}^{\prime }D_{%
\overline{\varkappa }}\underline{E}\right\}  \notag \\
&&+\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ \left( L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{%
\psi }}\otimes L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{\psi }}\right) \right\} -%
\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\left[ tr\left\{ L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{\psi 
}}\right\} \right] ^{2}  \notag \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{\omega }%
}L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\sigma }\right\} +\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{
\left( D_{\psi }L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{\psi }}\otimes L^{\prime
}D_{\phi }L\right) \underline{K}_{m_{n}m_{n}}\right\}  \notag \\
&&+\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ \left( L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\otimes
L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\right) \underline{E}^{\prime }D_{\overline{\varkappa }}%
\underline{E}\right\} +\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\left[ tr\left\{ L^{\prime
}D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{\psi }}\right\} \right] ^{2}-\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}%
\left[ tr\left\{ L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{\psi }}\right\} \right]
^{2}  \notag \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{\omega }%
}L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\sigma }\right\} +\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{
\left( D_{\overline{\psi }}L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{\psi }}\otimes
L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\right) \underline{K}_{m_{n}m_{n}}\right\}  \notag \\
&&+\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ \left( L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\otimes
L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\right) \underline{E}^{\prime }D_{\overline{\varkappa }}%
\underline{E}\right\}  \label{MS Cal 3}
\end{eqnarray}

Focusing first on the first term of (\ref{MS Cal 3}), we get%
\begin{eqnarray}
&&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{\omega }%
}L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\sigma }\right\}  \notag \\
&\leq &\sqrt{\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{%
\overline{\omega }}^{2}L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\right\} }\sqrt{\frac{1}{%
K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\sigma }^{2}L^{\prime }D_{\phi
}L\right\} }  \notag \\
&\leq &\sqrt{\underset{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}{\max }\overline{%
\omega }_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{4}}\sqrt{\underset{1\leq \left( i,t\right)
\leq m_{n}}{\max }\sigma _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{4}}\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}%
tr\left\{ L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LL^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\right\}  \notag \\
&\leq &\sqrt{\underset{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}{\max }\overline{%
\omega }_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{4}}\sqrt{\underset{1\leq \left( i,t\right)
\leq m_{n}}{\max }\sigma _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{4}}\sqrt{\frac{1}{%
K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ D_{\phi }LL^{\prime }D_{\phi }^{2}LL^{\prime }D_{\phi
}\right\} }\sqrt{\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ LL^{\prime }LL^{\prime
}\right\} }  \notag \\
&\leq &\sqrt{\underset{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}{\max }\overline{%
\omega }_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{4}}\sqrt{\underset{1\leq \left( i,t\right)
\leq m_{n}}{\max }\sigma _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{4}}\sqrt{\underset{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}{\max }\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}}  \notag
\\
&&\times \sqrt{\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ LL^{\prime }D_{\phi
}^{2}LL^{\prime }\right\} }\sqrt{\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ LL^{\prime
}LL^{\prime }\right\} }  \notag \\
&\leq &\sqrt{\underset{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}{\max }\overline{%
\omega }_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{4}}\sqrt{\underset{1\leq \left( i,t\right)
\leq m_{n}}{\max }\sigma _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{4}}\left( \underset{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}{\max }\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}\right) 
\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ L^{\prime }LL^{\prime }L\right\}  \notag \\
&\leq &\sqrt{\underset{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}{\max }E\left(
u_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) }\sqrt{\underset{%
1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}{\max }E\left( \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) ,n}^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) }\left( \underset{1\leq \left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}{\max }\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}\right) \frac{1%
}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ L^{\prime }LL^{\prime }L\right\}  \notag \\
&\leq &C\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ L^{\prime }LL^{\prime }L\right\} =%
\frac{C}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\left\Vert LL^{\prime }\right\Vert _{F}^{2}\text{ \ \ }%
a.s.\text{,}  \label{bound 1}
\end{eqnarray}%
where the first and third inequalities follow from CS and where the sixth
inequality follows from the conditional version of the Jensen's inequality
and the last inequality follows in light of the assumptions of this lemma.
In addition, let $G$\ be an $m_{n}\times m_{n}$\ matrix and $D=diag\left(
d_{1},...,d_{m_{n}}\right) $\ such that $d_{\left( i,t\right) }\geq 0$\ for
all $\left( i,t\right) \in \left\{ 1,...,m_{n}\right\} $, and note that the
second and fourth inequalities in (\ref{bound 1}) above follows from the
inequality%
\begin{equation}
tr\left\{ G^{\prime }DG\right\} \leq \left\{ \underset{\left( i,t\right) }{%
\max }\left( d_{\left( i,t\right) }\right) \right\} tr\left( G^{\prime
}G\right) \text{.}  \label{simple bd}
\end{equation}

Turning our attention now to the second term of (\ref{MS Cal 3}), we see
that, using the identity

\noindent $tr\left\{ \left( A\otimes B\right) \underline{K}%
_{m_{n}m_{n}}\right\} =tr\left\{ AB\right\} $ for $m_{n}\times m_{n}$
matrices $A$ and $B$, 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ \left( D_{\overline{\psi }}L^{\prime
}D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{\psi }}\otimes L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\right) 
\underline{K}_{m_{n}m_{n}}\right\} \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ D_{\overline{\psi }}L^{\prime }D_{\phi
}LD_{\overline{\psi }}L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\right\} =\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}%
tr\left\{ L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{\psi }}L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{%
\overline{\psi }}\right\} .
\end{eqnarray*}%
It follows by calculations similar to that used to obtain (\ref{bound 1}),
we obtain%
\begin{eqnarray}
&&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ \left( D_{\overline{\psi }}L^{\prime
}D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{\psi }}\otimes L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\right) 
\underline{K}_{m_{n}m_{n}}\right\}  \notag \\
&\leq &\left( \underset{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}{\max }\overline{%
\psi }_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}\right) \left( \underset{1\leq \left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}{\max }\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}\right) \frac{1%
}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ L^{\prime }LL^{\prime }L\right\}  \notag \\
&\leq &C\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ L^{\prime }LL^{\prime }L\right\} =%
\frac{C}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\left\Vert LL^{\prime }\right\Vert _{F}^{2}\text{ \ \ }%
a.s.  \label{bound 2}
\end{eqnarray}

Finally, to analyze the third term of (\ref{MS Cal 3}), we note that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\left\vert tr\left\{ \left( L^{\prime }D_{\phi
}L\otimes L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\right) \underline{E}^{\prime }D_{\overline{%
\varkappa }}\underline{E}\right\} \right\vert \\
&\leq &\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left\vert \overline{\varkappa }_{\left( i,t\right)
,n}\right\vert tr\left\{ e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }L^{\prime }D_{\phi
}Le_{\left( i,t\right) }L^{\prime }D_{\phi }Le_{\left( i,t\right) }e_{\left(
i,t\right) }^{\prime }\right\} \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left\vert \overline{\varkappa }_{\left( i,t\right)
,n}\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }L^{\prime }D_{\phi
}Le_{\left( i,t\right) }\right) ^{2} \\
&\leq &\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left\vert \overline{\varkappa }_{\left( i,t\right)
,n}\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }L^{\prime }D_{\phi
}^{2}Le_{\left( i,t\right) }\right) \left( e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime
}L^{\prime }Le_{\left( i,t\right) }\right) \\
&\leq &\left( \underset{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}{\max }\phi
_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}\right) \frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\left(
i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left\vert \overline{\varkappa }_{\left( i,t\right)
,n}\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }L^{\prime }Le_{\left(
i,t\right) }\right) ^{2} \\
&\leq &\left\{ \sqrt{E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{4}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] }\sqrt{E\left[ u_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{4}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] }+\left( \underset{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}{\max }\sigma _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}\right) \left( \underset{%
1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}{\max }\overline{\omega }_{\left(
i,t\right) ,n}^{2}\right) \right. \\
&&\left. +2\left( \underset{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}{\max }%
\overline{\psi }_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}\right) \right\} \left( \underset{%
1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}{\max }\phi _{\left( i,t\right)
,n}^{2}\right) \frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left( e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }L^{\prime }Le_{\left(
i,t\right) }\right) ^{2} \\
&\leq &C\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left( e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }L^{\prime }Le_{\left(
i,t\right) }\right) ^{2}\leq C\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\left(
i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left( e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }A^{\prime
}Ae_{\left( i,t\right) }\right) ^{2} \\
&=&C\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left(
e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }\left[ P^{\perp }-M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{%
\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\right] ^{2}e_{\left( i,t\right)
}\right) ^{2} \\
&=&C\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left(
e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }P^{\perp }e_{\left( i,t\right) }+e_{\left(
i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }%
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}e_{\left( i,t\right) }\right) ^{2}
\end{eqnarray*}%
where the first inequality above follows from T, the second inequality
follows from CS, the third inequality makes use of (\ref{simple bd}), the
fourth inequality uses CS and T, and the fifth inequality stems from our
assumption about the (almost sure) boundedness of the conditional moments.
Applying the inequality $\left\vert \dsum\nolimits_{i=1}^{m}a_{i}\right\vert
^{r}\leq m^{r-1}\dsum\nolimits_{i=1}^{m}\left\vert a_{i}\right\vert ^{r}$
for $r\geq 1$, we further obtain%
\begin{eqnarray}
&&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\left\vert tr\left\{ \left( L^{\prime }D_{\phi
}L\otimes L^{\prime }D_{\phi }L\right) \underline{E}^{\prime }D_{\overline{%
\varkappa }}\underline{E}\right\} \right\vert  \notag \\
&\leq &2C\left[ \frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp }\right)
^{2}+\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left(
e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }%
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}e_{\left( i,t\right) }\right) ^{2}\right]  \notag \\
&\leq &2C\left[ \frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{\perp }\right)
^{2}+\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert \widehat{%
\vartheta }_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\right) \frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}%
tr\left\{ D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{%
\vartheta }}\right\} \right]  \notag \\
&\leq &2C\left[ 1+\left( \frac{1}{C_{\ast }}\right) ^{2}\right] \left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,t\right) }^{\perp }\right) \left[ \frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{%
\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right)
}^{\perp }+\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}tr\left\{ D_{\widehat{\vartheta }%
}^{2}\right\} \right]  \notag \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{1}{n}\right)  \label{bound 3}
\end{eqnarray}%
where we have used Assumption 5(iv) and part (a) of Lemma OA-1 in arriving
at the last line above.

In light of (\ref{MS Cal 3}), it follows from (\ref{bound 1}), (\ref{bound 2}%
), (\ref{bound 3}), and Lemma OA-11 (given in section 3 below) that 
\begin{equation*}
\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}E\left[ \left( u^{\prime }L^{\prime }D_{\phi
}L\varepsilon -tr\left\{ L^{\prime }D_{\phi }LD_{\overline{\psi }}\right\}
\right) ^{2}\text{ }|\text{ }\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \leq 2C\left(
1/K_{2,n}^{2}\right) \left\Vert LL^{\prime }\right\Vert _{F}^{2}+C\left(
1/K_{2,n}\right) \leq C/K_{2,n}\text{ \ }a.s.
\end{equation*}%
It follows from (\ref{MS Calculation}) that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{1\leq \text{ }\left( k,\upsilon \right)
<\left( j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq \text{ }m_{n}}\frac{A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}\left\{ u_{\left( j,s\right)
,n}\varepsilon _{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,n}+\varepsilon _{\left(
j,s\right) ,n}u_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,n}\right\} }{K_{2,n}^{2}}\right)
^{2}|\text{ }\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&o_{a.s.}\left( 1\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
Moreover, by the conditional version of the Markov's inequality, we deduce
for any $\epsilon >0$ 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\Pr \left( \left\vert \dsum\limits_{1\leq \text{ }\left( k,\upsilon
\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq \text{ }m_{n}}\frac{%
A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) }\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}\left\{ u_{\left( j,s\right)
,n}\varepsilon _{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,n}+\varepsilon _{\left(
j,s\right) }u_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,n}\right\} }{K_{2,n}}\right\vert
\geq \epsilon \text{ }|\text{ }\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \\
&\rightarrow &0\text{ \ }a.s.
\end{eqnarray*}%
Since%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\sup_{n}E\left[ \left\vert \Pr \left( \left\vert \dsum\limits_{\substack{ %
1\leq \text{ }\left( k,\upsilon \right) <\left( j,s\right)  \\ <\left(
i,t\right) \leq \text{ }m_{n}}}\frac{A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\phi _{\left( i,t\right)
,n}\left\{ u_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}\varepsilon _{\left( k,\upsilon \right)
,n}+\varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) ,n}u_{\left( k,\upsilon \right)
,n}\right\} }{K_{2,n}}\right\vert \geq \epsilon \text{ }|\text{ }\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) \right\vert ^{2}\right] \\
&<&\infty \text{,}
\end{eqnarray*}%
it further follows by a version of the dominated convergence theorem, as
given by Theorem 25.12 of Billingsley (1986), that as $n\rightarrow \infty $%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\Pr \left( \left\vert \dsum\limits_{1\leq \text{ }\left( k,\upsilon
\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq \text{ }m_{n}}\frac{%
A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) }\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}\left\{ u_{\left( j,s\right)
,n}\varepsilon _{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,n}+\varepsilon _{\left(
j,s\right) ,n}u_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,n}\right\} }{K_{2,n}}\right\vert
\geq \epsilon \right) \\
&=&E\left[ \Pr \left( \left\vert \dsum\limits_{1\leq \text{ }\left(
k,\upsilon \right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq \text{ }m_{n}}%
\frac{A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) }\phi _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}\left\{ u_{\left( j,s\right)
,n}\varepsilon _{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,n}+\varepsilon _{\left(
j,s\right) ,n}u_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,n}\right\} }{K_{2,n}}\right\vert
\geq \epsilon \text{ }|\text{ }\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \right] \\
&\rightarrow &0,
\end{eqnarray*}%
as required for part (b).

It is easily seen that parts (c) and (d) can be proved in essentially the
same way as part (b); hence, to avoid redundancy, we do not provide detailed
arguments here. $\square $

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma S2-9: }Let 
\begin{equation*}
\widehat{\Delta }\left( \delta _{0}\right) =-\frac{\left( y-X\delta
_{0}\right) ^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) 
}{2}\left. \frac{\partial }{\partial \delta }\left\{ \frac{\left( y-X\delta
\right) ^{\prime }A\left( y-X\delta \right) }{\left( y-X\delta \right)
^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta \right) }\right\}
\right\vert _{\delta =\delta _{0}}\text{.}
\end{equation*}%
If Assumptions 1-6 and 8 are satisfied; then, $D_{\mu }^{-1}\widehat{\Delta }%
\left( \delta _{0}\right) =\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon /\sqrt{n}+D_{\mu }^{-1}\underline{U}^{\prime
}A\varepsilon +o_{p}\left( 1\right) $, where $\underline{U}=U-\varepsilon
\rho ^{\prime }$ and where $\rho =\lim_{n\rightarrow \infty }E\left[
U^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right] /E\left[ \varepsilon ^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right] $.

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma S2-9: }To proceed, note first that we can
write%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\widehat{\Delta }\left( \delta _{0}\right) \\
&=&-\frac{\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) ^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) }{2}\left. \frac{\partial }{\partial \delta }%
\left\{ \frac{\left( y-X\delta \right) ^{\prime }A\left( y-X\delta \right) }{%
\left( y-X\delta \right) ^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left(
y-X\delta \right) }\right\} \right\vert _{\delta =\delta _{0}} \\
&=&-\frac{\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) ^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) }{2} \\
&&\times \left\{ \frac{-2X^{\prime }A\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) }{\left(
y-X\delta _{0}\right) ^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta
_{0}\right) }+\frac{\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) ^{\prime }A\left( y-X\delta
_{0}\right) 2X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta
_{0}\right) }{\left[ \left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) ^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) \right] ^{2}}\right\} \\
&=&X^{\prime }A\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) -\frac{\left( y-X\delta
_{0}\right) ^{\prime }A\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) }{\left( y-X\delta
_{0}\right) ^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) 
}X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) \\
&=&X^{\prime }A\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) -\widehat{\ell }\left( \delta
_{0}\right) X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
where $A=P^{\perp }-M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }$. It follows from making use of the fact that

\noindent $\rho _{n}=E\left[ U^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\varepsilon \right] /E\left[ \varepsilon ^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\varepsilon \right] $ and from applying Lemma OA-5 and part (c) of Lemma
OA-4 that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&D_{\mu }^{-1}\widehat{\Delta }\left( \delta _{0}\right) \\
&=&D_{\mu }^{-1}\left[ X^{\prime }A\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) -\widehat{%
\ell }\left( \delta _{0}\right) X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left(
y-X\delta _{0}\right) \right] \\
&=&D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }A\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) -\widehat{\ell }%
\left( \delta _{0}\right) D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) \\
&=&\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}+D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }A\varepsilon -\frac{%
\varepsilon ^{\prime }A\varepsilon }{\varepsilon ^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon }%
\left[ 1+O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{1,n}}{n}\right) \right] \left[ \frac{\Upsilon
^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}%
+D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon \right] \\
&=&\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}+D_{\mu }^{-1}\left( U-\varepsilon \rho ^{\prime
}\right) ^{\prime }A\varepsilon -\varepsilon ^{\prime }A\varepsilon D_{\mu
}^{-1}\left[ \frac{U^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon }{%
\varepsilon ^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon }-\rho \right] \left[ 1+O_{p}\left( 
\frac{K_{1,n}}{n}\right) \right] \\
&&-\frac{\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{n}\frac{\varepsilon ^{\prime }A\varepsilon /\sqrt{%
K_{2,n}}}{\varepsilon ^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon /n}\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime
}Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}%
+O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{1,n}\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{n^{2}}\right) +O_{p}\left( \frac{%
K_{1,n}\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) n}\right) \\
&=&\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}+D_{\mu }^{-1}\left( U-\varepsilon \rho ^{\prime
}\right) ^{\prime }A\varepsilon -\varepsilon ^{\prime }A\varepsilon D_{\mu
}^{-1}\left[ \frac{U^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon }{%
\varepsilon ^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon }-\rho \right] \left[ 1+O_{p}\left( 
\frac{K_{1,n}}{n}\right) \right] \\
&&+O_{p}\left( \frac{\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{n}\right) +O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{1,n}%
\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) n}\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&=&\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}+D_{\mu }^{-1}\left( U-\varepsilon \rho ^{\prime
}\right) ^{\prime }A\varepsilon +O_{p}\left( \frac{1}{\mu _{n}^{\min }}\max
\left\{ \sqrt{\frac{K_{2,n}}{n}},\frac{K_{1,n}\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{n}\right\}
\right) \\
&&+O_{p}\left( \frac{\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{n}\right) +O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{1,n}%
\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) n}\right) \\
&=&\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}+D_{\mu }^{-1}\underline{U}^{\prime }A\varepsilon
+O_{p}\left( \max \left\{ \frac{1}{\mu _{n}^{\min }}\sqrt{\frac{K_{2,n}}{n}},%
\frac{K_{1,n}\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) n}\right\}
\right) \text{. } \\
&=&\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}+D_{\mu }^{-1}\underline{U}^{\prime }A\varepsilon
+o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{. }\square
\end{eqnarray*}

\noindent

\noindent \textbf{Lemma S2-10: }Let Assumptions 1-6 be satisfied, and let $%
\overline{\delta }_{n}$ be any estimator such that, as $n\rightarrow \infty $%
, $D_{\mu }\left( \overline{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right) /\mu _{n}^{\min
}=o_{p}\left( 1\right) $. Then, $-D_{\mu }^{-1}\left( \partial \widehat{%
\Delta }\left( \overline{\delta }_{n}\right) /\partial \delta ^{\prime
}\right) D_{\mu }^{-1}=H_{n}+o_{p}\left( 1\right) $, where $H_{n}=\Upsilon
^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }Z_{2}\Upsilon /n$ and
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\widehat{\Delta }\left( \delta \right) &=&-\left[ \left( y-X\delta \right)
^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta \right) /2\right] \left[
\partial \widehat{Q}_{FELIM}\left( \delta \right) /\partial \delta \right] \\
&=&X^{\prime }A\left( y-X\delta \right) -\widehat{\ell }\left( \delta
\right) X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta \right) ,
\end{eqnarray*}

\noindent

\noindent with%
\begin{equation*}
\widehat{\ell }\left( \delta \right) =\left( y-X\delta \right) ^{\prime
}A\left( y-X\delta \right) /\left[ \left( y-X\delta \right) ^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta \right) \right] .
\end{equation*}

\noindent In addition, we also have%
\begin{equation}
D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }\left[ A-\widehat{\ell }\left( \overline{\delta }%
_{n}\right) M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\right] XD_{\mu
}^{-1}=H_{n}+o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{.}  \label{LIM denom term}
\end{equation}

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma S2-10:}

Taking derivative of $-\widehat{\Delta }\left( \delta \right) $ with respect
to $\delta $, we obtain%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&-\frac{\partial \widehat{\Delta }\left( \delta \right) }{\partial \delta
^{\prime }} \\
&=&X^{\prime }AX-\frac{\left( y-X\delta \right) ^{\prime }A\left( y-X\delta
\right) }{\left( y-X\delta \right) ^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\left( y-X\delta \right) }X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }X-\frac{%
2X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta \right) \left(
y-X\delta \right) ^{\prime }AX}{\left( y-X\delta \right) ^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta \right) } \\
&&+2X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta \right) \left(
y-X\delta \right) ^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }X\frac{\left(
y-X\delta \right) ^{\prime }A\left( y-X\delta \right) }{\left[ \left(
y-X\delta \right) ^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta
\right) \right] ^{2}} \\
&=&X^{\prime }AX-\widehat{\ell }\left( \delta \right) X^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }X \\
&&-\frac{2X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta \right) }{%
\left( y-X\delta \right) ^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left(
y-X\delta \right) }\left\{ \left( y-X\delta \right) ^{\prime }AX-\widehat{%
\ell }\left( \delta \right) \left( y-X\delta \right) ^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }X\right\} \\
&=&X^{\prime }AX-\widehat{\ell }\left( \delta \right) X^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }X-\frac{2X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left(
y-X\delta \right) }{\left( y-X\delta \right) ^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta \right) }\widehat{\Delta }\left( \delta
\right) ^{\prime }
\end{eqnarray*}%
so that evaluating $-\partial \widehat{\Delta }\left( \delta \right)
/\partial \delta ^{\prime }$ at $\delta =\overline{\delta }_{n}$, we have%
\begin{eqnarray*}
-\frac{\partial \widehat{\Delta }\left( \overline{\delta }_{n}\right) }{%
\partial \delta ^{\prime }} &=&X^{\prime }AX-\widehat{\ell }\left( \overline{%
\delta }_{n}\right) X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }X-\frac{2X^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\overline{\delta }_{n}\right) }{\left(
y-X\overline{\delta }_{n}\right) ^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left(
y-X\overline{\delta }_{n}\right) }\widehat{\Delta }\left( \overline{\delta }%
_{n}\right) ^{\prime } \\
&=&X^{\prime }\left[ A-\widehat{\ell }\left( \overline{\delta }_{n}\right)
M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\right] X-\frac{2X^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\overline{\delta }_{n}\right) }{\left( y-X%
\overline{\delta }_{n}\right) ^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X%
\overline{\delta }_{n}\right) }\widehat{\Delta }\left( \overline{\delta }%
_{n}\right) ^{\prime }
\end{eqnarray*}%
Pre-multiplying and post-multiplying the above expression by $D_{\mu }^{-1}$%
, we then obtain 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&-D_{\mu }^{-1}\left( \frac{\partial \widehat{\Delta }\left( \overline{%
\delta }_{n}\right) }{\partial \delta ^{\prime }}\right) D_{\mu }^{-1} \\
&=&D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }\left[ A-\widehat{\ell }\left( \overline{\delta }%
_{n}\right) M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\right] XD_{\mu }^{-1}-\frac{2D_{\mu
}^{-1}X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\overline{\delta }%
_{n}\right) }{\left( y-X\overline{\delta }_{n}\right) ^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\overline{\delta }_{n}\right) }\widehat{\Delta }%
\left( \overline{\delta }_{n}\right) ^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}
\end{eqnarray*}%
Now, part (b) of Lemma S2-2 gives%
\begin{equation}
D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }AXD_{\mu }^{-1}=\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime
}Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }Z_{2}\Upsilon }{n}+o_{p}\left(
1\right) =H_{n}+o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{,}  \label{LIM denom term 1}
\end{equation}%
and, by part (a) of Lemma S2-2 as well as parts (c) and (d) of Lemma OA-6
given section 3 of this online appendix below, we have%
\begin{eqnarray}
&&\widehat{\ell }\left( \overline{\delta }_{n}\right) D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }XD_{\mu }^{-1}  \notag \\
&=&\frac{\left( y-X\overline{\delta }_{n}\right) ^{\prime }A\left( y-X%
\overline{\delta }_{n}\right) /\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}{\left(
y-X\overline{\delta }_{n}\right) ^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left(
y-X\overline{\delta }_{n}\right) /n}\left( \left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right)
^{2}\frac{D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }XD_{\mu }^{-1}}{n%
}\right)  \notag \\
&=&o_{p}\left( 1\right) O_{p}\left( 1\right) =o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{. }
\label{LIM denom term 2}
\end{eqnarray}%
It follows from expressions (\ref{LIM denom term 1}) and (\ref{LIM denom
term 2}) that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }\left[ A-\widehat{\ell }\left( \overline{\delta }%
_{n}\right) M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\right] XD_{\mu }^{-1} &=&D_{\mu
}^{-1}X^{\prime }AXD_{\mu }^{-1}-\widehat{\ell }\left( \overline{\delta }%
_{n}\right) D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }XD_{\mu }^{-1}
\\
&=&H_{n}+o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{.}
\end{eqnarray*}

\noindent where $H_{n}=\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }Z_{2}\Upsilon /n$. Moreover, making use of parts (a)-(d) of
Lemma OA-6, we further obtain 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\frac{2D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X%
\overline{\delta }_{n}\right) }{\left( y-X\overline{\delta }_{n}\right)
^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\overline{\delta }_{n}\right) }%
\widehat{\Delta }\left( \overline{\delta }_{n}\right) ^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}
\\
&=&\frac{2D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X%
\overline{\delta }_{n}\right) /n}{\left( y-X\overline{\delta }_{n}\right)
^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\overline{\delta }_{n}\right)
/n} \\
&&\times \left[ \left( y-X\overline{\delta }_{n}\right) ^{\prime }AXD_{\mu
}^{-1}-\frac{\left( y-X\overline{\delta }_{n}\right) ^{\prime }A\left( y-X%
\overline{\delta }_{n}\right) }{\left( y-X\overline{\delta }_{n}\right)
^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\overline{\delta }_{n}\right)
/n}\frac{\left( y-X\overline{\delta }_{n}\right) ^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }XD_{\mu }^{-1}}{n}\right] \\
&=&O_{p}\left( \frac{1}{\mu _{n}^{\min }}\right) \left[ o_{p}\left( \mu
_{n}^{\min }\right) -o_{p}\left( \left[ \mu _{n}^{\min }\right] ^{2}\right)
O_{p}\left( \frac{1}{\mu _{n}^{\min }}\right) \right] =o_{p}\left( 1\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
so that%
\begin{equation*}
-D_{\mu }^{-1}\left( \frac{\partial \widehat{\Delta }\left( \overline{\delta 
}_{n}\right) }{\partial \delta ^{\prime }}\right) D_{\mu }^{-1}=\frac{%
\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }Z_{2}\Upsilon }{n%
}+o_{p}\left( 1\right) =H_{n}+o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{. }\square
\end{equation*}

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma S2-11: }Let $\widehat{\ell }_{L}=Q\left( \widetilde{%
\beta }\right) =\min_{\beta \in \overline{B}}Q\left( \beta \right) $, where $%
Q\left( \beta \right) $ is as defined in Assumption 9. Then, $\widehat{\ell }%
_{L}$ is also the smallest root of the determinantal equation $\det \left[ 
\overline{X}^{\prime }A\overline{X}-\ell \overline{X}^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\overline{X}\right] =0$, where $\overline{X}=\left[ y,X%
\right] $. Assume in addition that condition (13) in Assumption 9 is
satisfied; then, $\widehat{\ell }_{L}$ has the representation 
\begin{equation}
\widehat{\ell }_{L}=\frac{\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }_{L}\right) ^{\prime
}A\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }_{L}\right) }{\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }%
_{L}\right) ^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }%
_{L}\right) }\text{,}  \label{FELIM root}
\end{equation}%
where $\widehat{\delta }_{L}$ denotes the FELIM\ estimator. Moreover, $%
\overline{X}^{\prime }A\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }_{L}\right) -\widehat{\ell 
}_{L}\overline{X}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\widehat{%
\delta }_{L}\right) $

\noindent $=0$. In particular, this implies that $\widehat{\Delta }\left( 
\widehat{\delta }_{L}\right) =0$, where

\noindent $\widehat{\Delta }\left( \delta \right) =-\left[ \left( y-X\delta
\right) ^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta \right) /2%
\right] \left( \partial \widehat{Q}_{FELIM}\left( \delta \right) /\partial
\delta \right) $, so that $\widehat{\delta }_{L}$ satisfies the set of
(normalized) first-order conditions for minimizing the variance ratio
objective function $\widehat{Q}_{FELIM}\left( \delta \right) =\left(
y-X\delta \right) ^{\prime }A\left( y-X\delta \right) /\left[ \left(
y-X\delta \right) ^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta
\right) \right] $.

\bigskip

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma S2-11:}

Note that the first-order condition for minimizing the objective function $%
Q\left( \beta \right) $ can be written as $\partial Q\left( \widetilde{\beta 
}\right) /\partial \beta =2\overline{X}^{\prime }A\overline{X}\widetilde{%
\beta }/\left( \widetilde{\beta }^{\prime }\overline{X}^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\overline{X}\widetilde{\beta }\right) $

\noindent $-\widetilde{\beta }^{\prime }\overline{X}^{\prime }A\overline{X}%
\widetilde{\beta }\left( 2\overline{X}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }%
\overline{X}\widetilde{\beta }\right) /\left[ \widetilde{\beta }^{\prime }%
\overline{X}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\overline{X}\widetilde{\beta 
}\right] ^{2}=0$. Pre-multiplying this first order condition by the factor $%
\frac{1}{2}\widetilde{\beta }^{\prime }\overline{X}^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\overline{X}\widetilde{\beta }$, we then obtain%
\begin{equation}
0=\left[ \overline{X}^{\prime }A\overline{X}-\widehat{\ell }_{L}\overline{X}%
^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\overline{X}\right] \widetilde{\beta }
\label{normalized FOC}
\end{equation}%
where we have set $\widehat{\ell }_{L}=Q\left( \widetilde{\beta }\right) =%
\widetilde{\beta }^{\prime }\overline{X}^{\prime }A\overline{X}\widetilde{%
\beta }/\widetilde{\beta }^{\prime }\overline{X}^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\overline{X}\widetilde{\beta }$. It is clear that in order
for there to be a nontrivial solution, i.e., $\widetilde{\beta }\neq 0$ such
that equation (\ref{normalized FOC}) is true, $\widehat{\ell }_{L}$ must be
a root of the determinantal equation $\det \left[ \overline{X}^{\prime }A%
\overline{X}-\ell \overline{X}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\overline{X%
}\right] =0.$ Moreover, since our goal is to minimize the value of the
objective function $Q\left( \beta \right) $, this implies that we should
choose $\widehat{\ell }_{L}$ to be the smallest root of this determinantal
equation. Now, define $\widetilde{\delta }=-\widetilde{\beta }_{2}/%
\widetilde{\beta }_{1}$, and rewrite the first-order conditions given by
expression (\ref{normalized FOC}) as $0=\overline{X}^{\prime }A\overline{X}%
\widetilde{\beta }-\widehat{\ell }_{L}\overline{X}^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\overline{X}\widetilde{\beta }=\widetilde{\beta }_{1}\left\{ 
\overline{X}^{\prime }A\left( y-X\widetilde{\delta }\right) -\widehat{\ell }%
_{L}\overline{X}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\widetilde{%
\delta }\right) \right\} $, so that, given the condition that $\left\vert 
\widetilde{\beta }_{1}\right\vert \geq \underline{C}>0$ \ $a.s.n.$ for some
constant $\underline{C}$ (as stated in Assumption 9), we must have 
\begin{equation}
\overline{X}^{\prime }A\left( y-X\widetilde{\delta }\right) -\widehat{\ell }%
_{L}\overline{X}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\widetilde{%
\delta }\right) =0  \label{FOC2}
\end{equation}%
Since $\overline{X}=\left[ y,X\right] $, we can partition (\ref{FOC2}) into
two sets of equations%
\begin{eqnarray}
0 &=&y^{\prime }A\left( y-X\widetilde{\delta }\right) -\widehat{\ell }%
_{L}y^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\widetilde{\delta }%
\right) ,  \label{FOC2_1} \\
0 &=&X^{\prime }A\left( y-X\widetilde{\delta }\right) -\widehat{\ell }%
_{L}X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\widetilde{\delta }%
\right) \text{.}  \label{FOC2_2}
\end{eqnarray}%
Solving (\ref{FOC2_2}) for $\widetilde{\delta }$, we obtain $\widetilde{%
\delta }=\left( X^{\prime }\left[ A-\widehat{\ell }_{L}M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\right] X\right) ^{-1}X^{\prime }\left[ A-\widehat{\ell }%
_{L}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\right] y=\widehat{\delta }_{L}$, so that the
FELIM estimator $\widehat{\delta }_{L}$ is a solution to the second set of
equations given by (\ref{FOC2_2}). In addition , note that, under condition
(13) in Assumption 9, we have%
\begin{equation*}
\widehat{\ell }_{L}=\frac{\widetilde{\beta }^{\prime }\overline{X}^{\prime }A%
\overline{X}\widetilde{\beta }}{\widetilde{\beta }^{\prime }\overline{X}%
^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\overline{X}\widetilde{\beta }}=\frac{%
\widetilde{\beta }_{1}\left( y-X\widetilde{\delta }\right) ^{\prime }A\left(
y-X\widetilde{\delta }\right) \widetilde{\beta }_{1}}{\widetilde{\beta }%
_{1}\left( y-X\widetilde{\delta }\right) M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X%
\widehat{\delta }\right) \widetilde{\beta }_{1}}=\frac{\left( y-X\widehat{%
\delta }_{L}\right) ^{\prime }A\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }_{L}\right) }{%
\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }_{L}\right) ^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }_{L}\right) }\text{.}
\end{equation*}%
which shows (\ref{FELIM root}). Furthermore, note that $\widehat{\delta }%
_{L} $ also satisfies equation (\ref{FOC2_1}) since%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&y^{\prime }A\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }_{L}\right) -\widehat{\ell }%
_{L}y^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }%
_{L}\right) \\
&=&\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }_{L}\right) ^{\prime }\left[ A-\widehat{\ell }%
_{L}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\right] \left( y-X\widehat{\delta }_{L}\right)
+\widehat{\delta }_{L}^{\prime }X^{\prime }\left[ A-\widehat{\ell }%
_{L}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\right] \left( y-X\widehat{\delta }_{L}\right)
\\
&=&\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }_{L}\right) ^{\prime }A\left( y-X\widehat{%
\delta }_{L}\right) -\frac{\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }_{L}\right) ^{\prime
}A\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }_{L}\right) \left( y-X\widehat{\delta }%
_{L}\right) ^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }%
_{L}\right) }{\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }_{L}\right) M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }_{L}\right) } \\
&&+\widehat{\delta }_{L}^{\prime }X^{\prime }\left[ A-\widehat{\ell }%
_{L}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\right] y \\
&&-\widehat{\delta }_{L}^{\prime }X^{\prime }\left[ A-\widehat{\ell }%
_{L}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\right] X\left( X^{\prime }\left[ A-\widehat{%
\ell }_{L}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\right] X\right) ^{-1}X^{\prime }\left[
A-\widehat{\ell }_{L}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\right] y \\
&=&0
\end{eqnarray*}%
from which we further deduce that $\widehat{\delta }_{L}$ is a solution of
the complete set of first-order conditions given by (\ref{FOC2}). Finally,
since $\widehat{\Delta }\left( \widehat{\delta }_{L}\right) =X^{\prime
}A\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }_{L}\right) -\widehat{\ell }_{L}X^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }_{L}\right) $, the
fact that $\widehat{\delta }_{L}$ is a solution of (\ref{FOC2_2}) directly
imply that $\widehat{\delta }_{L}$ satisfies the set of (normalized)
first-order conditions for minimizing the variance ratio objective function. 
$\square $

\bigskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma S2-12: }If Assumptions 1-6 are satisfied; then,

\noindent $D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }\left[ A-\widehat{\ell }_{F,n}M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\right] XD_{\mu }^{-1}=H_{n}+o_{p}\left( 1\right) $, where $%
H_{n}=\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}Z_{2}\Upsilon /n$,

\noindent $\widehat{\ell }_{F,n}=\left[ \widehat{\ell }_{L,n}-\left( 1-%
\widehat{\ell }_{L,n}\right) \left( C/m_{n}\right) \right] /\left[ 1-\left(
1-\widehat{\ell }_{L,n}\right) \left( C/m_{n}\right) \right] $, and $%
\widehat{\ell }_{L,n}$ is smallest root of the determinantal equation $\det
\left\{ \overline{X}^{\prime }A\overline{X}-\ell \overline{X}^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\overline{X}\right\} =0$, with $\overline{X}=%
\left[ 
\begin{array}{cc}
y & X%
\end{array}%
\right] $.

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma S2-12: }The result follows directly from
applying part (b) of Lemma S2-7, parts (a) and (b) of Lemma S2-2, and the
Slutsky theorem. $\square $

\bigskip

\noindent \noindent \textbf{Lemma S2-13: }If Assumptions 1-6 and 8-9 are
satisfied; then,

\noindent $D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }\left[ A-\widehat{\ell }_{F,n}M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\right] \left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) =\mathcal{Y}_{n}\left[
1+o_{p}\left( 1\right) \right] $, where $\mathcal{Y}_{n}=\Upsilon ^{\prime
}Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon /\sqrt{n}+D_{\mu }^{-1}%
\underline{U}^{\prime }A\varepsilon $ with $\underline{U}=U-\varepsilon \rho
^{\prime }$ and $\rho =\lim_{n\rightarrow \infty }E\left[ U^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right] /E\left[ \varepsilon ^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon %
\right] $.

\bigskip

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma S2-13:}

Note that, by Lemma S2-11 above, $\widehat{\ell }_{L,n}$ has the
representation%
\begin{equation*}
\widehat{\ell }_{L,n}=\frac{\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }_{L,n}\right)
^{\prime }A\left( y-X\widehat{\delta }_{L,n}\right) }{\left( y-X\widehat{%
\delta }_{L,n}\right) ^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\widehat{%
\delta }_{L,n}\right) }\text{.}
\end{equation*}%
Next, from expression (\ref{asy equiv of F and L}), we have $\widehat{\ell }%
_{F,n}=\widehat{\ell }_{L,n}+O_{p}\left( n^{-1}\right) $. It then follows,
by tedious but straightforward calculations\footnote{%
Further details are available from the authors upon request.} and by making
use of Assumptions 1, 2(i), 3-6, and 8 that 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }\left[ A-\widehat{\ell }_{F,n}M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\right] \left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) \\
&=&D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }A\left( y-X\delta _{0}\right) -\widehat{\ell }%
_{L,n}D_{\mu }^{-1}X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\left( y-X\delta
_{0}\right) +O_{p}\left( \frac{1}{n}\right) O_{p}\left( \frac{n}{\mu
_{n}^{\min }}\right) \\
&=&\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}+D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }A\varepsilon -\frac{%
\varepsilon ^{\prime }A\varepsilon }{\varepsilon ^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon }%
\left[ 1+o_{p}\left( 1\right) \right] \left[ \frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime
}Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}+D_{\mu
}^{-1}U^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon \right] \\
&&+O_{p}\left( \frac{1}{\mu _{n}^{\min }}\right) \\
&=&\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}+D_{\mu }^{-1}\left( U-\varepsilon \rho ^{\prime
}\right) ^{\prime }A\varepsilon \left[ 1+o_{p}\left( 1\right) \right]
-\varepsilon ^{\prime }A\varepsilon D_{\mu }^{-1}\left[ \frac{U^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon }{\varepsilon ^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon }-\rho \right] \left[ 1+o_{p}\left( 1\right) \right] \\
&&-\frac{\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{n}\frac{\varepsilon ^{\prime }A\varepsilon /\sqrt{%
K_{2,n}}}{\varepsilon ^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon /n}\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime
}Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}\left[
1+o_{p}\left( 1\right) \right] +O_{p}\left( \frac{1}{\mu _{n}^{\min }}\right)
\\
&=&\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}+D_{\mu }^{-1}\left( U-\varepsilon \rho ^{\prime
}\right) ^{\prime }A\varepsilon \left[ 1+o_{p}\left( 1\right) \right]
+O_{p}\left( \frac{1}{\mu _{n}^{\min }}\max \left\{ \sqrt{\frac{K_{2,n}}{n}},%
\frac{K_{1,n}\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{n}\right\} \right) \\
&&+O_{p}\left( \frac{\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{n}\right) +O_{p}\left( \frac{1}{\mu
_{n}^{\min }}\right) \\
&=&\left( \frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}\varepsilon }{\sqrt{n}}+D_{\mu }^{-1}\underline{U}^{\prime }A\varepsilon
\right) \left[ 1+o_{p}\left( 1\right) \right] \text{, where }\underline{U}%
=U-\varepsilon \rho ^{\prime }\text{. }\square
\end{eqnarray*}

\bigskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma S2-14: }For any $a\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$ such that $%
\left\Vert a\right\Vert =1$, define $b_{1n}=\Sigma _{n}^{-1/2}a$, $b_{2n}=%
\sqrt{K_{2,n}}D_{\mu }^{-1}\Sigma _{n}^{-1/2}a$, $\underline{u}_{2,\left(
i,t\right) ,n}=b_{2n}^{\prime }\underline{U}_{\left( i,t\right) }$

\noindent $=\sqrt{K_{2,n}}a^{\prime }\Sigma _{n}^{-1/2}D_{\mu }^{-1}%
\underline{U}_{\left( i,t\right) }$, $\sigma _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}=E%
\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] $, $%
\widetilde{\psi }_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}=E\left[ \underline{u}_{2,\left(
i,t\right) ,n}\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] $%
, and $\widetilde{\omega }_{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}=E\left[ \underline{u}%
_{2,\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] $. If Assumptions
1-2 and 5-6 are satisfied; then, the following statements are true.

\noindent (a) $\dsum\nolimits_{\left( i,t\right)
=2}^{m_{n}}\dsum\nolimits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{\left( i,t\right) -1}\left[
b_{1n}^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}e_{\left( i,t\right) }/\sqrt{n}\right] \left( A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }/\sqrt{K_{2,n}}\right) \left\{ \varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) }%
\widetilde{\psi }_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}+\underline{u}_{2,\left( j,s\right)
}\sigma _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}\right\} =O_{p}\left( K_{2,n}^{1/4}/\mu
_{n}^{\min }\right) =o_{p}\left( 1\right) $.

\noindent (b) $\dsum\nolimits_{\left( i,t\right)
=2}^{m_{n}}\dsum\nolimits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{\left( i,t\right)
-1}\left( A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}/K_{2,n}\right)
\left( \varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) }^{2}-\sigma _{\left( j,s\right)
,n}^{2}\right) \widetilde{\omega }_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}=O_{p}\left(
K_{2,n}\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{-2}n^{-1/2}\right) =o_{p}\left(
1\right) $.

\noindent (c) $\dsum\nolimits_{\left( i,t\right)
=2}^{m_{n}}\dsum\nolimits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{\left( i,t\right)
-1}\left( A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}/K_{2,n}\right)
\left( \underline{u}_{2,\left( j,s\right) ,n}^{2}-\widetilde{\omega }%
_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}^{2}\right) \sigma _{\left( i,t\right)
,n}^{2}=O_{p}\left( K_{2,n}\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right)
^{-2}n^{-1/2}\right) =o_{p}\left( 1\right) $.

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma S2-14:}

To show part (a), first let $\mathfrak{W}_{n}=\dsum\nolimits_{\left(
i,t\right) =2}^{m_{n}}\dsum\nolimits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{\left(
i,t\right) -1}\left[ b_{1n}^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }e_{\left( i,t\right) }/\sqrt{n}\right] \left(
A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }/\sqrt{K_{2,n}}\right) $

\noindent $\times \left\{ \varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) }\widetilde{\psi }%
_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}+\underline{u}_{2,\left( j,s\right) ,n}\sigma
_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}\right\} $. By taking expectation and applying
the triangle inequality, we obtain $E\left[ \mathfrak{W}_{n}^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] \leq \mathcal{H}_{1}+\mathcal{H}_{2}+\mathcal{H}_{3}+%
\mathcal{H}_{4}$, where $\mathcal{H}_{1}=\dsum\nolimits_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( k,\upsilon \right) =2}^{m_{n}}\left\vert n^{-1}\left[ b_{1n}^{\prime
}\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }e_{\left(
i,t\right) }\right] \right. $

\noindent $\left. \times \left[ b_{1n}^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime
}Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }e_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) }%
\right] \widetilde{\psi }_{\left( i,t\right) ,n}\widetilde{\psi }_{\left(
k,\upsilon \right) ,n}\dsum\nolimits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{\min \left\{
\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) \right\} -1}\left( A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }\sigma _{\left( j,s\right) ,n}^{2}/K_{2,n}\right) \right\vert $,

\noindent $\mathcal{H}_{2}=\dsum\nolimits_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) =2}^{m_{n}}\left\vert \left( \left[ b_{1n}^{\prime
}\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }e_{\left(
i,t\right) }\right] \left[ b_{1n}^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }e_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\right] /n\right)
\sigma _{\left( i,t\right) ,n}^{2}\widetilde{\psi }_{\left( k,\upsilon
\right) ,n}\right. $

\noindent $\left. \times \dsum\nolimits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{\min \left\{
\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) \right\} -1}\left( A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }\widetilde{\psi }_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}/K_{2,n}\right)
\right\vert $, $\mathcal{H}_{3}=\dsum\nolimits_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) =2}^{m_{n}}\left\vert n^{-1}\left[ b_{1n}^{\prime
}\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }e_{\left(
i,t\right) }\right] \right. $

\noindent $\left. \times \left[ b_{1n}^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime
}Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }e_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) }%
\right] \sigma _{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,n}^{2}\widetilde{\psi }_{\left(
i,t\right) ,n}\dsum\nolimits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{\min \left\{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) \right\} -1}\left( A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }\widetilde{\psi }_{\left( j,s\right) ,n}/K_{2,n}\right)
\right\vert $,

\noindent $\mathcal{H}_{4}=\dsum\nolimits_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
