Z_{1},Q\right) }D_{\sigma ^{2}}\left[ P^{\perp }-M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }%
\right] Z_{2}\Upsilon }{n} \\
&&+\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }\left[ P^{\perp }-M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\right] D_{\sigma ^{2}}\left[ P^{\perp }-M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\right] Z_{2}\Upsilon }{n} \\
&=&0\text{.}
\end{eqnarray*}%
where the last equality follows from the fact that 
\begin{eqnarray*}
\left[ P^{\perp }-M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\right] Z_{2} &=&\left[
P^{\left( Z,Q\right) }-P^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }-\left( I_{m_{n}}-P^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }\right) \right] Z_{2} \\
&=&-M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }Z_{2} \\
&=&0\text{.}
\end{eqnarray*}%
It follows from expression (\ref{Cov Mat1 approx 1}) that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }AD\left( \varepsilon \circ
\varepsilon \right) AZ_{2}\Upsilon }{n}-\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime
}Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }D_{\sigma ^{2}}M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }Z_{2}\Upsilon }{n} \\
&=&\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }P^{\perp }D_{\sigma ^{2}}P^{\perp
}Z_{2}\Upsilon }{n}-\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z_{1},Q\right) }D_{\sigma ^{2}}M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }Z_{2}\Upsilon }{n}%
+O_{p}\left( \sqrt{\frac{K_{2,n}}{n}}\right) \\
&=&O_{p}\left( \sqrt{\frac{K_{2,n}}{n}}\right) =o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{,}
\end{eqnarray*}%
as required. $\square $

\bigskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma OA-9:}

Suppose that Assumptions 1-6 are satisfied. Then,

\begin{enumerate}
\item[(a)] 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }AD\left( \varepsilon \circ \varepsilon \right)
AUD_{\mu }^{-1} \\
&&-\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] D_{\mu }^{-1}E\left[ U_{\left( j,s\right)
}U_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] D_{\mu }^{-1} \\
&=&O_{p}\left( \frac{\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}%
\right) =o_{p}\left( 1\right)
\end{eqnarray*}

\item[(b)] 
\begin{equation*}
\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }AD\left( \varepsilon \circ
\varepsilon \right) AUD_{\mu }^{-1}}{\sqrt{n}}=o_{p}\left( 1\right)
\end{equation*}
\end{enumerate}

\bigskip

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma OA-9:}

To show part (a), let $a,b\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$ such that $\left\Vert
a\right\Vert _{2}=\left\Vert b\right\Vert _{2}=1$, and define $u_{a,\left(
i,t\right) }=a^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U_{\left( i,t\right) }$ and $%
u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }=b^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U_{\left( j,s\right) }$.
Note that 
\begin{eqnarray}
&&a^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }AD\left( \varepsilon \circ \varepsilon
\right) AUD_{\mu }^{-1}b  \notag \\
&&-\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] a^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}E\left[ U_{\left(
j,s\right) }U_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
D_{\mu }^{-1}b  \notag \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left( j,s\right)
,\left( k,v\right) \right\} }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right)
}^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }  \notag \\
&&-\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left(
j,s\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]  \notag \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left( \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right)
}^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }-E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ u_{a,\left(
j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) 
\notag \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) =1  \\ %
\left( j,s\right) \neq \left( k,v\right) }}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left(
i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) \right\}
}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
k,v\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right)
}u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }  \label{UADAU term}
\end{eqnarray}

Focusing on the first term in expression (\ref{UADAU term}) above, we apply
the CS inequality, parts (b) and (c) of Lemma S2-1, and Assumptions 2(i) and
3(ii) to obtain%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left( \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }-E%
\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E%
\left[ u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \right) \right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{4}E\left\{ \left( \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right)
}^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }-E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ u_{a,\left(
j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right\} \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{4}\left\{ E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}u_{a,\left( i,t\right)
}u_{b,\left( i,t\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right. \\
&&\left. -E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] E\left[ u_{a,\left( i,t\right) }u_{b,\left( i,t\right) }|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right\} \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( k,v\right) }}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left(
j,s\right) \neq \left\{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) \right\}
}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left( k,v\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&&\times \left\{ E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( k,v\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}u_{b,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right. \\
&&\left. -E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( k,v\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \left( E\left[ u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2}\right\} \\
&&+2\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) =1  \\ %
\left( j,s\right) \neq \left( k,v\right) }}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left(
i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) \right\}
}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left( k,v\right) ,\left(
i,t\right) }^{2} \\
&&\text{ \ }\times \left\{ E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right)
}^{2}u_{a,\left( i,t\right) }u_{b,\left( i,t\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( k,v\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] E\left[ u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] \right. \\
&&\left. -E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( k,v\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] E\left[ u_{a,\left( i,t\right) }u_{b,\left( i,t\right) }|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right\} \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( k,v\right) }}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left(
j,s\right) \neq \left\{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) \right\}
}\left\{ A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( k,v\right) }^{2}\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ }\times \left( E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right)
}^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left(
j,s\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ u_{a,\left( k,v\right)
}u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ }\left. \left. -\left( E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2}E\left[ u_{a,\left(
j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[
u_{a,\left( k,v\right) }u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\right) \right\} \\
&\leq &2\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert U_{\left(
i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \frac{1}{%
\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}}\left\{ 2\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{4}\right. \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( k,v\right) ,  \\ \left(
j,s\right) \neq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \neq \left( k,v\right) 
}}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left( k,v\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}+2\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
k,v\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( j,s\right) \neq \left(
k,v\right) ,  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) ,\left( i,t\right)
\neq \left( k,v\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}A_{\left( k,v\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{2}
\end{eqnarray*}%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\left. +\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right)
,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( k,v\right) ,  \\ %
\left( j,s\right) \neq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \neq \left(
k,v\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }^{2}\right\} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{3}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}n^{2}%
}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right)
^{4}n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min
}\right) ^{4}n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{\left( \mu
_{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}n}\right) \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}n}%
\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
Hence, there exists a constant $\overline{C}<\infty $ such that for all $n$
sufficiently large 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \frac{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}n}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\left(
\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left(
i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2}\left( \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}u_{a,\left(
j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }-E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right)
}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left(
j,s\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \right) ^{2}\right] \\
&=&\frac{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}n}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\times \\
&&E_{Z}\left( E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left( \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }-E%
\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E%
\left[ u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \right) \right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \\
&\leq &\overline{C}\text{. \ }
\end{eqnarray*}%
It follows from the Markov's inequality that for any $\epsilon >0$, 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\Pr \left( \frac{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}\sqrt{n}}{K_{2,n}}%
\left\vert \dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1 
\\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left( \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right)
}^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }-E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ u_{a,\left(
j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right)
\right\vert \geq \sqrt{\frac{\overline{C}}{\epsilon }}\right) \\
&=&\Pr \left\{ \frac{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}n}{K_{2,n}^{2}}%
\left( \dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left( \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right)
}^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }-E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ u_{a,\left(
j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right)
\right) ^{2}\geq \frac{\overline{C}}{\epsilon }\right\} \\
&\leq &\epsilon \frac{E\left[ \frac{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}n}{%
K_{2,n}^{2}}\left( \dsum\nolimits_{\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right)
}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }-E\left[
\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[
u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\right\} \right) ^{2}\right] }{\overline{C}} \\
&\leq &\epsilon
\end{eqnarray*}%
for all $n$ sufficiently large, which shows that%
\begin{eqnarray}
&&\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left( \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right)
}^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }-E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ u_{a,\left(
j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) 
\notag \\
&=&O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}\sqrt{n}}%
\right) .  \label{UADAU1}
\end{eqnarray}

Turning our attention to the second term in expression (\ref{UADAU term}),
we first define $\varsigma _{\left( i,t\right) }=\varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}-E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] $. Note that by the decoupling inequality given in Lemma
OA-7, there exist finite constants $C_{2}$ and $C_{3}$, whose explicit forms
are given in Lemma OA-7, and independent copies $\left\{ \left( u_{a,\left(
i,t\right) }^{\left( g\right) },u_{b,\left( i,t\right) }^{\left( g\right)
},\varsigma _{\left( i,t\right) }^{\left( g\right) }\right) \right\}
_{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}$ (for $g=1,2,3$) of the sequence $\left\{
\left( u_{a,\left( i,t\right) },u_{b,\left( i,t\right) },\varsigma _{\left(
i,t\right) }\right) \right\} _{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}$ such that%
\begin{eqnarray}
&&E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,v\right) =1  \\ \left( j,s\right) \neq \left( k,v\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left( j,s\right)
,\left( k,v\right) \right\} }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right)
}^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right]  \notag \\
&\leq &2E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,v\right) =1  \\ \left( j,s\right) \neq \left( k,v\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left( j,s\right)
,\left( k,v\right) \right\} }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] u_{a,\left( j,s\right)
}u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]  \notag \\
&&+2E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,v\right) =1  \\ \left( j,s\right) \neq \left( k,v\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left( j,s\right)
,\left( k,v\right) \right\} }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }u_{a,\left( j,s\right)
}u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}-E\left[
\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right]
\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]  \notag \\
&\leq &2C_{2}E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( j,s\right)
,\left( k,v\right) =1  \\ \left( j,s\right) \neq \left( k,v\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left( j,s\right)
,\left( k,v\right) \right\} }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }^{\left(
1\right) }u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }^{\left( 2\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right]  \notag \\
&&+2C_{3}E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,v\right) =1  \\ \left( j,s\right) \neq \left( k,v\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left( j,s\right)
,\left( k,v\right) \right\} }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }^{\left(
1\right) }u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }^{\left( 2\right) }\varsigma _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{\left( 3\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] 
\notag \\
&=&2C_{2}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) =1 
\\ \left( j,s\right) \neq \left( k,v\right) }}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left(
i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) \right\}
}\dsum\limits_{\left( \ell ,h\right) \neq \left\{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) \right\} }\left\{ A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }A_{\left( \ell
,h\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( \ell ,h\right) ,\left( k,v\right)
}\right.  \notag \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \times E\left[
\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[
\varepsilon _{\left( \ell ,h\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[
\left( u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }^{\left( 1\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ \left( u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }^{\left( 2\right)
}\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right\}  \notag \\
&&+2C_{2}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right)
,\left( i,t\right) =1  \\ \left( j,s\right) \neq \left( k,v\right)  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) \right\} 
}}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( k,v\right) }^{2}\left( E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2}E\left[ \left( u_{a,\left( j,s\right)
}^{\left( 1\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ \left(
u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }^{\left( 2\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right]  \notag \\
&&+2C_{3}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right)
,\left( i,t\right) =1  \\ \left( j,s\right) \neq \left( k,v\right)  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) \right\} 
}}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( k,v\right) }^{2}\left\{ E\left[ \left( u_{a,\left( j,s\right)
}^{\left( 1\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ \left(
u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }^{\left( 2\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \right.  \notag \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left.
\times E\left[ \left( \varsigma _{\left( i,t\right) }^{\left( 3\right)
}\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right\}  \label{UADAU2}
\end{eqnarray}%
Define $D_{\sigma ^{2}}=diag\left( \sigma _{\left( 1,2\right)
}^{2},....,\sigma _{\left( n,T_{n}\right) }^{2}\right) $ where $\sigma
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}=E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] $ for $\left( i,t\right) =1,...,m_{n}$. By
applying Assumptions 2(i), 3(ii), and 5 as well as parts (a) and (b) of
Lemma OA-1, we can estimate the (almost sure) order of magnitude of the
first term on the right-hand side of (\ref{UADAU2}) as follows%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) =1  \\ %
\left( j,s\right) \neq \left( k,v\right) }}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left(
i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) \right\}
}\dsum\limits_{\left( \ell ,h\right) \neq \left\{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) \right\} }\left\{ A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }A_{\left( \ell
,h\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( \ell ,h\right) ,\left( k,v\right)
}\right. \\
&&\text{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \times E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( \ell ,h\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ \left(
u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }^{\left( 1\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] E\left[ \left( u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }^{\left( 2\right) }\right)
^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right\} \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}E\left[ \left( u_{a,\left(
j,s\right) }^{\left( 1\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( k,v\right) =1  \\ \left( k,v\right) \neq
\left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}e_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime
}A\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,v\right) \right\} }e_{\left( i,t\right) }E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime
}Ae_{\left( k,v\right) } \\
&&\times E\left[ \left( u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }^{\left( 2\right) }\right)
^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] e_{\left( k,v\right) }^{\prime
}\dsum\limits_{\left( \ell ,h\right) \neq \left\{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) \right\} }Ae_{\left( \ell ,h\right) }E\left[
\varepsilon _{\left( \ell ,h\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
e_{\left( \ell ,h\right) }^{\prime }Ae_{\left( j,s\right) } \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}E\left[ \left( u_{a,\left(
j,s\right) }^{\left( 1\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( k,v\right) =1  \\ \left( k,v\right) \neq
\left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}e_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime
}A\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,v\right) \right\} }e_{\left( i,t\right) }E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime
}Ae_{\left( k,v\right) } \\
&&\times E\left[ \left( u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }^{\left( 2\right) }\right)
^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \left[ e_{\left( k,v\right) }^{\prime
}AD_{\sigma ^{2}}Ae_{\left( j,s\right) }-e_{\left( k,v\right) }^{\prime
}Ae_{\left( i,t\right) }E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }Ae_{\left(
j,s\right) }\right] \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}E\left[ \left( u_{a,\left(
j,s\right) }^{\left( 1\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( k,v\right) =1  \\ \left( k,v\right) \neq
\left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}E\left[ \left( u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }^{\left(
2\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \left[ e_{\left(
k,v\right) }^{\prime }AD_{\sigma ^{2}}Ae_{\left( j,s\right) }\right] ^{2} \\
&&-\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}E\left[ \left( u_{a,\left(
j,s\right) }^{\left( 1\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( k,v\right) ,\left( i,t\right) =1 
\\ \left( k,v\right) \neq \left( j,s\right)  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq
\left\{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) \right\} }}^{m_{n}}\left[
e_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime }Ae_{\left( i,t\right) }E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] e_{\left( i,t\right)
}^{\prime }Ae_{\left( k,v\right) }\right] ^{2}E\left[ \left( u_{b,\left(
k,v\right) }^{\left( 2\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}E\left[ \left( u_{a,\left(
j,s\right) }^{\left( 1\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\dsum\limits_{\left( k,v\right) =1}^{m_{n}}E\left[ \left( u_{b,\left(
k,v\right) }^{\left( 2\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
e_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime }AD_{\sigma ^{2}}Ae_{\left( k,v\right)
}e_{\left( k,v\right) }^{\prime }AD_{\sigma ^{2}}Ae_{\left( j,s\right) } \\
&\leq &\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert
U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\right) ^{2}\frac{1}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}}\dsum\limits_{%
\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}e_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime }AD_{\sigma
^{2}}A^{2}D_{\sigma ^{2}}Ae_{\left( j,s\right) }
\end{eqnarray*}%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&\leq &\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert
U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\right) ^{2}\left( 1+\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert 
\widehat{\vartheta }_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\right) \left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2} \\
&&\times \frac{1}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}}\dsum\limits_{\left(
j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}e_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime }A^{2}e_{\left(
j,s\right) } \\
&\leq &\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert
U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\right) ^{2}\left( 1+\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert 
\widehat{\vartheta }_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\right) \left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2} \\
&&\times \frac{1}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}}\left[ tr\left\{
P^{\perp }\right\} +tr\left\{ D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}^{2}\right\} \right] \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}}\right)
+O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}n}%
\right) =O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}}%
\right) .
\end{eqnarray*}%
By applying Assumptions 2(i) and 3(ii) as well as part (c) of Lemma S2-1, we
can also derive the (almost sure) order of magnitude for the second and the
third terms of (\ref{UADAU2}) as follows%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) =1  \\ \left( j,s\right) \neq \left(
k,v\right) ,\left( i,t\right)  \\ \left( k,v\right) \neq \left( i,t\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( k,v\right) }^{2}\left( E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2}E\left[ \left( u_{a,\left( j,s\right)
}^{\left( 1\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ \left(
u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }^{\left( 2\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \\
&\leq &\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert U_{\left(
i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2}%
\frac{1}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ %
\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) =1  \\ \left( j,s\right) \neq \left\{
\left( k,v\right) ,\left( i,t\right) \right\} ,\left( k,v\right) \neq \left(
i,t\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}n}%
\right) =o_{a.s.}\left( 1\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
and 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) =1  \\ \left( j,s\right) \neq \left(
k,v\right) ,\left( i,t\right)  \\ \left( k,v\right) \neq \left( i,t\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}\left\{ A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }^{2}E\left[ \left( u_{a,\left( j,s\right)
}^{\left( 1\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \times E\left[
\left( u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }^{\left( 2\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ \left( \varsigma _{\left( i,t\right) }^{\left(
3\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right\} \\
&\leq &\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert U_{\left(
i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2}%
\frac{1}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ %
\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) =1  \\ \left( j,s\right) \neq \left\{
\left( k,v\right) ,\left( i,t\right) \right\} ,\left( k,v\right) \neq \left(
i,t\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}n}%
\right) =o_{a.s.}\left( 1\right) \text{. }
\end{eqnarray*}%
These results imply that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) =1  \\ \left( j,s\right)
\neq \left\{ \left( k,v\right) ,\left( i,t\right) \right\} ,\left(
k,v\right) \neq \left( i,t\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }\varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }\right) ^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}}\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
Hence, there exists a constant $\overline{C}<\infty $ such that for all $n$
sufficiently large 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \frac{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}}{K_{2,n}}\left(
\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) =1  \\ \left( j,s\right) \neq \left\{ \left(
k,v\right) ,\left( i,t\right) \right\} ,\left( k,v\right) \neq \left(
i,t\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right)
}^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }\right) ^{2}\right] \\
&=&E_{Z}\left( E\left[ \frac{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}}{K_{2,n}}%
\left( \dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ %
\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) =1  \\ \left( j,s\right) \neq \left\{
\left( k,v\right) ,\left( i,t\right) \right\} ,\left( k,v\right) \neq \left(
i,t\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right)
}^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \\
&\leq &\overline{C}\text{. \ }
\end{eqnarray*}%
It follows from the Markov's inequality that for any $\epsilon >0$, 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\Pr \left( \frac{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}{\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}%
\left\vert \dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) =1  \\ \left( j,s\right)
\neq \left\{ \left( k,v\right) ,\left( i,t\right) \right\} ,\left(
k,v\right) \neq \left( i,t\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }\varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }\right\vert
\geq \sqrt{\frac{\overline{C}}{\epsilon }}\right) \\
&=&\Pr \left\{ \frac{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}}{K_{2,n}}\left(
\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) =1  \\ \left( j,s\right) \neq \left\{ \left(
k,v\right) ,\left( i,t\right) \right\} ,\left( k,v\right) \neq \left(
i,t\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right)
}^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }\right) ^{2}\geq \frac{%
\overline{C}}{\epsilon }\right\} \\
&\leq &\frac{\epsilon }{\overline{C}}E\left[ \frac{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min
}\right) ^{4}}{K_{2,n}}\left( \dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) =1 
\\ \left( j,s\right) \neq \left\{ \left( k,v\right) ,\left( i,t\right)
\right\} ,\left( k,v\right) \neq \left( i,t\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left(
k,v\right) }\right) ^{2}\right] \leq \epsilon
\end{eqnarray*}%
for all $n$ sufficiently large, which shows that 
\begin{equation}
\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) =1  \\ \left( j,s\right) \neq \left\{ \left(
k,v\right) ,\left( i,t\right) \right\} ,\left( k,v\right) \neq \left(
i,t\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right)
}^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }=O_{p}\left( \frac{%
\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}\right)  \label{UADAU2ab}
\end{equation}%
Now, (\ref{UADAU1}) and (\ref{UADAU2ab}) together imply that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&a^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }AD\left( \varepsilon \circ \varepsilon
\right) AUD_{\mu }^{-1}b \\
&&-\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] a^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}E\left[ U_{\left(
j,s\right) }U_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
D_{\mu }^{-1}b \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left( \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right)
}^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }-E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ u_{a,\left(
j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) =1  \\ %
\left( j,s\right) \neq \left( k,v\right) }}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left(
i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) \right\}
}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
k,v\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}u_{a,\left( j,s\right)
}u_{b,\left( k,v\right) } \\
&=&O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}\sqrt{n}}%
\right) +O_{p}\left( \frac{\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right)
^{2}}\right) \\
&=&O_{p}\left( \frac{\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}%
\right) .
\end{eqnarray*}%
Finally, since the above argument holds for all $a$, $b\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$
such that $\left\Vert a\right\Vert _{2}=\left\Vert b\right\Vert _{2}=1$, we
obtain the desired result%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }AD\left( \varepsilon \circ \varepsilon \right)
AUD_{\mu }^{-1}-\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] D_{\mu }^{-1}E\left[
U_{\left( j,s\right) }U_{\left( j,s\right) }^{\prime }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] D_{\mu }^{-1} \\
&=&O_{p}\left( \frac{\sqrt{K_{2,n}}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}%
\right) \text{. }
\end{eqnarray*}

To show part (b), again let $a$, $b\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$ such that $\left\Vert
a\right\Vert _{2}=\left\Vert b\right\Vert _{2}=1$ and define $u_{b,\left(
k,v\right) }=b^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U_{\left( k,v\right) }$ and $%
u_{b}=UD_{\mu }^{-1}b$. We can apply Lo\`{e}ve's $c_{r}$ inequality to obtain%
\begin{eqnarray}
&&E\left[ \left( \frac{a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }AD\left(
\varepsilon \circ \varepsilon \right) AUD_{\mu }^{-1}b}{\sqrt{n}}\right)
^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]  \notag \\
&=&\frac{1}{n}E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,v\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) \right\} }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }a^{\prime }\Upsilon
^{\prime }Z_{2,\left( j,s\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right)
}^{2}u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]  \notag
\\
&\leq &\frac{2}{n}E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,v\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) \right\} }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }a^{\prime }\Upsilon
^{\prime }Z_{2,\left( j,s\right) }E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right)
}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }\right) ^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]  \notag \\
&&+\frac{2}{n}E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,v\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) \right\} }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }a^{\prime }\Upsilon
^{\prime }Z_{2,\left( j,s\right) }\left\{ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right)
}^{2}-E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \right\} u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right]  \notag \\
&=&\frac{2}{n}E\left[ \left( a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime
}AD_{\sigma ^{2}}Au_{b}\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]  \notag \\
&&+\frac{2}{n}E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,v\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) \right\} }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }a^{\prime }\Upsilon
^{\prime }Z_{2,\left( j,s\right) }\varsigma _{\left( i,t\right) }u_{b,\left(
k,v\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]  \label{GADAU}
\end{eqnarray}%
where $\varsigma _{\left( i,t\right) }=\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right)
}^{2}-E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] $. Focusing on the first term of expression (\ref{GADAU}) above, we
can apply Assumptions 2(i), 3(ii), and 3(iii) as well as part (b) of Lemma
OA-1 to obtain 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\frac{2}{n}E\left[ \left( a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime
}AD_{\sigma ^{2}}Au_{b}\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\frac{2}{n}a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }AD_{\sigma ^{2}}AE%
\left[ u_{b}u_{b}^{\prime }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] AD_{\sigma
^{2}}AZ_{2}\Upsilon a \\
&\leq &\frac{1}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}\left( \max_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert U_{\left( i,t\right)
}\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \frac{a^{\prime
}\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }AD_{\sigma ^{2}}A^{2}D_{\sigma
^{2}}AZ_{2}\Upsilon a}{n} \\
&\leq &\frac{1}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}\left( \max_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert U_{\left( i,t\right)
}\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \left(
1+\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert \widehat{\vartheta }%
_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\right) ^{2} \\
&&\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2}\frac{%
a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }Z_{2}\Upsilon a}{n} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{1}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}\right)
=o_{a.s.}\left( 1\right) .
\end{eqnarray*}%
Turning our attention now to the second term of (\ref{GADAU}), note that we
can apply the inequality $\left\vert XY\right\vert \leq \left( 1/2\right)
X^{2}+\left( 1/2\right) Y^{2}$, Assumptions 1, 2(i), and 3(iii) as well as
part (c) of Lemma S2-1 to get 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\frac{2}{n}E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,v\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) \right\} }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }a^{\prime }\Upsilon
^{\prime }Z_{2,\left( j,s\right) }\varsigma _{\left( i,t\right) }u_{b,\left(
k,v\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &\frac{2}{n}\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) ,\left(
\ell ,h\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) \neq \left\{
\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) \right\}
}\left\vert A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }^{2}\right.
\\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \
\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \times a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime
}Z_{2,\left( j,s\right) }a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2,\left( \ell
,h\right) }E\left[ \varsigma _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] E\left[ u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\right\vert \\
&&+\frac{2}{n}\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) ,\left(
\ell ,h\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) \neq \left\{
\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) \right\}
}\left\vert A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( k,v\right) }A_{\left( k,v\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left(
k,v\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \
\ }\left. \times a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2,\left( j,s\right)
}a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2,\left( \ell ,h\right) }E\left[ \varsigma
_{\left( i,t\right) }u_{b,\left( i,t\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E%
\left[ \varsigma _{\left( k,v\right) }u_{b,\left( k,v\right) }|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] \right\vert \\
&\leq &\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2}\frac{%
a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }Z_{2}\Upsilon a}{n}\frac{1}{%
\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( k,v\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right)
=1  \\ \left( k,v\right) \neq \left( i,t\right)  \\ \left( \ell ,h\right)
\neq \left( i,t\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right)
}^{2}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }^{2} \\
&&+\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert
U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\right) ^{2}\frac{a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }Z_{2}\Upsilon
a}{n}\frac{1}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\left(
i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( k,v\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( k,v\right) \neq \left( i,t\right)  \\ \left(
j,s\right) \neq \left( i,t\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }^{2} \\
&&+\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert
U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\right) \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \frac{a^{\prime
}\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }Z_{2}\Upsilon a}{n\left( \mu _{n}^{\min
}\right) ^{2}} \\
&&\text{ \ \ }\times \dsum\limits_{\left( k,v\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) =1  \\ \left(
i,t\right) \neq \left( k,v\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) \neq \left(
k,v\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( k,v\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right)
}^{2}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }^{2} \\
&&+\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert
U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\right) \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \frac{a^{\prime
}\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }Z_{2}\Upsilon a}{n\left( \mu _{n}^{\min
}\right) ^{2}} \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ }\times \dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( k,v\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1 
\\ \left( k,v\right) \neq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \neq \left(
i,t\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left(
k,v\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}n}%
\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
It follows from these results that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \left( \frac{a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }AD\left(
\varepsilon \circ \varepsilon \right) AUD_{\mu }^{-1}b}{\sqrt{n}}\right)
^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &\frac{2}{n}E\left[ \left( a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime
}AD_{\sigma ^{2}}Au_{b}\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&&+\frac{2}{n}E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,v\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) \neq \left\{ \left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,v\right) \right\} }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,v\right) }a^{\prime }\gamma
_{\left( j,s\right) }\varsigma _{\left( i,t\right) }u_{b,\left( k,v\right)
}\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{1}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}\right)
+O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}n}%
\right) =o_{a.s.}\left( 1\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
Now, by the conditional version of the Markov's inequality, we deduce that,
for any $\epsilon >0$, 
\begin{equation*}
\Pr \left( \left\vert \frac{a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime
}AD\left( \varepsilon \circ \varepsilon \right) AUD_{\mu }^{-1}b}{\sqrt{n}}%
\right\vert \geq \epsilon \text{ }|\text{ }\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right)
\rightarrow 0\text{ \ }a.s.
\end{equation*}%
Since%
\begin{equation*}
\sup_{n}E\left[ \left\vert \Pr \left( \left\vert \frac{a^{\prime }\Upsilon
^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }AD\left( \varepsilon \circ \varepsilon \right)
AUD_{\mu }^{-1}b}{\sqrt{n}}\right\vert \geq \epsilon \text{ }|\text{ }%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \right\vert ^{2}\right] <\infty \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
it then follows by a version of the dominated convergence theorem, as given
by Theorem 25.12 of Billingsley (1986), that as $n\rightarrow \infty $%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\Pr \left( \left\vert \frac{a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime
}AD\left( \varepsilon \circ \varepsilon \right) AUD_{\mu }^{-1}b}{\sqrt{n}}%
\right\vert \geq \epsilon \right) \\
&=&E\left[ \Pr \left( \left\vert \frac{a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime
}Z_{2}^{\prime }AD\left( \varepsilon \circ \varepsilon \right) AUD_{\mu
}^{-1}b}{\sqrt{n}}\right\vert \geq \epsilon \text{ }|\text{ }\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) \right] \rightarrow 0,
\end{eqnarray*}%
Finally, since the above result holds for all $a,b\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$ such
that $\left\Vert a\right\Vert _{2}=\left\Vert b\right\Vert _{2}=1$, we
further deduce that 
\begin{equation*}
\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }AD\left( \varepsilon \circ
\varepsilon \right) AUD_{\mu }^{-1}}{\sqrt{n}}\overset{p}{\rightarrow }0%
\text{, as }n\rightarrow \infty
\end{equation*}%
as required for part (b). $\square $

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma OA-10:}

Under Assumptions 5 and 6, the following statements are true.

\begin{enumerate}
\item[(a)] 
\begin{eqnarray*}
tr\left\{ A^{4}\right\} &=&tr\left\{ \left( P^{\perp }-M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\right) ^{4}\right\} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( K_{2,n}\right) \text{.}
\end{eqnarray*}

\item[(b)] $\left\vert S_{n}\right\vert =O_{a.s.}\left( K_{2,n}\right) $,
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
S_{n} &=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) \leq m_{n}}\left( A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon
\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }+A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon
\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) } \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \text{\ }%
+A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right)
}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }\right)
\end{eqnarray*}

\item[(c)] $\left\vert \dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left(
j,s\right) <\left( k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) \leq
m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right)
}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }\right\vert =O_{a.s.}\left(
K_{2,n}\right) $.
\end{enumerate}

\bigskip

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma OA-10:}

To show part (a), note first that $P^{\perp }M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}=0=M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }P^{\perp }$. Now, write%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\left( P^{\perp }-M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }\right) ^{4} \\
&=&\left[ \left( P^{\perp }-M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }%
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\right) \left( P^{\perp }-M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{%
\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\right) \right] ^{2} \\
&=&\left( P^{\perp }+M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\right) ^{2} \\
&=&\left( P^{\perp }+M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\right) \left(
P^{\perp }+M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\right) \\
&=&P^{\perp }+M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{%
\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }
\end{eqnarray*}

\noindent Hence, 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&tr\left\{ \left( P^{\perp }-M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }%
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\right) ^{4}\right\} \\
&=&tr\left\{ P^{\perp }\right\} +tr\left\{ M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{%
\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{%
\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\right\} \\
&=&K_{2,n}+tr\left\{ M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{%
\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }\right\}
\end{eqnarray*}%
In addition, note that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
0 &\leq &tr\left\{ M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{%
\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }\right\} \\
&\leq &tr\left\{ M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}^{2}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{%
\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\right\} \\
&\leq &\left( \max_{\left( i,t\right) \in \Lambda _{1}}\left\vert \widehat{%
\vartheta }_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\right) tr\left\{ M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{%
\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\right\} \\
&\leq &\left( \max_{\left( i,t\right) \in \Lambda _{1}}\left\vert \widehat{%
\vartheta }_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\right) tr\left\{ M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}^{2}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\right\} \\
&=&\left( \max_{\left( i,t\right) \in \Lambda _{1}}\left\vert \widehat{%
\vartheta }_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\right) tr\left\{ D_{%
\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}\right\}
\\
&\leq &\left( \max_{\left( i,t\right) \in \Lambda _{1}}\left\vert \widehat{%
\vartheta }_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\right) tr\left\{ D_{%
\widehat{\vartheta }}^{2}\right\}
\end{eqnarray*}%
It follows from applying parts (a) and (b) of Lemma OA-1 that 
\begin{eqnarray*}
tr\left\{ A^{4}\right\} &=&tr\left\{ \left( P^{\perp }-M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\right) ^{4}\right\} \\
&=&K_{2,n}+tr\left\{ M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{%
\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }\right\} \\
&=&K_{2,n}+\left( \max_{\left( i,t\right) \in \Lambda _{1}}\left\vert 
\widehat{\vartheta }_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert ^{2}\right) tr\left\{
D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}^{2}\right\} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( K_{2,n}\right) \text{. }
\end{eqnarray*}

Next, to show part (b), decompose $A=P^{\perp }-M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{%
\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }$ as follows%
\begin{equation*}
A=L+L^{\prime }\text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where $L$ be the lower triangular matrix such that $L_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }=A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }\mathbb{I}%
\left\{ \left( i,t\right) >\left( j,s\right) \right\} $, i.e., $L$ is lower
triangular matrix whose lower triangular elements correspond to the lower
triangular elements of $A$. \ It follows that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&A^{4} \\
&=&\left( L+L^{\prime }\right) ^{4}=\left( L^{2}+LL^{\prime }+L^{\prime
}L+\left( L^{\prime }\right) ^{2}\right) ^{2} \\
&=&L^{4}+L^{3}L^{\prime }+L^{2}L^{\prime }L+L^{2}\left( L^{\prime }\right)
^{2}+LL^{\prime }L^{2}+LL^{\prime }LL^{\prime }+L\left( L^{\prime }\right)
^{2}L+L\left( L^{\prime }\right) ^{3} \\
&&+L^{\prime }L^{3}+L^{\prime }L^{2}L^{\prime }+L^{\prime }LL^{\prime
}L+L^{\prime }L\left( L^{\prime }\right) ^{2}+\left( L^{\prime }\right)
^{2}L^{2}+\left( L^{\prime }\right) ^{2}LL^{\prime }+\left( L^{\prime
}\right) ^{3}L+\left( L^{\prime }\right) ^{4}
\end{eqnarray*}%
Using the fact that $tr\left\{ AB\right\} =tr\left\{ BA\right\} $ and $%
tr\left\{ A\right\} =tr\left\{ A^{\prime }\right\} $, we obtain%
\begin{equation*}
tr\left\{ A^{4}\right\} =2tr\left\{ L^{4}\right\} +8tr\left\{ L^{3}L^{\prime
}\right\} +4tr\left\{ L^{2}\left( L^{\prime }\right) ^{2}\right\}
+2tr\left\{ LL^{\prime }LL^{\prime }\right\}
\end{equation*}%
We compute each of the terms on the right-hand side above as follows.%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&tr\left\{ L^{4}\right\} \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) }\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right)
}\dsum\limits_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\dsum\limits_{\left( \ell
,h\right) }\left[ A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }\mathbb{I}\left\{
\left( i,t\right) >\left( j,s\right) \right\} A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) }\mathbb{I}\left\{ \left( j,s\right) >\left( k,\upsilon
\right) \right\} \right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \times
A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }\mathbb{I}\left\{
\left( k,\upsilon \right) >\left( \ell ,h\right) \right\} A_{\left( \ell
,h\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }\mathbb{I}\left\{ \left( \ell ,h\right)
>\left( i,t\right) \right\} \right] \\
&=&0
\end{eqnarray*}%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&tr\left\{ L^{3}L^{\prime }\right\} \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) }\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right)
}\dsum\limits_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\dsum\limits_{\left( \ell
,h\right) }\left[ A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }\mathbb{I}\left\{
\left( i,t\right) >\left( j,s\right) \right\} A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) }\mathbb{I}\left\{ \left( j,s\right) >\left( k,\upsilon
\right) \right\} \right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \times
A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }\mathbb{I}\left\{
\left( k,\upsilon \right) >\left( \ell ,h\right) \right\} A_{\left( \ell
,h\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }\mathbb{I}\left\{ \left( i,t\right) >\left(
\ell ,h\right) \right\} \right] \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( \ell ,h\right) <\left( k,\upsilon \right)
<\left( j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( \ell
,h\right) ,\left( i,t\right) } \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( \ell
,h\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( \ell ,h\right) } \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}A_{\left( \ell ,h\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right)
,\left( \ell ,h\right) }\text{ (by symmetry of }A\text{)}
\end{eqnarray*}%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&tr\left\{ L^{2}\left( L^{\prime }\right) ^{2}\right\} \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) }\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right)
}\dsum\limits_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\dsum\limits_{\left( \ell
,h\right) }\left[ A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }\mathbb{I}\left\{
\left( i,t\right) >\left( j,s\right) \right\} A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) }\mathbb{I}\left\{ \left( j,s\right) >\left( k,\upsilon
\right) \right\} \right. \\
&&\text{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \times
A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }\mathbb{I}\left\{
\left( \ell ,h\right) >\left( k,\upsilon \right) \right\} A_{\left( \ell
,h\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }\mathbb{I}\left\{ \left( i,t\right) >\left(
\ell ,h\right) \right\} \right] \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right)
=\left( j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( \ell
,h\right) ,\left( i,t\right) } \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right)
<\left( j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( \ell
,h\right) ,\left( i,t\right) } \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( k,\upsilon \right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
\ell ,h\right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left(
k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( \ell ,h\right) ,\left(
i,t\right) } \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( k,\upsilon \right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( i,t\right) } \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right)
<\left( j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\left[ A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( \ell
,h\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 
}\left. +A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( \ell
,h\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }\right] \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2} \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) \leq m_{n}}\left[ A_{\left( \ell
,h\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left(
i,t\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( \ell ,h\right) }\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }%
\left. +A_{\left( \ell ,h\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( i,t\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }\right] \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2} \\
&&+2\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right)
,\left( \ell ,h\right) }
\end{eqnarray*}%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&tr\left\{ LL^{\prime }LL^{\prime }\right\} \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{\left( i,t\right) }\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right)
}\dsum\limits_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\dsum\limits_{\left( \ell
,h\right) }\left[ A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }\mathbb{I}\left\{
\left( i,t\right) >\left( j,s\right) \right\} A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) }\mathbb{I}\left\{ \left( k,\upsilon \right) >\left(
j,s\right) \right\} \right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \times
A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }\mathbb{I}\left\{
\left( k,\upsilon \right) >\left( \ell ,h\right) \right\} A_{\left( \ell
,h\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }\mathbb{I}\left\{ \left( i,t\right) >\left(
\ell ,h\right) \right\} \right] \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
i,t\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( i,t\right) } \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) <\left( k,\upsilon \right) <\left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( i,t\right) } \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) <\left( i,t\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon
\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( i,t\right) } \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) <\left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right)
}A_{\left( \ell ,h\right) ,\left( i,t\right) } \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( \ell ,h\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right)
}A_{\left( \ell ,h\right) ,\left( i,t\right) } \\
&&+\left( \dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( \ell ,h\right) <\left( j,s\right)
<\left( k,\upsilon \right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}+\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) <\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}\right) A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( \ell
,h\right) ,\left( i,t\right) } \\
&&+\left( \dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( \ell ,h\right) <\left( j,s\right)
<\left( i,t\right) <\left( k,\upsilon \right) \leq
m_{n}}+\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( j,s\right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) <\left(
i,t\right) <\left( k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}\right) A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( \ell
,h\right) ,\left( i,t\right) } \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) \leq
m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{4}+2\dsum\limits_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left( k,\upsilon \right) \leq
m_{n}}\left( A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}+A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}^{2}\right) \\
&&+4\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
\ell ,h\right) }
\end{eqnarray*}%
It follows that 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&tr\left\{ A^{4}\right\} \\
&=&8\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) \leq m_{n}}\left[ A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon
\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }%
+A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left(
k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) } \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }%
\left. +A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( \ell
,h\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }\right] \\
&&+2\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) \leq
m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{4} \\
&&+4\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}\left( A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}+A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}+A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}\right) \text{\ \
\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ } \\
&=&8S_{n}+2\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) \leq
m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{4} \\
&&+4\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}\left( A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}+A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}+A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
It follows from the triangle inequality, the result given in part (a) above,
parts (b) and (c) of Lemma S2-1, and the symmetry of $A$ that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\left\vert S_{n}\right\vert &\leq &\frac{1}{8}tr\left\{ A^{4}\right\} +\frac{%
1}{4}\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) \leq
m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{4} \\
&&+\frac{1}{2}\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right)
<\left( k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}\left( A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}^{2}+A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}A_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}+A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}\right)
\\
&\leq &\frac{1}{8}tr\left\{ A^{4}\right\} +\frac{1}{4}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right)
\neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{4}+\frac{3}{2}\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) =1  \\ \left(
i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( K_{2,n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n^{2}}%
\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right) \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( K_{2,n}\right)
\end{eqnarray*}

Finally, for part (c), we take $\left\{ \eta _{\left( i,t\right) }\right\} $
to be a double-indexed sequence of $i.i.d.$ random variables with mean $0$
and variance $1$ and where $\eta _{\left( i,t\right) }$ and $Z$ are
independent for all $\left( i,t\right) $ and $n$. Define the random
quantities 
\begin{eqnarray*}
\Delta _{1} &=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right)
<\left( k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}\left[ A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\eta _{\left(
j,s\right) }\eta _{\left( k,\upsilon \right) }+A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\eta _{\left(
i,t\right) }\eta _{\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. +A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) }\eta _{\left( i,t\right) }\eta _{\left( j,s\right) }%
\right] \\
\Delta _{2} &=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right)
<\left( k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}\left[ A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\eta _{\left(
j,s\right) }\eta _{\left( k,\upsilon \right) }+A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\eta _{\left(
i,t\right) }\eta _{\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\right] \\
\Delta _{3} &=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right)
<\left( k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\eta
_{\left( i,t\right) }\eta _{\left( j,s\right) }
\end{eqnarray*}%
Next, note that using part (c) of Lemma S2-1 and the symmetry of $A$, we have%
\begin{eqnarray*}
E\left[ \Delta _{3}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] &=&E\left[ \left(
\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left( k,\upsilon
\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\eta _{\left( i,t\right)
}\eta _{\left( j,s\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left\{ \left(
k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) \right\} \leq m_{n}}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) } \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }^{2}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2} \\
&&+2\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
\ell ,h\right) } \\
&\leq &\dsum\limits_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right)
\neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }^{2}A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&&+2\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
\ell ,h\right) } \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right) +2\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left(
i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left( k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell
,h\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }
\end{eqnarray*}%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \Delta _{2}\Delta _{3}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) <\left(
j_{1},s_{1}\right) <\left( k_{1},g_{1}\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\{ A_{\left(
i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left( j_{1},s_{1}\right) }A_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right)
,\left( k_{1},g_{1}\right) }\eta _{\left( j_{1},s_{1}\right) }\eta _{\left(
k_{1},g_{1}\right) }\right. \right. \right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }%
\left. \left. +A_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left( j_{1},s_{1}\right)
}A_{\left( j_{1},s_{1}\right) ,\left( k_{1},g_{1}\right) }\eta _{\left(
i_{1},t_{1}\right) }\eta _{\left( k_{1},g_{1}\right) }\right\} \right) \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ }\left. \times \left( \dsum\limits_{1\leq \left(
i_{2},t_{2}\right) <\left( j_{2},s_{2}\right) <\left( k_{2},g_{2}\right)
\leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i_{2},t_{2}\right) ,\left( k_{2},g_{2}\right)
}A_{\left( j_{2},s_{2}\right) ,\left( k_{2},g_{2}\right) }\eta _{\left(
i_{2},t_{2}\right) }\eta _{\left( j_{2},s_{2}\right) }\right) |\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) \leq m_{n}}\left[ A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon
\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }%
\left. +A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right)
}A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }\right]
\end{eqnarray*}%
and%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \Delta _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right)
<\left( k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}\left\{ A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\varsigma
_{\left( j,s\right) }\varsigma _{\left( k,\upsilon \right) }+A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }\eta _{\left( i,t\right) }\eta _{\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}\right\} \right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left\{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right)
\right\} <\left( j,s\right) <\left( k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }A_{\left( \ell ,h\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( \ell
,h\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) } \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left\{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left(
\ell ,h\right) \right\} <\left( k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( \ell
,h\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) } \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left( \ell
,h\right) <\left( k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( \ell ,h\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) } \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( \ell ,h\right) <\left( i,t\right) <\left(
j,s\right) <\left( k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}A_{\left( \ell ,h\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }A_{\left( \ell ,h\right)
,\left( k,\upsilon \right) } \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}^{2}+\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2} \\
&&+2\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) <\left(
j,s\right) <\left( k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}A_{\left( \ell ,h\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( \ell ,h\right)
,\left( k,\upsilon \right) } \\
&&+2\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left( \ell
,h\right) <\left( k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( \ell ,h\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) } \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
