k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left(
\ell ,h\right) } \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( \ell
,h\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( \ell ,h\right) } \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}^{2}+\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}+2S_{n} \\
&\leq &2\dsum\limits_{\left( j,s\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ %
\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq
\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}+2S_{n} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left(
K_{2,n}\right) =O_{a.s.}\left( K_{2,n}\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
Since $\Delta _{1}=\Delta _{2}+\Delta _{3}$, it follows from part (b) of
this lemma and the results given above that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
E\left[ \Delta _{1}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] &=&E\left[ \Delta
_{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] +E\left[ \Delta _{3}^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] +2E\left[ \Delta _{2}\Delta _{3}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right) +4S_{n} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left(
K_{2,n}\right) =O_{a.s.}\left( K_{2,n}\right) \text{.}
\end{eqnarray*}%
Moreover, note that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
\ell ,h\right) } \\
&=&\frac{1}{2}E\left[ \Delta _{3}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] -\frac{1}{2}%
\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left( k,\upsilon
\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}^{2}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2} \\
&=&\frac{1}{2}E\left[ \left( \Delta _{1}-\Delta _{2}\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] -\frac{1}{2}\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left(
j,s\right) <\left( k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }^{2}
\end{eqnarray*}%
so that, by making use of the triangle inequality, Lo\`{e}ve's $c_{r}$
inequality, and the symmetry of $A$; we obtain%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\left\vert \dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right)
<\left( k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }\right\vert \\
&\leq &E\left[ \Delta _{1}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] +E\left[ \Delta
_{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] +\frac{1}{2}\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left(
i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) }^{2} \\
&\leq &E\left[ \Delta _{1}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] +E\left[ \Delta
_{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] +\frac{1}{2}\dsum\limits_{\left(
k,\upsilon \right) =1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( k,\upsilon \right)
,\left( j,s\right) \neq \left( k,\upsilon \right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( K_{2,n}\right) \text{. }\square
\end{eqnarray*}

\bigskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma OA-11:}

Let $L$ be the lower triangular matrix such that $L_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }=A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }\mathbb{I}%
\left\{ \left( i,t\right) >\left( j,s\right) \right\} $. Then, under
Assumptions 5-6,%
\begin{equation*}
\left\Vert LL^{\prime }\right\Vert _{F}=O_{a.s.}\left( \sqrt{K_{2,n}}\right) 
\text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where $\left\Vert \cdot \right\Vert _{F}$ denotes the Frobenius norm, i.e., $%
\left\Vert A\right\Vert _{F}=\left[ tr\left( A^{\prime }A\right) \right]
^{1/2}$.

\bigskip

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma OA-11: }

By parts (b) and (c) of Lemma S2-1 and part (c) of Lemma OA-10, we have%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\left\Vert LL^{\prime }\right\Vert _{F}^{2} \\
&=&tr\left\{ LL^{\prime }LL^{\prime }\right\} \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) \leq
m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{4}+2\dsum\limits_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left( k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}} 
\left[ A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}+A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }^{2}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}\right] \\
&&+4\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left(
k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( \ell ,h\right)
,\left( i,t\right) } \\
&\leq &\dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) \leq
m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{4}+2\dsum\limits_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right) <\left( k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}} 
\left[ A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}+A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }^{2}A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{2}\right] \\
&&+4\left\vert \dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right)
<\left( k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( \ell
,h\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert \\
&\leq &\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{4}+4\dsum\limits_{\left( k,\upsilon \right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1 
\\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( j,s\right) \neq
\left( k,\upsilon \right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }^{2}A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&&+4\left\vert \dsum\limits_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) <\left( j,s\right)
<\left( k,\upsilon \right) <\left( \ell ,h\right) \leq m_{n}}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }A_{\left( \ell
,h\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }\right\vert \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{%
K_{2,n}^{2}}{n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( K_{2,n}\right) =O_{a.s.}\left(
K_{2,n}\right) \text{,}
\end{eqnarray*}%
from which the required result follows. $\square $

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma OA-12:}

Under Assumptions 1-6, the following statements are true.

\begin{enumerate}
\item[(a)] 
\begin{equation*}
\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }AZ_{2}\Upsilon }{n}=\frac{\Upsilon
^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }Z_{2}\Upsilon }{n}%
=O_{a.s.}\left( 1\right)
\end{equation*}

\item[(b)] 
\begin{equation*}
D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }AUD_{\mu }^{-1}=o_{p}\left( 1\right)
\end{equation*}

\item[(c)] 
\begin{equation*}
\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }AUD_{\mu }^{-1}}{\sqrt{n}}%
=o_{p}\left( 1\right) ,\text{ \ }\frac{D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime
}AZ_{2}\Upsilon }{\sqrt{n}}=o_{p}\left( 1\right) .
\end{equation*}
\end{enumerate}

\bigskip

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma OA-12:}

To show part (a), note that, by making use of the fact that $M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }Z_{2}=0$, we have 
\begin{eqnarray*}
\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }AZ_{2}\Upsilon }{n} &=&\frac{%
\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }P^{\perp }Z_{2}\Upsilon }{n}-\frac{%
\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{%
\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }Z_{2}\Upsilon }{n} \\
&=&\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }P^{\perp }Z_{2}\Upsilon }{n} \\
&=&\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }\left( P^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}-P^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }\right) Z_{2}\Upsilon }{n} \\
&=&\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }\left( M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}-M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\right) Z_{2}\Upsilon }{n} \\
&=&\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}Z_{2}\Upsilon }{n}
\end{eqnarray*}

\noindent Moreover, part (iii) of Assumption 3 implies that%
\begin{equation*}
\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right)
}Z_{2}\Upsilon }{n}\leq \frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime
}Z_{2}\Upsilon }{n}=O_{a.s.}\left( 1\right)
\end{equation*}%
where we take $A\leq B$ for two square matrices $A$ and $B$ to mean that $%
A-B $ is negative semi-definite, or, alternatively, $B-A$ is positive
semidefinite. It follows immediately that%
\begin{equation*}
\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }AZ_{2}\Upsilon }{n}=\frac{\Upsilon
^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z_{1},Q\right) }Z_{2}\Upsilon }{n}%
=O_{a.s.}\left( 1\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
as required.

To show part (b), note that, for $a$, $b\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$ such that $%
\left\Vert a\right\Vert _{2}=\left\Vert b\right\Vert _{2}=1$, we write%
\begin{eqnarray*}
a^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }AUD_{\mu }^{-1}b &=&a^{\prime }D_{\mu
}^{-1}\left( \dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
=1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }U_{\left( i,t\right) }U_{\left( j,s\right)
}^{\prime }\right) D_{\mu }^{-1}b \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }u_{a,\left( i,t\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) },
\end{eqnarray*}%
where $u_{a,\left( i,t\right) }=a^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U_{\left( i,t\right)
}$ and $u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }=b^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U_{\left(
j,s\right) }$. Next, making use of the CS inequality, part (a) of Lemma
S2-1, and Assumptions 1, 2(i), 3(ii), and 5; we get 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \left( a^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }AUD_{\mu }^{-1}b\right)
^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }u_{a,\left( i,t\right)
}u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ %
\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) =1  \\ \left( k,\upsilon
\right) \neq \left( \ell ,h\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }A_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) }E\left[
u_{a,\left( i,t\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }u_{a,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }u_{b,\left( \ell ,h\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{ E\left[ u_{a,\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] +E\left[ u_{a,\left( i,t\right) }u_{b,\left( i,t\right) }|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left(
j,s\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right\} \\
&\leq &\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{ E\left[ u_{a,\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] +E\left[ \left\vert u_{a,\left( i,t\right) }u_{b,\left(
i,t\right) }\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ \left\vert
u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }\right\vert |\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] \right\} \\
&\leq &\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}E\left[ u_{a,\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \\
&&+\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\sqrt{E\left[ u_{a,\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F%
}_{n}^{Z}\right] }\sqrt{E\left[ u_{b,\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] }\sqrt{E\left[ u_{a,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] }\sqrt{E\left[ u_{b,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] } \\
&\leq &\frac{CK_{2,n}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}}\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}%
\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left(
i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{4}}\right) 
\text{ \ } \\
&=&o_{a.s.}\left( 1\right) ,
\end{eqnarray*}%
It follows from the conditional version of the Markov's inequality that for
any $\epsilon >0$%
\begin{equation*}
\Pr \left( \left\vert a^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }AUD_{\mu
}^{-1}b\right\vert \geq \epsilon |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \rightarrow 0%
\text{ }a.s.
\end{equation*}%
Moreover, note that%
\begin{equation*}
\sup_{n}E\left[ \left\vert \Pr \left( \left\vert a^{\prime }D_{\mu
}^{-1}U^{\prime }AUD_{\mu }^{-1}b\right\vert \geq \epsilon |\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) \right\vert ^{2}\right] <\infty
\end{equation*}%
Hence, by a version of the dominated convergence theorem, as given by
Theorem 25.12 of Billingsley (1986), it follows that as $n\rightarrow \infty 
$%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\Pr \left( \left\vert a^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }AUD_{\mu
}^{-1}b\right\vert \geq \epsilon \right) \\
&=&E\left[ \Pr \left( \left\vert a^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }AUD_{\mu
}^{-1}b\right\vert \geq \epsilon |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \right]
\rightarrow 0
\end{eqnarray*}%
Since the above result holds for all $a$, $b\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$ such that $%
\left\Vert a\right\Vert _{2}=\left\Vert b\right\Vert _{2}=1$, we further
deduce that 
\begin{equation*}
D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }AUD_{\mu }^{-1}=o_{p}\left( 1\right) ,
\end{equation*}%
as required.

To show part (c), again, let $u_{b,\left( i,t\right) }=U_{\left( i,t\right)
}D_{\mu }^{-1}b$. Note again that, by making use of the conditional serial
independence assumption in Assumption 1, we have%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left( \left[ \frac{a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }AUD_{\mu
}^{-1}b}{\sqrt{n}}\right] ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \\
&=&E\left( \left[ \frac{1}{\sqrt{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
k,\upsilon \right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right)
}a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2,\left( i,t\right) }u_{b,\left(
k,\upsilon \right) }\right] ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \\
&=&\frac{1}{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( k,\upsilon \right) }}%
^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( j,s\right) ,\left( \ell ,h\right) =1 
\\ \left( j,s\right) \neq \left( \ell ,h\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( \ell
,h\right) }a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2,\left( i,t\right) }a^{\prime
}\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2,\left( j,s\right) }E\left[ u_{b,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }u_{b,\left( \ell ,h\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\frac{1}{n}\dsum\limits_{\left( k,\upsilon \right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits _{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1 
\\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( j,s\right) \neq
\left( k,\upsilon \right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }a^{\prime
}\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2,\left( i,t\right) }a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime
}Z_{2,\left( j,s\right) }b^{\prime }D_{\mu }^{-1}E\left[ U_{\left(
k,\upsilon \right) }U_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) }^{\prime }|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] D_{\mu }^{-1}b \\
&\leq &\frac{\max_{1\leq \left( k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[
\left\Vert U_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] }{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}} \\
&&\times \frac{1}{n}\dsum\limits_{\left( k,\upsilon \right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1 
\\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( k,\upsilon \right) ,\left( j,s\right) \neq
\left( k,\upsilon \right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon
\right) }A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( k,\upsilon \right) }a^{\prime
}\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2,\left( i,t\right) }a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime
}Z_{2,\left( j,s\right) } \\
&=&\frac{\max_{1\leq \left( k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert
U_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}\frac{a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime
}Z_{2}^{\prime }AA^{\prime }Z_{2}\Upsilon a}{n}
\end{eqnarray*}%
Next, by note that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\frac{a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }AA^{\prime
}Z_{2}\Upsilon a}{n} \\
&=&\frac{a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }\left( P^{\perp
}-M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}\right) \left( P^{\perp }-M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }%
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\right) Z_{2}\Upsilon a}{n} \\
&=&\frac{a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }\left( P^{\perp
}+M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{%
\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }\right) Z_{2}\Upsilon a}{n} \\
&=&\frac{a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }P^{\perp
}Z_{2}\Upsilon a}{n} \\
&\leq &\frac{a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }Z_{2}\Upsilon a}{n}
\end{eqnarray*}%
from which it follows by Assumptions 2 and 3(iii) that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left( \left[ \frac{a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }AUD_{\mu
}^{-1}b}{\sqrt{n}}\right] ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \\
&\leq &\frac{\max_{1\leq \left( k,\upsilon \right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[
\left\Vert U_{\left( k,\upsilon \right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] }{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}\frac{a^{\prime
}\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }Z_{2}\Upsilon a}{n} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{1}{\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}}\right)
=o_{a.s.}\left( 1\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
It further follows from the conditional version of the Markov's inequality
that for any $\epsilon >0$%
\begin{equation*}
\Pr \left( \left\vert \frac{a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime
}AUD_{\mu }^{-1}b}{\sqrt{n}}\right\vert \geq \epsilon |\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) \rightarrow 0\text{ }a.s.
\end{equation*}%
In addition, note that%
\begin{equation*}
\sup_{n}E\left[ \left\vert \Pr \left( \left\vert \frac{a^{\prime }\Upsilon
^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }AUD_{\mu }^{-1}b}{\sqrt{n}}\right\vert \geq
\epsilon |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right) \right\vert ^{2}\right] <\infty
\end{equation*}%
Hence, by a version of the dominated convergence theorem, as given by
Theorem 25.12 of Billingsley (1986), it follows that as $n\rightarrow \infty 
$%
\begin{equation*}
\Pr \left( \left\vert \frac{a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime
}AUD_{\mu }^{-1}b}{\sqrt{n}}\right\vert \geq \epsilon \right) =E\left[ \Pr
\left( \left\vert \frac{a^{\prime }\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime
}AUD_{\mu }^{-1}b}{\sqrt{n}}\right\vert \geq \epsilon |\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right) \right] \rightarrow 0
\end{equation*}%
Since the above result holds for all $a$, $b\in \mathbb{R}^{d}$ such that $%
\left\Vert a\right\Vert _{2}=\left\Vert b\right\Vert _{2}=1$, we further
deduce that 
\begin{equation*}
\frac{\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }AUD_{\mu }^{-1}}{\sqrt{n}}%
=o_{p}\left( 1\right) ,
\end{equation*}%
\noindent Moreover, it follows immediately that%
\begin{equation*}
\frac{D_{\mu }^{-1}U^{\prime }AZ_{2}\Upsilon }{\sqrt{n}}=\left( \frac{%
\Upsilon ^{\prime }Z_{2}^{\prime }AUD_{\mu }^{-1}}{\sqrt{n}}\right) ^{\prime
}=o_{p}\left( 1\right) ,
\end{equation*}%
as required. $\square $

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma OA-13: }Let $A=P^{\perp }-M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }D_{%
\widehat{\vartheta }}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }$. Then, under Assumptions 2-6,
the following result holds as $K_{2,n}$, $n\rightarrow \infty $.%
\begin{equation*}
\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq j}}^{n}\dsum%
\limits_{t_{1},t_{2}=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s_{1},s_{2}=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left(
i,t_{1}\right) ,\left( j,s_{1}\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i,t_{2}\right) ,\left(
j,s_{2}\right) }^{2}=O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{3}}{n^{2}}\right) \text{.}
\end{equation*}

\smallskip

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma OA-13:}

To proceed, we apply the inequality $\left\vert XY\right\vert \leq \left(
1/2\right) X^{2}+\left( 1/2\right) Y^{2}$ as well as the result given part
(b) of Lemma S2-1 to obtain%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq j}}^{n}\dsum%
\limits_{t_{1},t_{2}=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s_{1},s_{2}=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left(
i,t_{1}\right) ,\left( j,s_{1}\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i,t_{2}\right) ,\left(
j,s_{2}\right) }^{2} \\
&\leq &\frac{1}{2}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq j}}%
^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{1},t_{2}=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum%
\limits_{s_{1},s_{2}=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) ,\left(
j,s_{1}\right) }^{4}+\frac{1}{2}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq j}}%
^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{1},t_{2}=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum%
\limits_{s_{1},s_{2}=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left( i,t_{2}\right) ,\left(
j,s_{2}\right) }^{4} \\
&\leq &\frac{\overline{T}^{2}}{2}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t_{1}\right) ,\left( j,s_{1}\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t_{1}\right) \neq
\left( j,s_{1}\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) ,\left(
j,s_{1}\right) }^{4}+\frac{\overline{T}^{2}}{2}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ %
\left( i,t_{2}\right) ,\left( j,s_{2}\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t_{2}\right)
\neq \left( j,s_{2}\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t_{2}\right) ,\left(
j,s_{2}\right) }^{4}\text{ \ (by Assumption 6(ii))} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{3}}{n^{2}}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{%
K_{2,n}^{3}}{n^{2}}\right) \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}^{3}}{n^{2}}\right) \text{. }\square
\end{eqnarray*}

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma OA-14: }Suppose that Assumptions 1, 2, 5, and 6 are
satisfied. Then, the following statements are true.

\begin{enumerate}
\item[(a)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{1,2}=O_{p}\left( \frac{1}{\sqrt{n}}\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{1,2} &=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\left( M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right)
}^{Q}\right) ^{2}\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right) }^{2}\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \times
\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ c=1  \\ c\neq q}}%
^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}M_{\left( j,v\right)
,\left( j,c\right) }^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }\varepsilon
_{\left( j,c\right) }\right\}
\end{eqnarray*}

\item[(b)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{1,3}=O_{p}\left( \frac{1}{\sqrt{n}}\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{1,3} &=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ r=1  \\ r\neq g}}%
^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}M_{\left( i,h\right)
,\left( i,r\right) }^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right) }\varepsilon
_{\left( i,r\right) }\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }%
\left. \text{\ }\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,v\right) }\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\left( M_{\left( j,v\right)
,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2}\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right)
}^{2}\right\}
\end{eqnarray*}

\item[(c)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{1,4}=O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{n}\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{1,4} &=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ r=1  \\ r\neq g}}%
^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}M_{\left( i,h\right)
,\left( i,r\right) }^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right) }\varepsilon
_{\left( i,r\right) }\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }%
\left. \times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ c=1  \\ c\neq
q }}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}M_{\left(
j,v\right) ,\left( j,c\right) }^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( j,c\right) }\right\}
\end{eqnarray*}

\item[(d)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{1}=O_{p}\left( \frac{1}{\sqrt{n}}\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\mathcal{A}_{1} \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right)
^{2}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&-\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}\varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) }^{2}
\end{eqnarray*}
\end{enumerate}

\medskip \bigskip

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma OA-14:}

To show part (a), write

\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{1,2} &=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left( M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
i,g\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2}\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right) }^{2} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ c=1  \\ c\neq q}}%
^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}M_{\left( j,v\right)
,\left( j,c\right) }^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }\varepsilon
_{\left( j,c\right) } \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ t,s=1  \\ %
t\neq s}}^{T_{i}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left( M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
i,g\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( i,s\right) ,\left( i,v\right)
}\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ c=1  \\ c\neq q}}%
^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,v\right) ,\left( i,q\right) }^{Q}M_{\left( i,v\right)
,\left( i,c\right) }^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right) }^{2}\varepsilon
_{\left( i,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,c\right) } \\
&&+\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq j}}%
^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left( M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
i,g\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ c=1  \\ c\neq q}}%
^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}M_{\left( j,v\right)
,\left( j,c\right) }^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right) }^{2}\varepsilon
_{\left( j,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,c\right) } \\
&=&\mathcal{A}_{1,2,1}+\mathcal{A}_{1,2,2}
\end{eqnarray*}%
Now, applying part (f) of Lemma S2-1 as well as Assumptions 2(i), 5, and 6;
we obtain%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{1,2,1}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \\
&\leq &\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ t,s=1 
\\ t\neq s}}^{T_{i}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left( M_{\left(
i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,s\right) ,\left(
i,v\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ %
c=1  \\ c\neq q}}^{T_{i}}\left\vert M_{\left( i,v\right) ,\left( i,q\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert M_{\left( i,v\right) ,\left( i,c\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert E\left[ \left\vert \varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right)
}^{2}\varepsilon _{\left( i,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,c\right)
}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &\overline{T}^{3}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert
M_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{4}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \frac{1}{K_{2,n}}%
\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ t,s=1  \\ t\neq s}}%
^{T_{i}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,s\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{n}\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
Moreover, let $\varsigma _{\left( i,g\right) }=\varepsilon _{\left(
i,g\right) }^{2}-E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] $, and, making use of Lo\`{e}ve's $c_{r}$ inequality, we can
write%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{1,2,2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &2E\left[ \left( \frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ %
i\neq j}}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left( M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
i,g\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2}\right. \right. \\
&&\left. \left. \times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,v\right) }\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ c=1 
\\ c\neq q}}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}M_{\left(
j,v\right) ,\left( j,c\right) }^{Q}\varsigma _{\left( i,g\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,c\right) }\right)
^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&&+2E\left[ \left( \frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq
j }}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left( M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
i,g\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2}\right. \right. \\
&&\left. \left. \times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,v\right) }\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ c=1 
\\ c\neq q}}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}M_{\left(
j,v\right) ,\left( j,c\right) }^{Q}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right)
}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( j,c\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] 
\text{.}
\end{eqnarray*}%
Now, note that, by the decoupling inequality given in Lemma OA-7, there
exists a finite constant $C_{3}$, whose explicit form is given in Lemma
OA-7, and independent copies $\left\{ \left( \varsigma _{\left( i,t\right)
}^{\left( \ell \right) },\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{\left( \ell
\right) }\right) \right\} _{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}$ (for $\ell =1,2,3$%
) of the sequence $\left\{ \left( \varsigma _{\left( i,t\right)
},\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }\right) \right\} _{\left( i,t\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}$ such that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&2E\left[ \left( \frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq
j }}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left( M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
i,g\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2}\right. \right. \\
&&\left. \left. \times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,v\right) }\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ c=1 
\\ c\neq q}}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}M_{\left(
j,v\right) ,\left( j,c\right) }^{Q}\varsigma _{\left( i,g\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,c\right) }\right)
^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &\left( 2\cdot C_{3}\right) E\left[ \left( \frac{1}{K_{2,n}}%
\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq j}}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}%
\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left( M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
i,g\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2}\right. \right. \\
&&\left. \left. \times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,v\right) }\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ c=1 
\\ c\neq q}}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}M_{\left(
j,v\right) ,\left( j,c\right) }^{Q}\varsigma _{\left( i,g\right) }^{\left(
1\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }^{\left( 2\right) }\varepsilon
_{\left( j,c\right) }^{\left( 3\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \\
&=&\left( 2\cdot C_{3}\right) \frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ %
i,j=1  \\ i\neq j}}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{1},t_{2}=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum%
\limits_{s_{1},s_{2}=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) ,\left(
j,s_{1}\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i,t_{2}\right) ,\left( j,s_{2}\right) }^{2} \\
&&\times
\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{h_{1},h_{2}=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) ,\left( i,h_{1}\right) }\right\vert \left\vert
J_{\left( i,t_{2}\right) ,\left( i,h_{2}\right) }\right\vert \left(
M_{\left( i,h_{1}\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2}\left(
M_{\left( i,h_{2}\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v_{1},v_{2}=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s_{1}\right) ,\left( j,v_{1}\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s_{2}\right) ,\left( j,v_{2}\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ c=1  \\ c\neq q}}%
^{T_{j}}\left\vert M_{\left( j,v_{1}\right) ,\left( j,q\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert M_{\left( j,v_{1}\right) ,\left( j,c\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert M_{\left( j,v_{2}\right) ,\left( j,q\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert M_{\left( j,v_{2}\right) ,\left( j,c\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \\
&&\times E\left[ \left( \varsigma _{\left( i,g\right) }^{\left( 1\right)
}\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ \left( \varepsilon _{\left(
j,q\right) }^{\left( 2\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E%
\left[ \left( \varepsilon _{\left( j,c\right) }^{\left( 3\right) }\right)
^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &\left( 2\cdot C_{3}\right) \overline{T}^{3}\left\Vert J\right\Vert
_{\infty }^{4}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq
m_{n}}\left\vert M_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\right) ^{8}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[
\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2}
\\
&&\times \frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq j}}%
^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{1},t_{2}=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum%
\limits_{s_{1},s_{2}=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) ,\left(
j,s_{1}\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i,t_{2}\right) ,\left( j,s_{2}\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{n^{2}}\right) =o_{a.s.}\left( \frac{1}{n}%
\right) \text{,}
\end{eqnarray*}%
where the (almost sure) order of magnitude above is calculated using Lemma
OA-13 and Assumptions 2(i), 5, and 6. Moreover, a further application of the
decoupling inequality given in Lemma OA-7 shows that there exists a finite
constant $C_{2}$, whose explicit form is given in Lemma OA-7, and
independent copies $\left\{ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{\left( \ell
\right) }\right\} _{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}$ (for $\ell =1,2$) of the
sequence $\left\{ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }\right\} _{\left(
i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}$ such that 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&2E\left[ \left( \frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq
j }}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left( M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
i,g\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2}\right. \right. \\
&&\left. \left. \times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,v\right) }\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ c=1 
\\ c\neq q}}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}M_{\left(
j,v\right) ,\left( j,c\right) }^{Q}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right)
}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( j,c\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &2C_{2}E\left[ \left( \frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1 
\\ i\neq j}}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{j}}A_{%
\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left( M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
i,g\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2}\right. \right. \\
&&\left. \left. \times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,v\right) }\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ c=1 
\\ c\neq q}}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}M_{\left(
j,v\right) ,\left( j,c\right) }^{Q}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right)
}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }^{\left(
1\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,c\right) }^{\left( 2\right) }\right) ^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &2C_{2}\frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{i_{1},i_{2}=1}^{n}\dsum%
\limits_{\substack{ j=1  \\ j\neq i_{1},i_{2}}}^{n}\dsum%
\limits_{t_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\dsum\limits_{t_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\dsum%
\limits_{s_{1},s_{2}=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left(
j,s_{1}\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i_{2},t_{2}\right) ,\left( j,s_{2}\right) }^{2}
\\
&&\times
\dsum\limits_{g_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\dsum\limits_{g_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\dsum%
\limits_{h_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\dsum\limits_{h_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left( i_{1},h_{1}\right) }\right\vert
\left\vert J_{\left( i_{2},t_{2}\right) ,\left( i_{2},h_{2}\right)
}\right\vert \left( M_{\left( i_{1},h_{1}\right) ,\left( i_{1},g_{1}\right)
}^{Q}\right) ^{2}\left( M_{\left( i_{2},h_{2}\right) ,\left(
i_{2},g_{2}\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v_{1},v_{2}=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s_{1}\right) ,\left( j,v_{1}\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s_{2}\right) ,\left( j,v_{2}\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ c=1  \\ c\neq q}}%
^{T_{j}}\left\vert M_{\left( j,v_{1}\right) ,\left( j,q\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert M_{\left( j,v_{1}\right) ,\left( j,c\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert M_{\left( j,v_{2}\right) ,\left( j,q\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert M_{\left( j,v_{2}\right) ,\left( j,c\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \\
&&\times E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i_{1},g_{1}\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i_{2},g_{2}\right) }^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ \left( \varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right)
}^{\left( 1\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ \left(
\varepsilon _{\left( j,c\right) }^{\left( 2\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &2C_{2}\overline{T}^{4}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{4}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert
M_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{8}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{4} \\
&&\times \frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{i_{1},i_{2}=1}^{n}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ j=1  \\ j\neq i_{1},i_{2}}}^{n}\dsum%
\limits_{t_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\dsum\limits_{t_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\dsum%
\limits_{s_{1},s_{2}=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left(
j,s_{1}\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i_{2},t_{2}\right) ,\left( j,s_{2}\right) }^{2}
\\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{1}{n}\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
where the (almost sure) order of magnitude above is calculated using part
(e) of Lemma S2-1 and Assumptions 2(i), 5, and 6. It follows that%
\begin{equation*}
E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{1,2,2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] =O_{a.s.}\left( 
\frac{K_{2,n}}{n^{2}}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{1}{n}\right)
=O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{1}{n}\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
so that, by the triangle inequality, the conditional version of Liapunov's
inequality, and Assumption 5(ii), we further obtain%
\begin{eqnarray*}
E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{1,2}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
&\leq &E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{1,2,1}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] +E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{1,2,2}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{1,2,1}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] +\sqrt{E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{1,2,2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] }
\\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{1}{\sqrt{n}}%
\right) =O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{1}{\sqrt{n}}\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
Hence, there exists a constant $\overline{C}<\infty $ such that for all $n$
sufficiently large 
\begin{equation*}
E\left[ \sqrt{n}\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{1,2}\right\vert \right] =E_{X}\left( 
\sqrt{n}E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{1,2}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \right) \leq \overline{C}\text{. \ }
\end{equation*}%
It follows from the Markov's inequality that for any $\epsilon >0$,%
\begin{equation*}
\Pr \left( \left\vert \sqrt{n}\mathcal{A}_{1,2}\right\vert \geq \frac{%
\overline{C}}{\epsilon }\right) \leq \epsilon \frac{\sqrt{n}E\left[
\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{1,2}\right\vert \right] }{\overline{C}}\leq \epsilon
\end{equation*}%
for all $n$ sufficiently large, which shows that%
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{A}_{1,2}=O_{p}\left( \frac{1}{\sqrt{n}}\right) .  \label{A12 term}
\end{equation}

To show part (b), note that since $A$ is symmetric, so that $A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }=A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }$,
it follows that $\mathcal{A}_{1,2}=\mathcal{A}_{1,3}$. Hence, using the same
argument as that given for part (a) above, we can show that%
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{A}_{1,3}=O_{p}\left( \frac{1}{\sqrt{n}}\right) .  \label{A13 term}
\end{equation}

Turning our attention to part (c), note that, in this case, we can write%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{1,4} &=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ r=1  \\ r\neq g}}%
^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}M_{\left( i,h\right)
,\left( i,r\right) }^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right) }\varepsilon
_{\left( i,r\right) } \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ c=1  \\ c\neq q}}%
^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}M_{\left( j,v\right)
,\left( j,c\right) }^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }\varepsilon
_{\left( j,c\right) } \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ s,t=1  \\ %
s\neq t}}^{T_{i}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ r=1  \\ r\neq g}}%
^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}M_{\left( i,h\right)
,\left( i,r\right) }^{Q} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ c=1  \\ c\neq q}}%
^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,v\right) ,\left( i,q\right) }^{Q}M_{\left( i,v\right)
,\left( i,c\right) }^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right) }\varepsilon
_{\left( i,r\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left(
i,c\right) } \\
&&+\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq j}}%
^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( i,h\right) }\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ r=1 
\\ r\neq g}}^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}M_{\left(
i,h\right) ,\left( i,r\right) }^{Q} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ c=1  \\ c\neq q}}%
^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}M_{\left( j,v\right)
,\left( j,c\right) }^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right) }\varepsilon
_{\left( i,r\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left(
j,c\right) } \\
&=&\mathcal{A}_{1,4,1}+\mathcal{A}_{1,4,2}\text{.}
\end{eqnarray*}%
Now, by the triangle inequality, part (f) of Lemma S2-1, and Assumptions
2(i), 5, and 6; we have%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{1,4.1}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \\
&\leq &\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ s,t=1 
\\ s\neq t}}^{T_{i}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ %
r=1  \\ r\neq g}}^{T_{i}}\left\vert M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,r\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ %
c=1  \\ c\neq q}}^{T_{i}}\left\vert M_{\left( i,v\right) ,\left( i,q\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert M_{\left( i,v\right) ,\left( i,c\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert E\left[ \left\vert \varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( i,r\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,q\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( i,c\right) }\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &\overline{T}^{4}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert
M_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{4}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \frac{1}{K_{2,n}}%
\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{s,t=1}^{T_{i}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( i,s\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{n}\right) =o_{a.s.}\left( 1\right) \text{. }
\end{eqnarray*}%
In addition, by the decoupling inequality given in Lemma OA-7, there exists
a finite constant $C_{4}$, whose explicit form is given in Lemma OA-7, and
independent copies $\left\{ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{\left( \ell
\right) }\right\} _{\left( i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}$ (for $\ell =1,2,3,4$) of
the sequence $\left\{ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }\right\} _{\left(
i,t\right) =1}^{m_{n}}$ such that 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{1,4.2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&E\left[ \left( \frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq
j }}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ r=1  \\ r\neq g}}^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
i,g\right) }^{Q}M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,r\right) }^{Q}\right. \right.
\\
&&\left. \left. \times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,v\right) }\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ c=1 
\\ c\neq q}}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}M_{\left(
j,v\right) ,\left( j,c\right) }^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( i,r\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( j,c\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &\frac{C_{4}}{K_{2,n}^{2}}E\left[ \left( \dsum\limits_{\substack{ %
i,j=1  \\ i\neq j}}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum%
\limits_{s=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ r=1  \\ r\neq g}}%
^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}M_{\left( i,h\right)
,\left( i,r\right) }^{Q}\right. \right. \\
&&\left. \left. \times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,v\right) }\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ c=1 
\\ c\neq q}}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}M_{\left(
j,v\right) ,\left( j,c\right) }^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right) }^{\left(
1\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,r\right) }^{\left( 2\right) }\varepsilon
_{\left( j,q\right) }^{\left( 3\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,c\right)
}^{\left( 4\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &\frac{C_{4}}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq j}}%
^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{1},t_{2}=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum%
\limits_{s_{1},s_{2}=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) ,\left(
j,s_{1}\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) ,\left( j,s_{1}\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h_{1},h_{2}=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t_{1}\right)
,\left( i,h_{1}\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left( i,t_{2}\right)
,\left( i,h_{2}\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ r=1  \\ r\neq g}}%
^{T_{i}}\left\vert M_{\left( i,h_{1}\right) ,\left( i,g\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert M_{\left( i,h_{1}\right) ,\left( i,r\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert M_{\left( i,h_{2}\right) ,\left( i,g\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert M_{\left( i,h_{2}\right) ,\left( i,r\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v_{1},v_{2}=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s_{1}\right) ,\left( j,v_{1}\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s_{2}\right) ,\left( j,v_{2}\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ c=1  \\ c\neq q}}%
^{T_{j}}\left\vert M_{\left( j,v_{1}\right) ,\left( j,q\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert M_{\left( j,v_{1}\right) ,\left( j,c\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert M_{\left( j,v_{2}\right) ,\left( j,q\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert M_{\left( j,v_{2}\right) ,\left( j,c\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert E\left[ \left( \varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right) }^{\left(
1\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&&\times E\left[ \left( \varepsilon _{\left( i,r\right) }^{\left( 2\right)
}\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ \left( \varepsilon _{\left(
j,q\right) }^{\left( 3\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E%
\left[ \left( \varepsilon _{\left( j,c\right) }^{\left( 4\right) }\right)
^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &C_{4}\overline{T}^{4}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{4}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert
M_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{8}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{4} \\
&&\times \frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq j}}%
^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{1},t_{2}=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum%
\limits_{s_{1},s_{2}=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) ,\left(
j,s_{1}\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) ,\left( j,s_{1}\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{n^{2}}\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
where the (almost sure) order of magnitude above is calculated using Lemma
OA-13 and Assumptions 2(i), 5, and 6. By the triangle inequality, the
conditional version of Liapunov's inequality, and Assumption 5(ii); we then
obtain%
\begin{eqnarray*}
E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{1,4}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
&\leq &E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{1,4,1}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] +E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{1,4,2}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{1,4,1}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] +\sqrt{E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{1,4,2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] }
\\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{\sqrt{%
K_{2,n}}}{n}\right) =O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{n}\right) =o_{a.s.}\left(
1\right) \text{. }
\end{eqnarray*}%
Hence, there exists a constant $\overline{C}<\infty $ such that for all $n$
sufficiently large 
\begin{equation*}
E\left[ \frac{n}{K_{2,n}}\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{1,4}\right\vert \right]
=E_{Z}\left( \frac{n}{K_{2,n}}E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}%
_{1,4}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \leq \overline{C}\text{%
. \ }
\end{equation*}%
It follows from the Markov's inequality that for any $\epsilon >0$,%
\begin{equation*}
\Pr \left( \left\vert \frac{n}{K_{2,n}}\mathcal{A}_{1,4}\right\vert \geq 
\frac{\overline{C}}{\epsilon }\right) \leq \epsilon \frac{n}{K_{2,n}}\frac{E%
\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{1,4}\right\vert \right] }{\overline{C}}\leq
\epsilon
\end{equation*}%
for all $n$ sufficiently large, which shows that%
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{A}_{1,4}=O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{n}\right) .  \label{A14 term}
\end{equation}%
\qquad

Finally to show part (d), note that we can decompose $\mathcal{A}_{1}$ as

\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\mathcal{A}_{1} \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right)
^{2}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&-\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}\varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{r=1}^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,h\right)
,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,r\right)
}^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,r\right) } \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{c=1}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right)
,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,c\right)
}^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,c\right) }-%
\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}\varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&=&\mathcal{A}_{1,1}+\mathcal{A}_{1,2}+\mathcal{A}_{1,3}+\mathcal{A}_{1,4}
\end{eqnarray*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\mathcal{A}_{1,1} \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left( M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
i,g\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2}\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\left( M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left(
j,q\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2}\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }^{2} \\
&&-\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}\varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) }^{2}
\end{eqnarray*}%
and where $\mathcal{A}_{1,2}$, $\mathcal{A}_{1,3}$, and $\mathcal{A}_{1,4}$
are as defined in parts (a)-(c) above. We will first show that $\mathcal{A}%
_{1,1}=0$. To proceed, note first that it is easily seen that $M^{Q}\circ
M^{Q}$ is a block diagonal matrix, which can be written as%
\begin{equation*}
M^{Q}\circ M^{Q}=\left( 
\begin{array}{cccc}
\left( M^{Q}\circ M^{Q}\right) _{1} & 0 & \cdots & 0 \\ 
0 & \left( M^{Q}\circ M^{Q}\right) _{2} & \ddots & \vdots \\ 
\vdots & \ddots & \ddots & 0 \\ 
0 & \cdots & 0 & \left( M^{Q}\circ M^{Q}\right) _{n}%
\end{array}%
\right)
\end{equation*}%
where the $i^{th}$ diagonal matrix $\left( M^{Q}\circ M^{Q}\right) _{i}$ is $%
T_{i}\times T_{i}$. Moreover, by definition $J=\left( M^{Q}\circ
M^{Q}\right) ^{-1}$, where the inverse exists in light of Assumption 6.
Hence, $J$ can also be written in block diagonal form as%
\begin{equation*}
J=\left( 
\begin{array}{cccc}
J_{1} & 0 & \cdots & 0 \\ 
0 & J_{2} & \ddots & \vdots \\ 
\vdots & \ddots & \ddots & 0 \\ 
0 & \cdots & 0 & J_{n}%
\end{array}%
\right) =\left( 
\begin{array}{cccc}
\left( M^{Q}\circ M^{Q}\right) _{1}^{-1} & 0 & \cdots & 0 \\ 
0 & \left( M^{Q}\circ M^{Q}\right) _{2}^{-1} & \ddots & \vdots \\ 
\vdots & \ddots & \ddots & 0 \\ 
0 & \cdots & 0 & \left( M^{Q}\circ M^{Q}\right) _{n}^{-1}%
\end{array}%
\right)
\end{equation*}%
Let $e_{\left( i,t\right) }$ be an $m_{n}\times 1$ elementary vector whose $%
\left( i,t\right) ^{th}$ component is one and all other components are zero,
and let $e_{h,T_{i}}$ be a $T_{i}\times 1$ elementary vector, whose $h^{th}$
component equals one and all other components equal to zero. Using these
notations, one can show by direct calculation that, for any $t,g\in \left\{
1,...,T_{i}\right\} $ and for any $i\in \left\{ 1,2,...,n\right\} $,%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left(
M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2}
&=&\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }Je_{\left(
i,h\right) }e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }\left[ M^{Q}\circ M^{Q}\right]
e_{\left( i,g\right) } \\
&=&\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}e_{t,T_{i}}^{\prime
}J_{i}e_{h,T_{i}}e_{h,T_{i}}^{\prime }\left( M^{Q}\circ M^{Q}\right)
_{i}e_{g,T_{i}} \\
&=&e_{t,T_{i}}^{\prime }\left( M^{Q}\circ M^{Q}\right)
_{i}^{-1}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}e_{h,T_{i}}e_{h,T_{i}}^{\prime }\left(
M^{Q}\circ M^{Q}\right) _{i}e_{g,T_{i}} \\
&=&e_{t,T_{i}}^{\prime }\left( M^{Q}\circ M^{Q}\right) _{i}^{-1}\left(
M^{Q}\circ M^{Q}\right) _{i}e_{g,T_{i}} \\
&=&e_{t,T_{i}}^{\prime }I_{T_{i}}e_{g,T_{i}}\text{ } \\
&=&\left\{ 
\begin{array}{cc}
1 & \text{if }t=g \\ 
0 & \text{if }t\neq g%
\end{array}%
\right.
\end{eqnarray*}%
These calculations imply that 
\begin{eqnarray}
&&\mathcal{A}_{1,1}  \notag \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{g,h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\left( M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2}\varepsilon
_{\left( i,g\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{q,v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,v\right) }\left( M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right)
}^{Q}\right) ^{2}\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }^{2}  \notag \\
&&-\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}\varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) }^{2}  \notag \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}\varepsilon _{\left( j,s\right) }^{2}-\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}%
\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left(
i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2}\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}\varepsilon _{\left(
j,s\right) }^{2}  \notag \\
&=&0\text{.}  \label{A11 term}
\end{eqnarray}

\noindent Combining (\ref{A11 term}) with the results obtained in
expressions (\ref{A12 term})-(\ref{A14 term}) above and making use of
Assumption 5(ii), we further obtain%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{1} &=&\mathcal{A}_{1,1}+\mathcal{A}_{1,2}+\mathcal{A}_{1,3}+%
\mathcal{A}_{1,4} \\
&=&0+O_{p}\left( \frac{1}{\sqrt{n}}\right) +O_{p}\left( \frac{1}{\sqrt{n}}%
\right) +O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{2,n}}{n}\right) =O_{p}\left( \frac{1}{\sqrt{n}}%
\right) \text{. }\square
\end{eqnarray*}

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma OA-15: }Let Assumptions 1-6 be satisfied, and let $%
\left\{ \widehat{\delta }_{n}\right\} $ be a sequence of estimators such that%
\begin{equation*}
\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}\overset{p}{%
\rightarrow }0\text{ as }n\rightarrow \infty \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
as long as $\sqrt{K_{2,n}}/\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}\rightarrow 0$%
. Then, the following statements are true.

\begin{enumerate}
\item[(a)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{2,1}=O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) =o_{p}\left( 1\right) 
\text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{2,1} &=&\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left(
e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) \left(
e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }%
\left. \times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon
\right) \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right)
\right\}
\end{eqnarray*}

\item[(b)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{2,2}=o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\mathcal{A}_{2,2}=\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left(
e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) \left(
e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }%
\left. \times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X%
\left[ \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right) \left( e_{\left(
j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \right\}
\end{eqnarray*}

\item[(c)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{2,3}=o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{2,3} &=&\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left(
e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{%
\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right) \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \
\ \ \ \ }\left. \text{\ }\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \right\}
\end{eqnarray*}

\item[(d)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{2,4}=o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\mathcal{A}_{2,4}=\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left(
e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{%
\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right) \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }%
\left. \times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X%
\left[ \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right) \left( e_{\left(
j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \right\}
\end{eqnarray*}

\item[(e)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{2}=o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\mathcal{A}_{2} \\
&=&\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon +e_{\left(
i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{\delta }%
_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right) \left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon +e_{\left(
j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{\delta }%
_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right) \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right)
\end{eqnarray*}
\end{enumerate}

\bigskip

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma OA-15:}

To show part (a), we first apply the triangle inequality and the inequality $%
\left\vert XY\right\vert \leq \left( 1/2\right) X^{2}+\left( 1/2\right)
Y^{2} $ to obtain%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{2,1}\right\vert \\
&\leq &\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\right\vert \right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ }\left. \times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left\vert \left( e_{\left(
i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) \left( e_{\left(
i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) \left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \right\vert \right\} \\
&\leq &\mathcal{A}_{2,1,1}+\mathcal{A}_{2,1,2}
\end{eqnarray*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{2,1,1} &=&\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\text{,} \\
\mathcal{A}_{2,1,2} &=&\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\text{.}
\end{eqnarray*}%
Clearly $\mathcal{A}_{2,1,1}\geq 0$ and $\mathcal{A}_{2,1,2}\geq 0$. Next,
note that we can apply Assumptions 1, 2(i), 5, and 6 as well as part (a) of
Lemma S2-1 to obtain%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{2,1,1}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right)
}^{Q}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,g\right) }^{Q}
\\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{\left( l,r\right) =1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,h\right)
,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\dsum\limits_{\left( k,c\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( k,c\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}E\left[
\varepsilon _{\left( l,r\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( k,c\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,g\right) }|\mathcal{%
F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\left( M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left(
j,q\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2}\left( P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( j,q\right)
}^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }^{4}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&&+\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\left(
M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2} \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \dsum\limits_{\left( l,r\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right) ^{2}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( l,r\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&&+\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( j,q\right)
}^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times
\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,g\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( j,g\right)
}^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( j,g\right) }^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\end{eqnarray*}%
\begin{eqnarray}
&\leq &\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq
m_{n}}\left\vert M_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\right) ^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[
\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right)
\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2}  \notag \\
&&\times \frac{2\overline{T}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}}{K_{2,n}}%
\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left(
i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2}  \notag \\
&&+2\overline{T}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert M_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2}  \notag \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ }\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) \frac{1}{%
K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}  \notag \\
&&+4\overline{T}^{2}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert M_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2}  \notag \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ }\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2}%
\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}  \notag \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}%
}{n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) =O_{a.s.}\left( 
\frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) \text{.}  \label{EA211}
\end{eqnarray}%
In the same way, we can also show that $E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{2,1,2}|\mathcal{%
F}_{n}^{Z}\right] =O_{a.s.}\left( K_{n}/n\right) $, from which it follows%
\begin{eqnarray*}
E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{2,1}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
&\leq &E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{2,1,1}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] +E\left[ 
\mathcal{A}_{2,1,2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}%
\right) =O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) \text{.}
\end{eqnarray*}%
Hence, there exists a constant $\overline{C}<\infty $ such that for all $n$
sufficiently large 
\begin{equation*}
E\left[ \frac{n}{K_{n}}\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{2,1}\right\vert \right]
=E_{Z}\left( \frac{n}{K_{n}}E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{2,1}\right\vert |%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \leq \overline{C}\text{. \ }
\end{equation*}%
It follows from the Markov's inequality that for any $\epsilon >0$,%
\begin{equation*}
\Pr \left( \left\vert \frac{n}{K_{n}}\mathcal{A}_{2,1}\right\vert \geq \frac{%
\overline{C}}{\epsilon }\right) \leq \epsilon \frac{n}{K_{n}}\frac{E\left[
\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{2,1}\right\vert \right] }{\overline{C}}\leq \epsilon
\end{equation*}%
for all $n$ sufficiently large, which shows that%
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{A}_{2,1}=O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) =o_{p}\left( 1\right) .
\label{A21}
\end{equation}

To show part (b), we again apply the triangle inequality and the inequality $%
\left\vert XY\right\vert \leq \left( 1/2\right) X^{2}+\left( 1/2\right)
Y^{2} $ to get 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{2,2}\right\vert \\
&\leq &\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ }\times \left\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime
}P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) \left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right) \left(
e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \right\vert \\
&=&\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \left\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
