}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }U\left[ \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right]
\right) \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right)
\right\vert \\
&\leq &\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&+\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ }\times e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}U\left[ \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \left[ \widehat{\delta }%
_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] ^{\prime }U^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left(
j,v\right) } \\
&\leq &\mathcal{A}_{2,2,1}+\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta
_{0}\right\Vert _{2}^{2}\mathcal{A}_{2,2,2}\text{,}
\end{eqnarray*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{2,2,1} &=&\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}, \\
\mathcal{A}_{2,2,2} &=&\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&\times e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }UU^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,v\right) }
\end{eqnarray*}%
Note that $\mathcal{A}_{2,2,1}$ is the same as $\mathcal{A}_{2,1,1}$ above,
so from expression (\ref{EA211}), we get%
\begin{equation*}
0\leq E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{2,2,1}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] =O_{a.s.}\left( 
\frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) \text{.}
\end{equation*}%
Moreover, using a similar argument as that given above to show expression (%
\ref{A21}) allows us to deduce that 
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{A}_{2,2,1}=O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) =o_{p}\left( 1\right)
.  \label{A221}
\end{equation}

Next, making use of the decomposition $M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}=M^{Q}-P^{Z^{\perp }}$, with $P^{Z^{\perp }}=M^{Q}Z\left( Z^{\prime
}M^{Q}Z\right) ^{-1}Z^{\prime }M^{Q}$, we can obtain the inequality 
\begin{eqnarray}
&&e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }UU^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,v\right) }  \notag \\
&=&e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }\left[ M^{Q}-P^{Z^{\perp }}\right]
UU^{\prime }\left[ M^{Q}-P^{Z^{\perp }}\right] e_{\left( j,v\right) }  \notag
\\
&\leq &e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}UU^{\prime }M^{Q}e_{\left(
j,v\right) }+2\left\vert e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}UU^{\prime
}P^{Z^{\perp }}e_{\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert +e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}UU^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}e_{\left( j,v\right) } 
\notag \\
&\leq &2e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}UU^{\prime }M^{Q}e_{\left(
j,v\right) }+2e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}UU^{\prime
}P^{Z^{\perp }}e_{\left( j,v\right) }  \label{ineq eMUUMe} \\
&&\left( \text{since }\left\vert e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}UU^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}e_{\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \leq \frac{%
e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}UU^{\prime }M^{Q}e_{\left( j,v\right) }%
}{2}+\frac{e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}UU^{\prime
}P^{Z^{\perp }}e_{\left( j,v\right) }}{2}\right)  \notag
\end{eqnarray}
Applying the inequality given in expression (\ref{ineq eMUUMe}) above, we
further obtain%
\begin{eqnarray*}
0 &\leq &\mathcal{A}_{2,2,2} \\
&=&\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&\times e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }UU^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,v\right) } \\
&\leq &\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}UU^{\prime }M^{Q}e_{\left( j,v\right) } \\
&&+\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}P^{Z^{\perp }}UU^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}e_{\left( j,v\right) } \\
&=&\mathcal{A}_{2,2,2,1}+\mathcal{A}_{2,2,2,2},\text{ }\left( say\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
Applying part (a) of Lemma S2-1 and Assumptions 2(i), 5, and 6; we get%
\begin{eqnarray*}
0 &\leq &E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{2,2,2,1}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert E\left[ \left( e_{\left(
i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}UU^{\prime }M^{Q}e_{\left( j,v\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \\
&\leq &\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{r=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert M_{\left(
i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert M_{\left(
i,h\right) ,\left( i,r\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{c=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert
M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,c\right) }^{Q}\right\vert E\left[ \left\vert
\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,r\right) }U_{\left(
j,q\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left( j,c\right) }\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \\
&\leq &4\overline{T}^{4}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert
M_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{4}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{1/2} \\
&&\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert
U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\right) ^{1/2}\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( 1\right) \text{.}
\end{eqnarray*}%
In addition, for $E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{2,2,2,2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] $%
, we have, by straightforward calculations using Assumption 1 and the
triangle inequality, 
\begin{eqnarray}
0 &\leq &E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{2,2,2,2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]  \notag \\
&=&\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert  \notag \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\right\vert E\left[ \left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}UU^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}e_{\left( j,v\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\notag \\
&=&\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{r=1}^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,h\right)
,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,r\right) }^{Q}  \notag
\\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \dsum\limits_{\left( k,q\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( k,q\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\dsum\limits_{\left( l,c\right) =1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left(
l,c\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( i,r\right) }U_{\left( k,q\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left(
l,c\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]  \notag \\
&\leq &\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \right.  \notag \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \left.
\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\left( M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right)
}^{Q}\right) ^{2}\left( P_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right) ^{2}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right) }^{2}U_{\left(
i,g\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left( i,g\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\right\}  \notag \\
&&+\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\left( M_{\left(
i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2}\right.  \notag \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left.
\times \dsum\limits_{\left( k,q\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left(
j,v\right) ,\left( k,q\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2}E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,g\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ U_{\left(
k,q\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left( k,q\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\right\}  \notag \\
&&+\frac{8}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\right\vert \dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{r=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert
M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert
M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,r\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right.  \notag \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left\vert P_{\left(
j,v\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert \left\vert P_{\left(
j,v\right) ,\left( i,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert E\left[ \left\vert
\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,r\right) }U_{\left(
i,g\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left( i,r\right) }\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \right\}  \label{EA2222 bd}
\end{eqnarray}%
Applying the CS inequality to (\ref{EA2222 bd}) and making use of part (a)
of Lemma S2-1 as well as Assumptions 2(i), 5, and 6; we then obtain 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{2,2,2,2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &4\overline{T}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert M_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{1/2} \\
&&\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert
U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\right) ^{1/2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2}\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}%
\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left(
i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&&+4\overline{T}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert M_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \\
&&\text{ \ }\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[
\left\Vert U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \right) \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) \frac{1}{K_{2,n}}%
\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left(
i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&&+8\overline{T}^{2}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert M_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{1/2} \\
&&\text{ \ \ }\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[
\left\Vert U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \right) ^{1/2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2}%
\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}%
}{n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) =O_{a.s.}\left( 
\frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) =o_{a.s.}\left( 1\right) .
\end{eqnarray*}%
It follows from these calculations that 
\begin{eqnarray*}
0 &\leq &E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{2,2,2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{2,2,2,1}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] +E\left[ 
\mathcal{A}_{2,2,2,2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( 1\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( 1\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
Hence, there exists a constant $\overline{C}<\infty $ such that for all $n$
sufficiently large 
\begin{equation*}
E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{2,2,2}\right\vert \right] =E\left[ \mathcal{A%
}_{2,2,2}\right] =E_{Z}\left( E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{2,2,2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \right) \leq \overline{C}\text{. \ }
\end{equation*}%
Application of the Markov's inequality then implies that, for any $\epsilon
>0$,%
\begin{equation*}
\Pr \left( \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{2,2,2}\right\vert \geq \frac{\overline{C}%
}{\epsilon }\right) \leq \epsilon \frac{E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{2,2,2}\right] }{%
\overline{C}}\leq \epsilon
\end{equation*}%
for all $n$ sufficiently large, which shows that%
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{A}_{2,2,2}=O_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{.}  \label{A222}
\end{equation}%
Combining the results on $\mathcal{A}_{2,2,1}$ and $\mathcal{A}_{2,2,2}$, we
have%
\begin{eqnarray}
\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{2,2}\right\vert &\leq &\mathcal{A}%
_{2,2,1}+\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}^{2}%
\mathcal{A}_{2,2,2}  \notag \\
&=&O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) +o_{p}\left( 1\right) O_{p}\left(
1\right) =o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{.}  \label{A22}
\end{eqnarray}%
\qquad

Next, to show part (c), note that since $A$ is symmetric, so that $A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }=A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }$,
it follows that $\mathcal{A}_{2,2}=\mathcal{A}_{2,3}$. Hence, using the same
argument as that given for part (b) above, we can show that

\begin{equation}
\mathcal{A}_{2,3}=o_{p}\left( 1\right) .  \label{A23}
\end{equation}

Turning our attention to part (d), note that, applying the triangle
inequality and the inequality that $\left\vert XY\right\vert \leq \left(
1/2\right) X^{2}+\left( 1/2\right) Y^{2}$, we obtain%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{2,4}\right\vert \\
&\leq &\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \left\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right]
\right) \left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right)
\left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ 
\widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right) \left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \right\vert \\
&\leq &\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&\times e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ 
\widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \left[ \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta
_{0}\right] ^{\prime }X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,v\right) }
\\
&&+\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&\text{ \ \ }\times e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X%
\left[ \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \left[ \widehat{\delta }%
_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] ^{\prime }X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left(
i,h\right) } \\
&\leq &\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert
_{2}^{2}\left( \mathcal{A}_{2,4,1}+\mathcal{A}_{2,4,2}\right) \text{,}
\end{eqnarray*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{2,4,1} &=&\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&\times e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }XX^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,v\right) } \\
&=&\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&\times e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }UU^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,v\right) } \\
\mathcal{A}_{2,4,2} &=&\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&\times e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }XX^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,h\right) } \\
&=&\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&\times e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }UU^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,h\right) }
\end{eqnarray*}%
Note that both $\mathcal{A}_{2,4,1}$ and $\mathcal{A}_{2,4,2}$ are of the
same form as $\mathcal{A}_{2,2,2}$, so that the result given in expression (%
\ref{A222}) allows us to deduce that%
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{2,4,1}=O_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{ and }\mathcal{A}%
_{2,4,2}=O_{p}\left( 1\right) ,
\end{equation*}%
from which it further follows that 
\begin{equation}
\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{2,4}\right\vert \leq \left\Vert \widehat{\delta }%
_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}^{2}\left( \mathcal{A}_{2,4,1}+\mathcal{A}%
_{2,4,2}\right) =o_{p}\left( 1\right) \left[ O_{p}\left( 1\right)
+O_{p}\left( 1\right) \right] =o_{p}\left( 1\right) .  \label{A24}
\end{equation}

Finally, for part (e), note that we can decompose $\mathcal{A}_{2}$ as%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\mathcal{A}_{2} \\
&=&\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left(
e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon +e_{\left(
i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{\delta }%
_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right) \left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \times
\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\left(
e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon +e_{\left(
j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{\delta }%
_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right) \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \right\} \\
&=&\mathcal{A}_{2,1}+\mathcal{A}_{2,2}+\mathcal{A}_{2,3}+\mathcal{A}_{2,4}%
\text{,}
\end{eqnarray*}%
where $\mathcal{A}_{2,1}$, $\mathcal{A}_{2,2}$, $\mathcal{A}_{2,3}$, and $%
\mathcal{A}_{2,4}$ are as defined in parts (a)-(d) above. It follows from
the results given in expressions (\ref{A21}), (\ref{A22}), (\ref{A23}), and (%
\ref{A24}) that 
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{2} &=&\mathcal{A}_{2,1}+\mathcal{A}_{2,2}+\mathcal{A}_{2,3}+%
\mathcal{A}_{2,4} \\
&=&O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) +o_{p}\left( 1\right) +o_{p}\left(
1\right) +o_{p}\left( 1\right) \\
&=&o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{. }\square
\end{eqnarray*}

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma OA-16: }Let Assumptions 1-6 be satisfied, and let $%
\left\{ \widehat{\delta }_{n}\right\} $ be a sequence of estimators such that%
\begin{equation*}
\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}\overset{p}{%
\rightarrow }0\text{ as }n\rightarrow \infty \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
as long as $\sqrt{K_{2,n}}/\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}\rightarrow 0$%
. Then, the following statements are true.

\begin{enumerate}
\item[(a)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{3,1}=O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) =o_{p}\left(
1\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&\mathcal{A}_{3,1} \\
&=&\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}
\end{eqnarray*}

\item[(b)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{3,2}=O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) =o_{p}\left( 1\right) 
\text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{3,2} &=&\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \times
\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\right\vert e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}XX^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,v\right) }\right\}
\end{eqnarray*}

\item[(c)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{3,3}=O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) =o_{p}\left( 1\right) 
\text{.}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray}
&&\mathcal{A}_{3,3}=\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\right\vert e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}XX^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,h\right) }\right.  \notag \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \
\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \text{\ }\times
\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\right\}  \notag
\end{eqnarray}

\item[(d)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{3,4}=O_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray}
&&\mathcal{A}_{3,4}=\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\right\vert e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}XX^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,h\right) }\right.  \notag \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \
\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }XX^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left(
j,v\right) }\right\}  \notag
\end{eqnarray}

\item[(e)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{3}=o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{3} &=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left[
e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon +e_{\left(
i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{\delta }%
_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right] ^{2}\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \times
\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\left[
e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon +e_{\left(
j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{\delta }%
_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right] ^{2}\right\}
\end{eqnarray*}
\end{enumerate}

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma OA-16:}

To show part (a), note that, by applying part (a) of Lemma S2-1 and
Assumptions 1, 2(i), 5, and 6; we have 
\begin{eqnarray*}
0 &\leq &E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{3,1}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert E\left[ \left( e_{\left(
i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\left( e_{\left(
j,v\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{\left( l,r\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\dsum\limits_{\left( k,c\right) =1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
k,c\right) }^{Z^{\perp }} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{\left( p,q\right) =1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( j,v\right)
,\left( p,q\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\dsum\limits_{\left( g,w\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( g,w\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}E\left[
\varepsilon _{\left( l,r\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( k,c\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( p,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( g,w\right) }|\mathcal{%
F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \dsum\limits_{\left( l,r\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right) ^{2}\left( P_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right) ^{2}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( l,r\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&&+\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{\left( l,r\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right) ^{2} \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \dsum\limits_{\left( p,q\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( p,q\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right) ^{2}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( l,r\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( p,q\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&&+\frac{8}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{\left( l,r\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left\vert P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right\vert \left\vert P_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right\vert \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \dsum\limits_{\left( k,c\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left\vert P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( k,c\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right\vert \left\vert P_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( k,c\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right\vert E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( l,r\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( p,q\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right]
\end{eqnarray*}%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&\leq &4\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{%
F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{3}%
\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&&+4\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{%
F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2}%
\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&&+8\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{%
F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2}%
\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{3}}{n^{3}}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{%
K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) .
\end{eqnarray*}%
Hence, there exists a constant $\overline{C}<\infty $ such that for all $n$
sufficiently large 
\begin{equation*}
E\left[ \frac{n^{2}}{K_{n}^{2}}\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{3,1}\right\vert %
\right] =E\left[ \frac{n^{2}}{K_{n}^{2}}\mathcal{A}_{3,1}\right]
=E_{Z}\left( E\left[ \frac{n^{2}}{K_{n}^{2}}\mathcal{A}_{3,1}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \leq \overline{C}\text{. \ }
\end{equation*}%
Application of the Markov's inequality then implies that, for any $\epsilon
>0$,%
\begin{equation*}
\Pr \left( \frac{n^{2}}{K_{n}^{2}}\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{3,1}\right\vert
\geq \frac{\overline{C}}{\epsilon }\right) \leq \epsilon \frac{n^{2}}{%
K_{n}^{2}}\frac{E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{3,1}\right] }{\overline{C}}\leq \epsilon
\end{equation*}%
for all $n$ sufficiently large, which shows that%
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{A}_{3,1}=O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) .  \label{A31}
\end{equation}

To show part (b), first let $e_{b,d}$ denote a $d\times 1$ elementary vector
whose $b^{th}$ component equals one for $b\in \left\{ 1,...,d\right\} $ and
whose other components all equal to zero. Using the fact that 
\begin{equation*}
M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X=M^{Q}U-P^{Z^{\perp }}U\text{,}
\end{equation*}%
we can apply the inequality $\left\vert
\dsum\nolimits_{i=1}^{m}a_{i}\right\vert ^{r}\leq
m^{r-1}\dsum\nolimits_{i=1}^{m}\left\vert a_{i}\right\vert ^{r}$ to obtain 
\begin{eqnarray*}
0 &\leq &\mathcal{A}_{3,2} \\
&=&\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }XX^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,v\right) } \\
&=&\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{b=1}^{d}\left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}Ue_{b,d}-e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}Ue_{b,d}\right)
^{2} \\
&\leq &\frac{8}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right)
^{2}\dsum\limits_{b=1}^{d}\left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}Ue_{b,d}\right) ^{2} \\
&&+\frac{8}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right)
^{2}\dsum\limits_{b=1}^{d}\left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}Ue_{b,d}\right) ^{2} \\
&=&\frac{8}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}UU^{\prime }M^{Q}e_{\left( j,v\right) } \\
&&+\frac{8}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}UU^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}e_{\left( j,v\right) } \\
&=&\mathcal{A}_{3,2,1}+\mathcal{A}_{3,2,2}
\end{eqnarray*}%
Making use of part (a) of Lemma S2-1 and Assumptions 1, 2(i), 5, and 6; we
obtain%
\begin{eqnarray*}
0 &\leq &E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{3,2,1}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\frac{8}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert E\left[ e_{\left(
j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}UU^{\prime }M^{Q}e_{\left( j,v\right) }e_{\left(
i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \varepsilon ^{\prime
}P^{Z^{\perp }}e_{\left( i,h\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\frac{8}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right)
}^{Q}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,g\right) }^{Q}
\\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{\left( l,r\right) =1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,h\right)
,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\dsum\limits_{\left( k,c\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( k,c\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}E\left[
U_{\left( j,q\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left( j,g\right) }\varepsilon _{\left(
l,r\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( k,c\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &\frac{8}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\left(
M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2}\left( P_{\left(
i,h\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2}E\left[ U_{\left(
j,q\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left( j,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right)
}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&&+\frac{8}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\left(
M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2} \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ }\times \dsum\limits_{\left( l,r\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left(
P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2}E\left[
U_{\left( j,q\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left( j,q\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( l,r\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \\
&&+\frac{16}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( j,q\right)
}^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert M_{\left(
j,v\right) ,\left( j,g\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert P_{\left(
i,h\right) ,\left( j,g\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert E\left[ \left\vert
U_{\left( j,q\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left( j,g\right) }\varepsilon _{\left(
j,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,g\right) }\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right]
\end{eqnarray*}%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&\leq &8\overline{T}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert M_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{1/2} \\
&&\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert
U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{W}\right]
\right) ^{1/2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2}\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}%
\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left(
i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&&+8\overline{T}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert M_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ }\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E%
\left[ \left\Vert U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{W}\right] \right) \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) \frac{1}{%
K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&&+16\overline{T}^{2}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert
M_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{1/2} \\
&&\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert
U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{W}\right]
\right) ^{1/2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2}\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}%
\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left(
i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}%
}{n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) =O_{a.s.}\left( 
\frac{K_{n}}{n}\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
Finally, applying part (a) of Lemma S2-1 and Assumptions 1, 2(i), 5, and 6;
we get 
\begin{eqnarray*}
0 &\leq &E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{3,2,3}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\frac{8}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\right\vert E\left[ e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}UU^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}e_{\left( j,v\right) }e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \varepsilon ^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}e_{\left( i,h\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\frac{8}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{\left( p,q\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( p,q\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\dsum\limits_{\left( f,g\right) =1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left(
f,g\right) }^{Z^{\perp }} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{\left( l,r\right) =1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,h\right)
,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\dsum\limits_{\left( k,c\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( k,c\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}E\left[
U_{\left( p,q\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left( f,g\right) }\varepsilon _{\left(
l,r\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( k,c\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &\frac{8}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \dsum\limits_{\left( l,r\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right) ^{2}\left( P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right) ^{2}E\left[ U_{\left( l,r\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left( l,r\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( l,r\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&&+\frac{8}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{\left( p,q\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( p,q\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right) ^{2} \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \dsum\limits_{\left( l,r\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right) ^{2}E\left[ U_{\left( p,q\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left( p,q\right) }|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{W}\right] E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( l,r\right) }^{2}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&&+\frac{16}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{\left( p,q\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left\vert P_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \dsum\limits_{\left( k,c\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left\vert P_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( k,c\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( k,c\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert E\left[
\left\vert U_{\left( l,r\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left( k,c\right) }\varepsilon
_{\left( l,r\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( k,c\right) }\right\vert |\mathcal{F%
}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\end{eqnarray*}%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&\leq &8\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{%
F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{1/2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{4}|\mathcal{%
F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{1/2} \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ }\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{3}%
\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&&+8\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{%
F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E%
\left[ \left\Vert U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2}%
\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&&+16\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{%
F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{1/2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{4}|\mathcal{%
F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{1/2} \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ }\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2}%
\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{3}}{n^{3}}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{%
K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right)
=O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
It follows from these calculations that 
\begin{eqnarray*}
0 &\leq &E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{3,2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{3,2,1}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] +E\left[ \mathcal{A%
}_{3,2,2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{%
n^{2}}\right) \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
Hence, there exists a constant $\overline{C}<\infty $ such that for all $n$
sufficiently large 
\begin{equation*}
E\left[ \frac{n}{K_{n}}\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{3,2}\right\vert \right] =E%
\left[ \frac{n}{K_{n}}\mathcal{A}_{3,2}\right] =E_{Z}\left( E\left[ \frac{n}{%
K_{n}}\mathcal{A}_{3,2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \leq \overline{C}%
\text{. \ }
\end{equation*}%
Application of the Markov's inequality then implies that, for any $\epsilon
>0$,%
\begin{equation*}
\Pr \left( \frac{n}{K_{n}}\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{3,2}\right\vert \geq \frac{%
\overline{C}}{\epsilon }\right) \leq \epsilon \frac{n}{K_{n}}\frac{E\left[ 
\mathcal{A}_{3,2}\right] }{\overline{C}}\leq \epsilon
\end{equation*}%
for all $n$ sufficiently large, which shows that%
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{A}_{3,2}=O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) \text{. }  \label{A32}
\end{equation}

Next, to show part (c), note that since $A$ is symmetric, so that $A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }=A_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }$,
it follows that $\mathcal{A}_{3,2}=\mathcal{A}_{3,3}$. Hence, using the same
argument as that given for part (b) above, we can show that%
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{A}_{3,3}=O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) \text{.}  \label{A33}
\end{equation}

Turning our attention to part (d), we apply the inequality $\left\vert
XY\right\vert \leq \left( 1/2\right) X^{2}+\left( 1/2\right) Y^{2}$ to
obtain 
\begin{eqnarray*}
0 &\leq &\mathcal{A}_{3,4} \\
&=&\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\right\vert e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}XX^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,h\right) }\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }%
\left. \text{\ }\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }XX^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left(
j,v\right) }\right\} \\
&=&\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\right\vert e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}UU^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,h\right) }\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \
\ \ }\left. \text{\ }\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }UU^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left(
j,v\right) }\right\} \\
&\leq &\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }UU^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left(
i,h\right) }\right) ^{2} \\
&&+\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }UU^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left(
j,v\right) }\right) ^{2} \\
&=&\mathcal{A}_{3,4,1}+\mathcal{A}_{3,4,2}
\end{eqnarray*}%
Focusing first on $\mathcal{A}_{3,4,1}$, note that by applying the
inequality $\left\vert \dsum\nolimits_{i=1}^{m}a_{i}\right\vert ^{r}\leq
m^{r-1}\dsum\nolimits_{i=1}^{m}\left\vert a_{i}\right\vert ^{r}$ and
following an argument similar to that given for $\mathcal{A}_{3,2}$ above,
we have%
\begin{eqnarray*}
0 &\leq &\mathcal{A}_{3,4,1} \\
&=&\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }UU^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left(
i,h\right) }\right) ^{2} \\
&=&\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left[ \dsum\limits_{b=1}^{d}%
\left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}Ue_{b,d}-e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}Ue_{b,d}\right) ^{2}\right] ^{2} \\
&\leq &\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \left[ 2e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}UU^{\prime }M^{Q}e_{\left( i,h\right) }+2e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}UU^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}e_{\left( i,h\right) }%
\right] ^{2} \\
&\leq &\frac{16}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}UU^{\prime }M^{Q}e_{\left( i,h\right) }\right) ^{2} \\
&&+\frac{16}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}UU^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}e_{\left( i,h\right)
}\right) ^{2} \\
&=&\mathcal{A}_{3,4,1,1}+\mathcal{A}_{3,4,1,2}
\end{eqnarray*}%
Applying the triangle inequality, part (a) of Lemma S2-1, as well as
Assumptions 2(i), 5, and 6; we obtain 
\begin{eqnarray*}
0 &\leq &E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{3,4,1,1}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\frac{16}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert E\left[ \left( e_{\left(
i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}UU^{\prime }M^{Q}e_{\left( i,h\right) }\right)
^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &\frac{16}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \dsum\limits_{r=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert M_{\left( i,h\right)
,\left( i,r\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
i,q\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \dsum\limits_{r=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert M_{\left(
i,h\right) ,\left( i,c\right) }^{Q}\right\vert E\left[ \left\vert U_{\left(
i,g\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left( i,r\right) }U_{\left( i,q\right) }^{\prime
}U_{\left( i,c\right) }\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &16\overline{T}^{4}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert
M_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{4}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert U_{\left(
i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \\
&&\times \frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( 1\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
Hence, there exists a constant $\overline{C}<\infty $ such that for all $n$
sufficiently large 
\begin{equation*}
E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{3,4,1,1}\right\vert \right] =E\left[ 
\mathcal{A}_{3,4,1,1}\right] =E_{W_{n}}\left( E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{3,4,1,1}|%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{W}\right] \right) \leq \overline{C}\text{. \ }
\end{equation*}%
Application of the Markov's inequality then implies that, for any $\epsilon
>0$,%
\begin{equation*}
\Pr \left( \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{3,4,1,1}\right\vert \geq \frac{\overline{C%
}}{\epsilon }\right) \leq \epsilon \frac{E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{3,4,1,1}\right]
}{\overline{C}}\leq \epsilon
\end{equation*}%
for all $n$ sufficiently large, which shows that%
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{3,4,1,1}=O_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{.}
\end{equation*}

Moreover, by applying part (a) of Lemma S2-1 as well as Assumptions 1, 2(i),
5, and 6; we have 
\begin{eqnarray*}
0 &\leq &E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{3,4,1,2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\frac{16}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}UU^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}e_{\left( i,h\right)
}\right) ^{2} \\
&=&\frac{16}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{\left( l,r\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\dsum\limits_{\left( k,c\right) =1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
k,c\right) }^{Z^{\perp }} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{\left( p,q\right) =1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,h\right)
,\left( p,q\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\dsum\limits_{\left( k,c\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( f,g\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}E\left[
U_{\left( l,r\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left( k,c\right) }U_{\left( p,q\right)
}^{\prime }U_{\left( f,g\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\frac{16}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{\left( l,r\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right) ^{4}E\left[ \left( U_{\left( l,r\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left(
l,r\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&&+\frac{16}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{\left( l,r\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right) ^{2} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( p,q\right) =1  \\ \left( p,q\right)
\neq \left( l,r\right) }}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
p,q\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2}E\left[ \left( U_{\left( l,r\right)
}^{\prime }U_{\left( l,r\right) }\right) |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[
\left( U_{\left( p,q\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left( p,q\right) }\right) |%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&&+\frac{32}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{\left( l,r\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right) ^{2} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( p,q\right) =1  \\ \left( p,q\right)
\neq \left( l,r\right) }}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
p,q\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2}E\left[ \left( U_{\left( l,r\right)
}^{\prime }U_{\left( p,q\right) }\right) |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[
\left( U_{\left( p,q\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left( l,r\right) }\right) |%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\end{eqnarray*}%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&\leq &16\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert
_{2}^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \left( \max_{1\leq \left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right) ^{3}\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&&+16\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert
_{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right) ^{2} \\
&&\text{ \ \ }\times \frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&&+32\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert
_{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left(
i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right) ^{2} \\
&&\text{ \ }\times \frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{3}}{n^{3}}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{%
K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right)
=O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) .
\end{eqnarray*}%
Hence, there exists a constant $\overline{C}<\infty $ such that for all $n$
sufficiently large 
\begin{equation*}
E\left[ \frac{n^{2}}{K_{n}^{2}}\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{3,4,1,2}\right\vert %
\right] =E\left[ \frac{n^{2}}{K_{n}^{2}}\mathcal{A}_{3,4,1,2}\right]
=E_{Z}\left( \frac{n^{2}}{K_{n}^{2}}E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{3,4,1,2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \leq \overline{C}\text{. \ }
\end{equation*}%
Application of the Markov's inequality then implies that, for any $\epsilon
>0$,%
\begin{equation*}
\Pr \left( \frac{n^{2}}{K_{n}^{2}}\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{3,4,1,2}\right%
\vert \geq \frac{\overline{C}}{\epsilon }\right) \leq \epsilon \frac{n^{2}}{%
K_{n}^{2}}\frac{E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{3,4,1,2}\right] }{\overline{C}}\leq
\epsilon
\end{equation*}%
for all $n$ sufficiently large, which shows that $\mathcal{A}%
_{3,4,1,2}=O_{p}\left( K_{n}^{2}/n^{2}\right) $. It follows that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{3,4,1} &\leq &\mathcal{A}_{3,4,1,1}+\mathcal{A}_{3,4,1,2} \\
&=&O_{p}\left( 1\right) +O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right)
=O_{p}\left( 1\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
In the same way, we can also show that $\mathcal{A}_{3,4,2}=O_{p}\left(
1\right) $, from which it further follows that%
\begin{equation}
0\leq \mathcal{A}_{3,4}\leq \mathcal{A}_{3,4,1}+\mathcal{A}%
_{3,4,2}=O_{p}\left( 1\right) +O_{p}\left( 1\right) =O_{p}\left( 1\right) .
\label{A34}
\end{equation}

Finally, consider part (e). Making use of the triangle inequality and the
inequality $\left\vert \dsum\nolimits_{i=1}^{m}a_{i}\right\vert ^{r}\leq
m^{r-1}\dsum\nolimits_{i=1}^{m}\left\vert a_{i}\right\vert ^{r}$, we can
write%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{3}\right\vert &\leq &\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right)
\neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \left[ e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon +e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ 
\widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right] ^{2} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\right\vert \left[ e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon +e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ 
\widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right] ^{2} \\
&\leq &\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&+\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \times \left( e_{\left(
i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] %
\left[ \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] ^{\prime }X^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,v\right) } \\
&&+\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] %
\left[ \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] ^{\prime }X^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,h\right) } \\
&&+\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \left[ \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right]
^{\prime }X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,h\right) }e_{\left(
j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{\delta }%
_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \left[ \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right]
^{\prime }X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( j,v\right) }
\end{eqnarray*}%
\begin{eqnarray}
&\leq &\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}  \notag \\
&&+\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}^{2}\frac{4}{%
K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\right\vert  \notag \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \left( e_{\left(
i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}e_{\left(
j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }XX^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}e_{\left( j,v\right) }  \notag \\
&&+\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}^{2}\frac{4}{%
K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\right\vert  \notag \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \left( e_{\left(
j,v\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}e_{\left(
i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }XX^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}e_{\left( i,h\right) }  \notag \\
&&+\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}^{4}\frac{4}{%
K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\right\vert e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}XX^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,h\right) }  \notag \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }XX^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left(
j,v\right) }  \notag \\
&=&\mathcal{A}_{3,1}+\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert
_{2}^{2}\mathcal{A}_{3,2}+\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta
_{0}\right\Vert _{2}^{2}\mathcal{A}_{3,3}+\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }%
_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}^{4}\mathcal{A}_{3,4}\text{,}  \label{A3 bd}
\end{eqnarray}%
where $\mathcal{A}_{3,1}$, $\mathcal{A}_{3,2}$, $\mathcal{A}_{3,3}$, and $%
\mathcal{A}_{3,4}$ are as defined in parts (a)-(d) above. It follows from
expressions (\ref{A31})-(\ref{A34}) that%
\begin{eqnarray}
\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{3}\right\vert &\leq &\mathcal{A}_{3,1}+\left\Vert 
\widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}^{2}\mathcal{A}%
