_{3,2}+\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}^{2}%
\mathcal{A}_{3,3}+\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert
_{2}^{4}\mathcal{A}_{3,4}  \notag \\
&=&O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) +o_{p}\left( 1\right)
O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) +o_{p}\left( 1\right) O_{p}\left( \frac{%
K_{n}}{n}\right) +o_{p}\left( 1\right) O_{p}\left( 1\right) =o_{p}\left(
1\right) \text{. }  \label{A3}
\end{eqnarray}

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma OA-17: }Let Assumptions 1-6 be satisfied, and let $%
\left\{ \widehat{\delta }_{n}\right\} $ be a sequence of estimators such that%
\begin{equation*}
\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}\overset{p}{%
\rightarrow }0\text{ as }n\rightarrow \infty \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
as long as $\sqrt{K_{2,n}}/\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}\rightarrow 0$%
. Then, the following statements are true.

\begin{enumerate}
\item[(a)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{4,1}=O_{p}\left( \sqrt{\frac{K_{n}}{n}}\right) =o_{p}\left(
1\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{4,1} &=&-\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left(
e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) \left(
e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \
\ \ \ \ }\left. \times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,v\right) }\left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon
\right) ^{2}\right\}
\end{eqnarray*}

\item[(b)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{4,2}=o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{4,2} &=&-\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left(
e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{%
\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right) \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \
\ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \text{\ \ }\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\right\}
\end{eqnarray*}

\item[(c)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{4}=o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{4} &=&-\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\left(
e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\right. \\
&&\text{\ }\left. \times \dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( i,h\right) }\left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon +e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ 
\widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right) \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \right\}
\end{eqnarray*}
\end{enumerate}

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma OA-17:}

To show part (a), note first that we can decompose $\mathcal{A}_{4,1}$ as 
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{4,1} &=&-\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right)
\left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&=&-\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ s,t=1 
\\ s\neq t}}^{T_{i}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\dsum\limits_{r=1}^{T_{i}}P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,r\right)
}^{Z^{\perp }}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
i,g\right) }^{Q}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,s\right) ,\left(
i,v\right) } \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times
\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,v\right) ,\left( i,q\right)
}^{Q}\dsum\limits_{c=1}^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,v\right) ,\left( i,c\right)
}^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( i,r\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( i,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,c\right) } \\
&&-\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ s,t=1  \\ %
s\neq t}}^{T_{i}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( l,r\right) =1  \\ l\neq i}}%
^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right)
}^{Q}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,s\right) ,\left( i,v\right) } \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times
\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,v\right) ,\left( i,q\right)
}^{Q}\dsum\limits_{c=1}^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,v\right) ,\left( i,c\right)
}^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( l,r\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( i,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,c\right) } \\
&&-\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq j}}%
^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( i,h\right) }\dsum\limits_{r=1}^{T_{i}}P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
i,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,h\right)
,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,v\right) } \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times
\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right)
}^{Q}\dsum\limits_{c=1}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,c\right)
}^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( i,r\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,c\right) } \\
&&-\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq j}}%
^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( i,h\right) }\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
i,g\right) }^{Q}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\dsum\limits_{r=1}^{T_{j}}P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
j,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp }} \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times
\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right)
}^{Q}\dsum\limits_{c=1}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,c\right)
}^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,r\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,c\right) } \\
&&-\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq j}}%
^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( i,h\right) }\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
i,g\right) }^{Q}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( l,r\right) =1  \\ l\neq i,j}}%
^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp }} \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times
\dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right)
}^{Q}\dsum\limits_{c=1}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,c\right)
}^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( l,r\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,c\right) } \\
&=&\mathcal{A}_{4,1,1}+\mathcal{A}_{4,1,2}+\mathcal{A}_{4,1,3}+\mathcal{A}%
_{4,1,4}+\mathcal{A}_{4,1,5}
\end{eqnarray*}%
Consider first $\mathcal{A}_{4,1,1}$. Applying the triangle inequality, part
(f) of Lemma S2-1, and Assumptions 2(i), 5, and 6; we obtain%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{4,1,1}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \\
&\leq &\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ s,t=1 
\\ s\neq t}}^{T_{i}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{r=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert P_{\left(
i,h\right) ,\left( i,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,s\right)
,\left( i,v\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert M_{\left( i,v\right) ,\left(
i,q\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \dsum\limits_{c=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert M_{\left(
i,v\right) ,\left( i,c\right) }^{Q}\right\vert E\left[ \left\vert
\varepsilon _{\left( i,r\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( i,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,c\right)
}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &2\overline{T}^{4}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert
M_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{3}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \\
&&\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) \frac{1}{K_{2,n}}%
\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ s,t=1  \\ s\neq t}}%
^{T_{i}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,s\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}K_{2,n}}{n^{2}}\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
Next, consider $\mathcal{A}_{4,1,2}$. Here, by applying the triangle
inequality, parts (f) and (g) of Lemma S2-1, and Assumptions 1, 2(i), 5, and
6; we get 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{4,1,2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&E\left[ \left( \frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ s,t=1  \\ s\neq t}}^{T_{i}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,s\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( l,r\right) =1  \\ l\neq i}}%
^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right)
}^{Q}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,s\right) ,\left( i,v\right)
}\right. \right. \\
&&\left. \left. \times \dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,v\right)
,\left( i,q\right) }^{Q}\dsum\limits_{c=1}^{T_{i}}M_{\left( i,v\right)
,\left( i,c\right) }^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( l,r\right) }\varepsilon
_{\left( i,g\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left(
i,c\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &\left\{ \frac{4}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{i_{1}=1}^{n}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ s_{1},t_{1}=1  \\ s_{1}\neq t_{1}}}^{T_{i_{1}}}A_{\left(
i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left( i_{1},s_{1}\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{i_{2}=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ s_{2},t_{2}=1  \\ %
s_{2}\neq t_{2}}}^{T_{i_{2}}}A_{\left( i_{2},t_{2}\right) ,\left(
i_{2},s_{2}\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left( i_{1},h_{1}\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{h_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\left\vert J_{\left( i_{2},t_{2}\right)
,\left( i_{2},h_{2}\right) }\right\vert \right. \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{\left( l,r\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left\vert P_{\left(
i,h_{1}\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}P_{\left( i,h_{2}\right)
,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{g_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\left\vert M_{\left( i_{1},h_{1}\right)
,\left( i_{1},g_{1}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{g_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\left\vert M_{\left( i_{2},h_{2}\right)
,\left( i_{2},g_{2}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{v_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\left\vert J_{\left( i_{1},s_{1}\right)
,\left( i_{1},v_{1}\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\left\vert J_{\left(
i_{2},s_{2}\right) ,\left( i_{2},v_{2}\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{q_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\left\vert M_{\left( i_{1},v_{1}\right)
,\left( i_{1},q_{1}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{q_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\left\vert M_{\left( i_{2},v_{2}\right)
,\left( i_{2},q_{2}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{c_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\left\vert M_{\left( i_{1},v_{1}\right)
,\left( i_{1},c_{1}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{c_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\left\vert M_{\left( i_{2},v_{2}\right)
,\left( i_{2},c_{2}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \\
&&\left. \times E\left[ \left\vert \varepsilon _{\left( l,r\right)
}^{2}\varepsilon _{\left( i_{1},g_{1}\right) }\varepsilon _{\left(
i_{1},q_{1}\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i_{1},c_{1}\right) }\varepsilon
_{\left( i_{2},g_{2}\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i_{2},q_{2}\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( i_{2},c_{2}\right) }\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \right\} \\
&&+\left\{ \frac{4}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{i_{1}=1}^{n}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ s_{1},t_{1}=1  \\ s_{1}\neq t_{1}}}^{T_{i_{1}}}A_{\left(
i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left( i_{1},s_{1}\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{i_{2}=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ s_{2},t_{2}=1  \\ %
s_{2}\neq t_{2}}}^{T_{i_{2}}}A_{\left( i_{2},t_{2}\right) ,\left(
i_{2},s_{2}\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left( i_{1},h_{1}\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{h_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\left\vert J_{\left( i_{2},t_{2}\right)
,\left( i_{2},h_{2}\right) }\right\vert \right. \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{r_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\left\vert P_{\left(
i_{1},h_{1}\right) ,\left( i_{2},r_{1}\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{r_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\left\vert P_{\left( i_{2},h_{2}\right)
,\left( i_{1},r_{2}\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{g_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\left\vert M_{\left( i_{1},h_{1}\right)
,\left( i_{1},g_{1}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{g_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\left\vert M_{\left( i_{2},h_{2}\right)
,\left( i_{2},g_{2}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\left\vert J_{\left(
i_{1},s_{1}\right) ,\left( i_{1},v_{1}\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{v_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\left\vert J_{\left( i_{2},s_{2}\right)
,\left( i_{2},v_{2}\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{q_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\left\vert M_{\left( i_{1},v_{1}\right)
,\left( i_{1},q_{1}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{q_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\left\vert M_{\left(
i_{2},v_{2}\right) ,\left( i_{2},q_{2}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{c_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\left\vert M_{\left( i_{1},v_{1}\right)
,\left( i_{1},c_{1}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{c_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\left\vert M_{\left( i_{2},v_{2}\right)
,\left( i_{2},c_{2}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \\
&&\left. \times E\left[ \left\vert \varepsilon _{\left( i_{1},r_{2}\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( i_{1},g_{1}\right) }\varepsilon _{\left(
i_{1},q_{1}\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i_{1},c_{1}\right) }\varepsilon
_{\left( i_{2},r_{1}\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i_{2},g_{2}\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( i_{2},q_{2}\right) }\varepsilon _{\left(
i_{2},c_{2}\right) }\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right\}
\end{eqnarray*}%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&\leq &\left\{ 4\overline{T}^{6}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{4}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert
M_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{6}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{8}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \left( \max_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right)
}^{Z^{\perp }}\right) \right. \\
&&\left. \times \frac{1}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ s_{1},t_{1}=1  \\ s_{1}\neq t_{1}}}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ s_{2},t_{2}=1  \\ s_{2}\neq t_{2}}}^{T_{i}}A_{\left(
i,t_{1}\right) ,\left( i,s_{1}\right) }^{2}A_{\left( i,t_{2}\right) ,\left(
i,s_{2}\right) }^{2}\right\} \\
&&+\left\{ 4\overline{T}^{8}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{4}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert
M_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{6}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{8}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \right. \\
&&\left. \times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2}\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}%
\dsum\limits_{i_{1}=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ s_{1},t_{1}=1  \\ %
s_{1}\neq t_{1}}}^{T_{i_{1}}}A_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left(
i_{1},s_{1}\right) }^{2}\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i_{2}=1 
\\ i_{2}\neq i_{1}}}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ s_{2},t_{2}=1  \\ s_{2}\neq
t_{2}}}^{T_{i_{2}}}A_{\left( i_{2},t_{2}\right) ,\left( i_{2},s_{2}\right)
}^{2}\right\} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n^{3}}\right)
+O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right)
=O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\frac{K_{2,n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
Now, consider $\mathcal{A}_{4,1,3}$. In this case, we can apply the triangle
inequality, part (a) of Lemma S2-1, and Assumptions 2(i), 5, and 6 to get 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{4,1,3}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \\
&\leq &\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq j}}%
^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{r=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,r\right)
}^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert \dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert M_{\left(
i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert M_{\left(
j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{c=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,c\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert E\left[ \left\vert \varepsilon _{\left( i,r\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( j,c\right) }\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &2\overline{T}^{4}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert
M_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{3}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) \\
&&\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \frac{1}{K_{2,n}%
}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq j}}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}%
\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
Turning our attention to $\mathcal{A}_{4,1,4}$, note that, by applying the
triangle inequality, part (a) of Lemma S2-1, and Assumptions 2(i), 5, and 6;
we obtain 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{4,1,4}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \\
&\leq &\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq j}}%
^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{r=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
j,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert \dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{c=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,c\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert E\left[ \left\vert \varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( j,r\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( j,c\right) }\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &2\overline{T}^{4}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert
M_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{3}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) \\
&&\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \frac{1}{K_{2,n}%
}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq j}}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}%
\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) \text{. }
\end{eqnarray*}%
Finally, consider%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{4,1,5}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&E\left[ \left( \frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i,j=1  \\ i\neq
j }}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s=1}^{T_{j}}A_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}M_{\left(
i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( l,r\right) =1 
\\ l\neq i,j}}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right. \right. \\
&&\left. \left. \times \dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right)
,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}\dsum\limits_{c=1}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right)
,\left( j,c\right) }^{Q}\varepsilon _{\left( l,r\right) }\varepsilon
_{\left( i,g\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left(
j,c\right) }\right) ^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\end{eqnarray*}%
In this case, note that, by applying the triangle and Jensen's inequalites,
parts (a) and (e) of Lemma S2-1, and Assumptions 1, 2(i), 5, and 6; we
obtain 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{4,1,5}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &\frac{4}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i_{1},j_{1}=1  \\ %
i_{1}\neq j_{1}}}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\dsum%
\limits_{s_{1}=1}^{T_{j_{1}}}A_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left(
j_{1},s_{1}\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i_{2},j_{2}=1  \\ i_{2}\neq
j_{2}}}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\dsum%
\limits_{s_{2}=1}^{T_{j_{2}}}A_{\left( i_{2},t_{2}\right) ,\left(
j_{2},s_{2}\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left( i_{1},h_{1}\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{h_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\left\vert J_{\left( i_{2},t_{2}\right)
,\left( i_{2},h_{2}\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v_{1}=1}^{T_{j_{1}}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j_{1},s_{1}\right) ,\left( j_{1},v_{1}\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{v_{2}=1}^{T_{j_{2}}}J_{\left( j_{2},s_{2}\right) ,\left(
j_{2},v_{2}\right) }\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( l,r\right) =1  \\ l\neq
i_{1},j_{1},i_{2},j_{2}}}^{m_{n}}\left\vert P_{\left( i_{1},h_{1}\right)
,\left( l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}P_{\left( i_{2},h_{2}\right) ,\left(
l,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{g_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\left\vert M_{\left( i_{1},h_{1}\right)
,\left( i_{1},g_{1}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{g_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\left\vert M_{\left(
i_{2},h_{2}\right) ,\left( i_{2},g_{2}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{q_{1}=1}^{T_{j_{1}}}\left\vert M_{\left( j_{1},v_{1}\right)
,\left( j_{1},q_{1}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{q_{2}=1}^{T_{j_{2}}}\left\vert M_{\left( j_{2},v_{2}\right)
,\left( j_{2},q_{2}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{c_{1}=1}^{T_{j_{1}}}\left\vert M_{\left( j_{1},v_{1}\right)
,\left( j_{1},c_{1}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{c_{2}=1}^{T_{j_{2}}}\left\vert M_{\left(
j_{2},v_{2}\right) ,\left( j_{2},c_{2}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert E\left[
\left\vert \varepsilon _{\left( l,r\right) }^{2}\varepsilon _{\left(
i_{1},g_{1}\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j_{1},q_{1}\right) }\varepsilon
_{\left( j_{1},c_{1}\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i_{2},g_{2}\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( j_{2},q_{2}\right) }\varepsilon _{\left(
j_{2},c_{2}\right) }\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&&+\frac{4}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i_{1},j_{1}=1  \\ i_{1}\neq
j_{1}}}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\dsum%
\limits_{s_{1}=1}^{T_{j_{1}}}A_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left(
j_{1},s_{1}\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i_{2},j_{2}=1  \\ i_{2}\neq
j_{2},i_{1}}}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\dsum%
\limits_{s_{2}=1}^{T_{j_{2}}}A_{\left( i_{2},t_{2}\right) ,\left(
j_{2},s_{2}\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left( i_{1},h_{1}\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{h_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\left\vert J_{\left( i_{2},t_{2}\right)
,\left( i_{2},h_{2}\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v_{1}=1}^{T_{j_{1}}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j_{1},s_{1}\right) ,\left( j_{1},v_{1}\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{v_{2}=1}^{T_{j_{2}}}\left\vert J_{\left( j_{2},s_{2}\right)
,\left( j_{2},v_{2}\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{g_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\left\vert M_{\left( i_{1},h_{1}\right)
,\left( i_{1},g_{1}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{g_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\left\vert M_{\left( i_{2},h_{2}\right)
,\left( i_{2},g_{2}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{q_{1}=1}^{T_{j_{1}}}\left\vert M_{\left( j_{1},v_{1}\right)
,\left( j_{1},q_{1}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{q_{2}=1}^{T_{j_{2}}}\left\vert M_{\left(
j_{2},v_{2}\right) ,\left( j_{2},q_{2}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{c_{1}=1}^{T_{j_{1}}}\left\vert M_{\left( j_{1},v_{1}\right)
,\left( j_{1},c_{1}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{c_{2}=1}^{T_{j_{2}}}\left\vert M_{\left( j_{2},v_{2}\right)
,\left( j_{2},c_{2}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{g_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\left\vert P_{\left( i_{1},h_{1}\right)
,\left( i_{2},g_{2}\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{g_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\left\vert P_{\left(
i_{2},h_{2}\right) ,\left( i_{1},g_{1}\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert E 
\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i_{1},g_{1}\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( i_{2},g_{2}\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ \left\vert \varepsilon _{\left( j_{1},q_{1}\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( j_{1},c_{1}\right) }\varepsilon _{\left(
j_{2},q_{2}\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j_{2},c_{2}\right) }\right\vert |%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&&+\frac{4}{K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ %
j_{1}=1  \\ j_{1}\neq i}}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\dsum%
\limits_{s_{1}=1}^{T_{j_{1}}}A_{\left( i,t_{1}\right) ,\left(
j_{1},s_{1}\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ j_{2}=1  \\ j_{2}\neq
i,j_{1} }}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\dsum%
\limits_{s_{2}=1}^{T_{j_{2}}}A_{\left( i,t_{2}\right) ,\left(
j_{2},s_{2}\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h_{1}=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left(
i,t_{1}\right) ,\left( i,h_{1}\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{h_{2}=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t_{2}\right) ,\left(
i,h_{2}\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v_{1}=1}^{T_{j_{1}}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j_{1},s_{1}\right) ,\left( j_{1},v_{1}\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{v_{2}=1}^{T_{j_{2}}}\left\vert J_{\left( j_{2},s_{2}\right)
,\left( j_{2},v_{2}\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert
M_{\left( i,h_{1}\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert
M_{\left( i,h_{2}\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{q_{1}=1}^{T_{j_{1}}}\left\vert M_{\left( j_{1},v_{1}\right)
,\left( j_{1},q_{1}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{q_{2}=1}^{T_{j_{2}}}\left\vert M_{\left(
j_{2},v_{2}\right) ,\left( j_{2},q_{2}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{c_{1}=1}^{T_{j_{1}}}\left\vert M_{\left( j_{1},v_{1}\right)
,\left( j_{1},c_{1}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{c_{2}=1}^{T_{j_{2}}}\left\vert M_{\left( j_{2},v_{2}\right)
,\left( j_{2},c_{2}\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{r_{1}=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert P_{\left( i,h_{1}\right) ,\left(
j_{2},r_{1}\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{r_{2}=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert P_{\left( i,h_{2}\right)
,\left( j_{1},r_{2}\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert E\left[ \left\vert
\varepsilon _{\left( j_{1},r_{2}\right) }\varepsilon _{\left(
j_{1},q_{1}\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j_{1},c_{1}\right) }\right\vert |%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ \left\vert \varepsilon _{\left(
j_{2},r_{1}\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j_{2},q_{2}\right) }\varepsilon
_{\left( j_{2},c_{2}\right) }\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[
\varepsilon _{\left( i,g\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\end{eqnarray*}%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&\leq &\frac{4\overline{T}^{6}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{4}}{%
K_{2,n}^{2}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i_{1},j_{1}=1  \\ i_{1}\neq j_{1}}}%
^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\dsum\limits_{s_{1}=1}^{T_{j_{1}}}A_{%
\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left( j_{1},s_{1}\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ i_{2},j_{2}=1  \\ i_{2}\neq j_{2}}}^{n}\dsum%
\limits_{t_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\dsum\limits_{s_{2}=1}^{T_{j_{2}}}A_{\left(
i_{2},t_{2}\right) ,\left( j_{2},s_{2}\right) }^{2} \\
&&\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq
m_{n}}\left\vert M_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\right) ^{6}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[
\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{8}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right)
\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) \\
&&+\frac{4\overline{T}^{8}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{4}}{K_{2,n}^{2}%
}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ i_{1},j_{1}=1  \\ i_{1}\neq j_{1}}}%
^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{1}=1}^{T_{i_{1}}}\dsum\limits_{s_{1}=1}^{T_{j_{1}}}A_{%
\left( i_{1},t_{1}\right) ,\left( j_{1},s_{1}\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ i_{2},j_{2}=1  \\ i_{2}\neq j_{2}}}^{n}\dsum%
\limits_{t_{2}=1}^{T_{i_{2}}}\dsum\limits_{s_{2}=1}^{T_{j_{2}}}A_{\left(
i_{2},t_{2}\right) ,\left( j_{2},s_{2}\right) }^{2} \\
&&\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq
m_{n}}\left\vert M_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert
\right) ^{6}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[
\varepsilon _{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2}
\\
&&\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2} \\
&&+\frac{4\overline{T}^{7}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{4}}{K_{2,n}^{2}%
}\dsum\limits_{i=1}^{n}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ j_{1}=1  \\ j_{1}\neq i}}%
^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{1}=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{s_{1}=1}^{T_{j_{1}}}A_{%
\left( i,t_{1}\right) ,\left( j_{1},s_{1}\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ j_{2}=1  \\ j_{2}\neq i}}^{n}\dsum\limits_{t_{2}=1}^{T_{i}}%
\dsum\limits_{s_{2}=1}^{T_{j_{2}}}A_{\left( i,t_{2}\right) ,\left(
j_{2},s_{2}\right) }^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert M_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{6} \\
&&\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \left( \max_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right)
}^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{%
n^{2}}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{3}}\right) =O_{a.s.}\left( 
\frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) \text{.}
\end{eqnarray*}%
It follows from these calculations and from Liapunov's inequality that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{4,1}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\\
&\leq &E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{4,1,1}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] +E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{4,1,2}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}%
_{n}^{Z}\right] +E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{4,1,3}\right\vert |\mathcal{%
F}_{n}^{Z}\right] +E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{4,1,4}\right\vert |%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&&+E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{4,1,5}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \\
&\leq &E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{4,1,1}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] +\sqrt{E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{4,1,2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] }+E%
\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{4,1,3}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
+E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{4,1,4}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \\
&&+\sqrt{E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{4,1,5}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] } \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}K_{2,n}}{n^{2}}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{%
K_{n}K_{2,n}}{n^{2}}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right)
+O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \sqrt{\frac{K_{n}}{n}}%
\right) \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \sqrt{\frac{K_{n}}{n}}\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
Hence, there exists a constant $\overline{C}<\infty $ such that for all $n$
sufficiently large 
\begin{equation*}
E\left[ \sqrt{\frac{n}{K_{n}}}\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{4,1}\right\vert \right]
=E_{Z}\left( \sqrt{\frac{n}{K_{n}}}E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}%
_{4,1}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \leq \overline{C}\text{%
. \ }
\end{equation*}%
It follows from the Markov's inequality that for any $\epsilon >0$,%
\begin{equation*}
\Pr \left( \left\vert \sqrt{\frac{n}{K_{n}}}\mathcal{A}_{4,1}\right\vert
\geq \frac{\overline{C}}{\epsilon }\right) \leq \epsilon \sqrt{\frac{n}{K_{n}%
}}\frac{E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{4,1}\right\vert \right] }{\overline{C%
}}\leq \epsilon
\end{equation*}%
for all $n$ sufficiently large, which shows that%
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{A}_{4,1}=O_{p}\left( \sqrt{\frac{K_{n}}{n}}\right)  \label{A41}
\end{equation}

Turning our attention to part (b), note that, here, we can apply the
triangle and CS inequalities and the inequality $\left\vert XY\right\vert
\leq \left( 1/2\right) X^{2}+\left( 1/2\right) Y^{2}$ to obtain%
\begin{eqnarray}
\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{4,2}\right\vert &\leq &\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right)
\neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right]
\right) \left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right)
\right\vert  \notag \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}  \notag \\
&\leq &\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}  \notag \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \sqrt{e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \left[ \widehat{%
\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] ^{\prime }X^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}e_{\left( i,h\right) }}  \notag \\
&&\times \sqrt{e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \varepsilon
^{\prime }M^{Q}e_{\left( i,h\right) }}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left(
j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}  \notag \\
&\leq &\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}\frac{1}{%
K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }XX^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left(
i,h\right) }  \notag \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}  \notag \\
&&+\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}\frac{1}{%
K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \varepsilon ^{\prime }M^{Q}e_{\left( i,h\right) }  \notag
\\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}  \notag \\
&=&\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}\left( 
\mathcal{A}_{4,2,1}+\mathcal{A}_{4,2,2}\right) \text{, }  \label{A42 bd}
\end{eqnarray}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{4,2,1} &=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}XX^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,h\right) } \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\text{,} \\
\mathcal{A}_{4,2,2} &=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon
\varepsilon ^{\prime }M^{Q}e_{\left( i,h\right)
}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}
\end{eqnarray*}

Next, observe that%
\begin{eqnarray*}
0 &\leq &\mathcal{A}_{4,2,1} \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ }\times e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}UU^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,h\right) } \\
&\leq &\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}UU^{\prime }M^{Q}e_{\left( i,h\right) } \\
&&+\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime
}P^{Z^{\perp }}UU^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}e_{\left( i,h\right) } \\
&=&\mathcal{A}_{4,2,1,1}+\mathcal{A}_{4,2,1,2},\text{ }\left( say\right) 
\text{.}
\end{eqnarray*}%
Considering first $\mathcal{A}_{4,2,1,1}$. Applying part (a) of Lemma S2-1
and Assumptions 2(i) and 6; we get%
\begin{eqnarray*}
0 &\leq &E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{4,2,1,1}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert E\left[ \left( e_{\left(
j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}UU^{\prime }M^{Q}e_{\left( i,h\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \\
&\leq &\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{r=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert M_{\left(
i,h\right) ,\left( i,g\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert M_{\left(
i,h\right) ,\left( i,r\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{c=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,q\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert
M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,c\right) }^{Q}\right\vert E\left[ \left\vert
\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,c\right) }U_{\left(
i,g\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left( i,r\right) }\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \\
&\leq &2\overline{T}^{4}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert
M_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{4}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{1/2} \\
&&\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert
U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\right) ^{1/2}\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( 1\right) \text{.}
\end{eqnarray*}%
In addition, for $E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{4,2,1,2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] $%
, we have, by straightforward calculations using Assumption 1 and the
triangle inequality, 
\begin{eqnarray}
0 &\leq &E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{4,2,1,2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]  \notag \\
&=&\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert  \notag \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\right\vert E\left[ \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}UU^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}e_{\left( i,h\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\notag \\
&=&\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{j}}\dsum\limits_{r=1}^{T_{j}}M_{\left( j,v\right)
,\left( j,g\right) }^{Q}M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,r\right) }^{Q}  \notag
\\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \dsum\limits_{\left( k,q\right)
=1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( k,q\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\dsum\limits_{\left( l,c\right) =1}^{m_{n}}P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left(
l,c\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( j,g\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( j,r\right) }U_{\left( k,q\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left(
l,c\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]  \notag \\
&\leq &\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \right.  \notag \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \left.
\dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{j}}\left( M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,g\right)
}^{Q}\right) ^{2}\left( P_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( j,g\right) }^{Z^{\perp
}}\right) ^{2}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left( j,g\right) }^{2}U_{\left(
j,g\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left( j,g\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\right\}  \notag \\
&&+\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{j}}\left( M_{\left(
j,v\right) ,\left( j,g\right) }^{Q}\right) ^{2}\right.  \notag \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left.
\times \dsum\limits_{\left( k,q\right) =1}^{m_{n}}\left( P_{\left(
i,h\right) ,\left( k,q\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2}E\left[ \varepsilon
_{\left( j,g\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] E\left[ U_{\left(
k,q\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left( k,q\right) }|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\right\}  \notag \\
&&+\frac{4}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\right\vert \dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{i}}\dsum\limits_{r=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert
M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,g\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \left\vert
M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left( j,r\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right.  \notag \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \times \dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert \left\vert P_{\left(
i,h\right) ,\left( j,g\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert \left\vert P_{\left(
i,h\right) ,\left( j,r\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right\vert E\left[ \left\vert
\varepsilon _{\left( j,g\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,r\right) }U_{\left(
j,g\right) }^{\prime }U_{\left( j,r\right) }\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \right\}  \label{EA4212 bd}
\end{eqnarray}%
Applying the CS inequality to (\ref{EA4212 bd}) and making use of part (a)
of Lemma S2-1 as well as Assumptions 2(i), 5, and 6; we then obtain 
\begin{eqnarray*}
&&E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{4,2,1,2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &2\overline{T}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert M_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{1/2} \\
&&\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \left\Vert
U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right]
\right) ^{1/2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2}\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}%
\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left(
i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&&+2\overline{T}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert M_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \\
&&\text{ \ }\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[
\left\Vert U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \right) \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}P_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) \frac{1}{K_{2,n}}%
\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left(
i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&&+4\overline{T}^{2}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left( \max_{1\leq
\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert M_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) ^{1/2} \\
&&\text{ \ \ }\times \left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[
\left\Vert U_{\left( i,t\right) }\right\Vert _{2}^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \right) ^{1/2}\left( \max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq
m_{n}}P_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,t\right) }^{Z^{\perp }}\right) ^{2}%
\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}%
}{n}\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}^{2}}{n^{2}}\right) =O_{a.s.}\left( 
\frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) =o_{a.s.}\left( 1\right) .
\end{eqnarray*}%
It follows from these calculations that 
\begin{eqnarray*}
0 &\leq &E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{4,2,1}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{4,2,1,1}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] +E\left[ 
\mathcal{A}_{4,2,1,2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( 1\right) +O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( 1\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
Hence, there exists a constant $\overline{C}<\infty $ such that for all $n$
sufficiently large 
\begin{equation*}
E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{4,2,1}\right\vert \right] =E\left[ \mathcal{A%
}_{4,2,1}\right] =E_{Z}\left( E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{4,2,1}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \right) \leq \overline{C}\text{. \ }
\end{equation*}%
Application of the Markov's inequality then implies that, for any $\epsilon
>0$,%
\begin{equation*}
\Pr \left( \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{4,2,1}\right\vert \geq \frac{\overline{C}%
}{\epsilon }\right) \leq \epsilon \frac{E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{4,2,1}\right] }{%
\overline{C}}\leq \epsilon
\end{equation*}%
for all $n$ sufficiently large, which shows that%
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{A}_{4,2,1}=O_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{.}  \label{A421 term}
\end{equation}

In addition, applying the triangle inequality, part (a) of Lemma S2-1, as
well as Assumptions 2(i), 5, and 6; we obtain%
\begin{eqnarray*}
0 &\leq &E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{4,2,2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{r=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert M_{\left( i,h\right) ,\left( i,r\right)
}^{Q}\right\vert \dsum\limits_{c=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert M_{\left( i,h\right)
,\left( i,c\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{q=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert M_{\left( j,v\right) ,\left(
j,q\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \dsum\limits_{g=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert M_{\left(
j,v\right) ,\left( j,g\right) }^{Q}\right\vert E\left[ \left\vert
\varepsilon _{\left( i,r\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( i,c\right)
}\varepsilon _{\left( j,q\right) }\varepsilon _{\left( j,g\right)
}\right\vert |\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \\
&\leq &\overline{T}^{4}\left\Vert J\right\Vert _{\infty }^{2}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) \leq m_{n}}\left\vert
M_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{Q}\right\vert \right) ^{4}\left(
\max_{1\leq \left( i,t\right) \leq m_{n}}E\left[ \varepsilon _{\left(
i,t\right) }^{4}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \frac{1}{K_{2,n}}%
\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left(
i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) }^{2} \\
&=&O_{a.s.}\left( 1\right)
\end{eqnarray*}%
Hence, there exists a constant $\overline{C}<\infty $ such that for all $n$
sufficiently large 
\begin{equation*}
E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{4,2,2}\right\vert \right] =E\left[ \mathcal{A%
}_{4,2,2}\right] =E_{Z}\left( E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{4,2,2}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}%
\right] \right) \leq \overline{C}\text{. \ }
\end{equation*}%
It follows from the Markov's inequality that for any $\epsilon >0$,%
\begin{equation*}
\Pr \left( \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{4,2,2}\right\vert \geq \frac{\overline{C}%
}{\epsilon }\right) \leq \epsilon \frac{E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}%
_{4,2,2}\right\vert \right] }{\overline{C}}\leq \epsilon
\end{equation*}%
for all $n$ sufficiently large, which shows that%
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{A}_{4,2,2}=O_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{.}  \label{A422 term}
\end{equation}

It follows from expressions (\ref{A42 bd})-(\ref{A422 term}) that 
\begin{equation}
\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{4,2}\right\vert \leq \left\Vert \widehat{\delta }%
_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}\left[ \mathcal{A}_{4,2,1}+\mathcal{A}%
_{4,2,2}\right] =o_{p}\left( 1\right) \left[ O_{p}\left( 1\right)
+O_{p}\left( 1\right) \right] =o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{.}  \label{A42}
\end{equation}

Finally, for part (c), note that we can write%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{4} &=&-\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon +e_{\left(
i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{\delta }%
_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right) \left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \\
&=&-\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right)
\left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&-\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ 
\widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right) \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&=&\mathcal{A}_{4,1}+\mathcal{A}_{4,2}\text{, }
\end{eqnarray*}%
where $\mathcal{A}_{4,1}$ and $\mathcal{A}_{4,2}$ are as defined in parts
(a) and (b) above. It follows from expressions (\ref{A41}) and (\ref{A42})
that%
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{A}_{4}=\mathcal{A}_{4,1}+\mathcal{A}_{4,2}=O_{p}\left( \sqrt{\frac{%
K_{n}}{n}}\right) +o_{p}\left( 1\right) =o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{. }%
\square \text{\textit{\ }}  \label{A4}
\end{equation}

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma OA-18: }Let Assumptions 1-6 be satisfied, and let $%
\left\{ \widehat{\delta }_{n}\right\} $ be a sequence of estimators such that%
\begin{equation*}
\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}\overset{p}{%
\rightarrow }\text{ }0\text{ as }n\rightarrow \infty \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
as long as $\sqrt{K_{2,n}}/\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}\rightarrow 0$%
. Then, the following statements are true.

\begin{enumerate}
\item[(a)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{5,1}=O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) =o_{p}\left( 1\right) 
\text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{5,1}=\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\text{.}
\end{equation*}

\item[(b)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{5,2}=O_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{5,2} &=&\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\right\vert e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}XX^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,h\right) }\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \
\ \ }\left. \times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\right\}
\end{eqnarray*}

\item[(c)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{5}=o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{5} &=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left(
e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon +e_{\left(
i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{\delta }%
_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right) ^{2}\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \
\ }\left. \times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right)
^{2}\right\}
\end{eqnarray*}
\end{enumerate}

\bigskip

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma OA-18:}

To show part (a), note that $\mathcal{A}_{5,1}$ is of the same form as $%
\mathcal{A}_{2,1,1}$, so from expression (\ref{EA211}), we have that%
\begin{equation*}
E\left[ \mathcal{A}_{5,1}|\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] =O_{a.s.}\left( \frac{%
K_{n}}{n}\right) \text{.}
\end{equation*}%
Hence, there exists a constant $\overline{C}<\infty $ such that for all $n$
sufficiently large 
\begin{equation*}
E\left[ \frac{n}{K_{n}}\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{5,1}\right\vert \right]
=E_{Z}\left( \frac{n}{K_{n}}E\left[ \left\vert \mathcal{A}_{5,1}\right\vert |%
\mathcal{F}_{n}^{Z}\right] \right) \leq \overline{C}\text{. \ }
\end{equation*}%
It follows from the Markov's inequality that for any $\epsilon >0$,%
\begin{equation*}
\Pr \left( \left\vert \frac{n}{K_{n}}\mathcal{A}_{5,1}\right\vert \geq \frac{%
\overline{C}}{\epsilon }\right) \leq \epsilon \frac{n}{K_{n}}\frac{E\left[
\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{5,1}\right\vert \right] }{\overline{C}}\leq \epsilon
\end{equation*}%
for all $n$ sufficiently large, which shows that%
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{A}_{5,1}=O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) \text{.}  \label{A51}
\end{equation}

For part (b), note that$\mathcal{A}_{5,2}$ is of the same form as $\mathcal{A%
}_{2,2,2}$, so that by expression (\ref{A222}), we have that%
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{A}_{5,2}=O_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{. }  \label{A52}
\end{equation}

Finally, onsider part (c). Applying the triangle inequality and the
inequality $\left\vert \dsum\nolimits_{i=1}^{m}a_{i}\right\vert ^{r}\leq
m^{r-1}\dsum\nolimits_{i=1}^{m}\left\vert a_{i}\right\vert ^{r}$, we obtain%
\begin{eqnarray}
\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{5}\right\vert &\leq &\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right)
\neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \left[ e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon +e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ 
\widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right] ^{2}  \notag \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}  \notag \\
&\leq &\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}  \notag \\
&&+\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}  \notag \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times \dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert
J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert e_{\left( i,h\right)
}^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}%
\right] \left[ \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] ^{\prime }X^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,h\right) }  \notag \\
&\leq &\mathcal{A}_{5,1}+\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta
_{0}\right\Vert _{2}^{2}\mathcal{A}_{5,2}\text{,}  \label{A5 bd}
\end{eqnarray}%
where $\mathcal{A}_{5,1}$ and $\mathcal{A}_{5,2}$ are as defined in parts
(a) and (b) above. In light of the upper bound given by (\ref{A5 bd}), it
then follows from expressions (\ref{A51}) and (\ref{A52}) that%
\begin{equation}
\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{5}\right\vert \leq \mathcal{A}_{5,1}+\left\Vert 
\widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}^{2}\mathcal{A}%
_{5,2}=O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) +o_{p}\left( 1\right) O_{p}\left(
1\right) =o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{. }\square  \label{A5}
\end{equation}

\bigskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma OA-19: }Let Assumptions 1-6 be satisfied, and let $%
\left\{ \widehat{\delta }_{n}\right\} $ be a sequence of estimators such that%
\begin{equation*}
\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}\overset{p}{%
\rightarrow }0\text{ as }n\rightarrow \infty \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
as long as $\sqrt{K_{2,n}}/\left( \mu _{n}^{\min }\right) ^{2}\rightarrow 0$%
. Then, the following statements are true.

\begin{enumerate}
\item[(a)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{6,1}=O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) =o_{p}\left( 1\right) 
\text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray}
\mathcal{A}_{6,1} &=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\right\vert \left[ e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon +e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left( 
\widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right) \right] ^{2}\right.  \notag \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \times
\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\right\vert \left[ e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon +e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ 
\widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right] ^{2}\right\}  \notag
\end{eqnarray}

\item[(b)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{6,2}=O_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{6,2} &=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right)
}\right\vert \left[ e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon +e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left( 
\widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right) \right] ^{2}\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 
}\left. \times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right)
,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\right\}
\end{eqnarray*}

\item[(c)] 
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{6}=o_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{6} &=&-\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\left\{
\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\left(
e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon +e_{\left(
i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{\delta }%
_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right) ^{2}\right. \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\left. \times
\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\left(
e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon +e_{\left(
j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{\delta }%
_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right) \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \right\}
\end{eqnarray*}
\end{enumerate}

\bigskip

\noindent \textbf{Proof of Lemma OA-19:}

To show part (a), note that$\mathcal{A}_{6,1}$ has the same form as the term
which we used to get an initial bound on $\mathcal{A}_{3}$. See, in
particular, the first inequality in expression (\ref{A3 bd}). Hence, it
follows from expression (\ref{A3}) that%
\begin{eqnarray}
&&\mathcal{A}_{6,1}  \notag \\
&=&\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \left[ e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon +e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left( 
\widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right) \right] ^{2}  \notag \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\right\vert \left[ e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon +e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ 
\widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right] ^{2}  \notag \\
&\leq &\mathcal{A}_{3,1}+\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta
_{0}\right\Vert _{2}^{2}\mathcal{A}_{3,2}+\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }%
_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}^{2}\mathcal{A}_{3,3}+\left\Vert \widehat{%
\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}^{4}\mathcal{A}_{3,4}  \notag \\
&=&o_{p}\left( 1\right) .  \label{A61}
\end{eqnarray}

Next, for part (b), note that we can apply the inequality $\left\vert
\dsum\nolimits_{i=1}^{m}a_{i}\right\vert ^{r}\leq
m^{r-1}\dsum\nolimits_{i=1}^{m}\left\vert a_{i}\right\vert ^{r}$ to obtain%
\begin{eqnarray*}
0 &\leq &\mathcal{A}_{6,2} \\
&\leq &\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&+\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }\times e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left( \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right)
\left( \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right) ^{\prime }X^{\prime
}M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,h\right) } \\
&\leq &\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&+\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}^{2}\frac{2}{%
K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right)
^{2} \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ }\times e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}XX^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,h\right) } \\
&=&\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2} \\
&&+\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}^{2}\frac{2}{%
K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ %
\left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right)
,\left( j,s\right) }^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left(
i,t\right) ,\left( i,h\right) }\right\vert
\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right)
}\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right)
^{2} \\
&&\text{ \ \ \ }\times e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right)
}UU^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,h\right) } \\
&=&\mathcal{A}_{6,2,1}+\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta
_{0}\right\Vert _{2}^{2}\mathcal{A}_{6,2,2}\text{,}
\end{eqnarray*}%
where%
\begin{eqnarray*}
\mathcal{A}_{6,2,1} &=&\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left(
j,s\right) ,\left( j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right)
}^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}\text{,} \\
\mathcal{A}_{6,2,2} &=&\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left(
i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left(
j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }UU^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }e_{\left( i,h\right) }\text{.}
\end{eqnarray*}%
Note that $\mathcal{A}_{6,2,1}$ is of the same form as $\mathcal{A}_{2,2,1}$
and $\mathcal{A}_{6,2,2}$ is of the same form as $\mathcal{A}_{2,2,2}$, so
that from expressions (\ref{A221}) and (\ref{A222}), we get%
\begin{equation*}
\mathcal{A}_{6,2,1}=O_{p}\left( \frac{K_{n}}{n}\right) =o_{p}\left( 1\right) 
\text{, }\mathcal{A}_{6,2,2}=O_{p}\left( 1\right) \text{,}
\end{equation*}%
from which it follows that 
\begin{equation}
0\leq \mathcal{A}_{6,2}\leq \mathcal{A}_{6,2,1}+\left\Vert \widehat{\delta }%
_{n}-\delta _{0}\right\Vert _{2}^{2}\mathcal{A}_{6,2,2}=O_{p}\left( \frac{%
K_{n}}{n}\right) +o_{p}\left( 1\right) O_{p}\left( 1\right) =o_{p}\left(
1\right) \text{.}  \label{A62}
\end{equation}

Finally, to show part (c), note that, by applying the triangle inequality
and the inequality $\left\vert XY\right\vert \leq \left( 1/2\right)
X^{2}+\left( 1/2\right) Y^{2}$ in this case, we obtain%
\begin{eqnarray}
\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{6}\right\vert &\leq &\frac{2}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits 
_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right)
\neq \left( j,s\right) }}^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \left[ e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon +e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left( 
\widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right) \right] ^{2}  \notag \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\right\vert \left\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}P^{Z^{\perp }}\varepsilon +e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left(
Z,Q\right) }X\left[ \widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right) \left(
e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) \right\vert  \notag
\\
&\leq &\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \left[ e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon +e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left( 
\widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right) \right] ^{2}  \notag \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\right\vert \left[ e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon +e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left[ 
\widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right] \right] ^{2}  \notag \\
&&+\frac{1}{K_{2,n}}\dsum\limits_{\substack{ \left( i,t\right) ,\left(
j,s\right) =1  \\ \left( i,t\right) \neq \left( j,s\right) }}%
^{m_{n}}A_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left( j,s\right)
}^{2}\dsum\limits_{h=1}^{T_{i}}\left\vert J_{\left( i,t\right) ,\left(
i,h\right) }\right\vert \left[ e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z^{\perp
}}\varepsilon +e_{\left( i,h\right) }^{\prime }M^{\left( Z,Q\right) }X\left( 
\widehat{\delta }_{n}-\delta _{0}\right) \right] ^{2}  \notag \\
&&\times \dsum\limits_{v=1}^{T_{j}}\left\vert J_{\left( j,s\right) ,\left(
j,v\right) }\right\vert \left( e_{\left( j,v\right) }^{\prime
}M^{Q}\varepsilon \right) ^{2}  \notag \\
&=&\mathcal{A}_{6,1}+\mathcal{A}_{6,2}\text{,}  \label{A6 bd}
\end{eqnarray}%
where $\mathcal{A}_{6,1}$ and $\mathcal{A}_{6,2}$ are as defined in parts
(a) and (b) above. In light of the upper bound for $\left\vert \mathcal{A}%
_{6}\right\vert $ given in (\ref{A6 bd}), it then follows from expressions (%
\ref{A61}) and (\ref{A62}) that 
\begin{equation}
\left\vert \mathcal{A}_{6}\right\vert \leq \mathcal{A}_{6,1}+\mathcal{A}%
_{6,2}=o_{p}\left( 1\right) +o_{p}\left( 1\right) =o_{p}\left( 1\right) 
\text{. }\square  \label{A6}
\end{equation}

\medskip

The next lemma provides more primitive sufficient conditions for part (iv)
of Asssumpton 5 in the main paper. To facilitate the statement and proof of
this lemma, we introduce a number of additional notations. Let $Z_{1,\cdot
,k}$ and $Z_{1,\left( i,t\right) ,k}$ denote, respectively, the $k^{th}$
column and the $\left( \left( i,t\right) ,k\right) ^{th}$ element of of $%
Z_{1}$ for $\left( i,t\right) =1,...,m_{n}$ and $k=1,...,K_{1,n}$.
Similarly, let $Z_{2,\cdot ,k}$ and $Z_{2,\left( i,t\right) ,k}$ denote,
respectively, the $k^{th}$ column and the $\left( \left( i,t\right)
,k\right) ^{th}$ element of of $Z_{2}$ for $\left( i,t\right) =1,...,m_{n}$
and $k=1,...,K_{2,n}$. Finally, let $\widetilde{Z}_{2,\left( i,t\right)
,k}=e_{\left( i,t\right) }^{\prime }P^{Z_{1}^{\perp }}Z_{2,\cdot ,k}$, where 
$P^{Z_{1}^{\perp }}=M^{Q}Z_{1}\left( Z_{1}^{\prime }M^{Q}Z_{1}\right)
^{-1}Z_{1}^{\prime }M^{Q}$.

\medskip

\noindent \textbf{Lemma OA-20: }

\begin{enumerate}
\item[(a)] Assume the following conditions hold:

\begin{enumerate}
\item[(a1)] There exists a positive constant $C$ such that%
\begin{equation*}
